{SDhPS, 1}
evaṃ mayā śrutam | [SDhPS, 1 1.1]
ekasmin samaye bhagavān rājagṛhe viharati sma gṛdhrakūṭe parvate mahatā bhikṣusaṃghena sārdhaṃ dvādaśabhirbhikṣuśataiḥ sarvairarhadbhiḥ kṣīṇāsravairniḥkleśairvaśībhūtaiḥ suvimuktacittaiḥ suvimuktaprajñair ājāneyair mahānāgaiḥ kṛtakṛtyaiḥ kṛtakaraṇīyairapahṛtabhārairanuprāptasvakārthaiḥ parikṣīṇabhavasaṃyojanaiḥ samyagājñāsuvimuktacittaiḥ sarvacetovaśitāparamapāramitāprāptair abhijñātābhijñātair mahāśrāvakaiḥ | [SDhPS, 1 2.1]
tadyathā āyuṣmatā ca ājñātakauṇḍinyena āyuṣmatā ca aśvajitā āyuṣmatā ca bāṣpeṇa āyuṣmatā ca mahānāmnā āyuṣmatā ca bhadrikeṇa āyuṣmatā ca mahākāśyapena āyuṣmatā ca urubilvakāśyapena āyuṣmatā ca nadīkāśyapena āyuṣmatā ca gayākāśyapena āyuṣmatā ca śāriputreṇa āyuṣmatā ca mahāmaudgalyāyanena āyuṣmatā ca mahākātyāyanena āyuṣmatā ca aniruddhena āyuṣmatā ca revatena āyuṣmatā ca kapphinena āyuṣmatā ca gavāṃpatinā āyuṣmatā ca pilindavatsena āyuṣmatā ca bakkulena āyuṣmatā ca mahākauṣṭhilena āyuṣmatā ca bharadvājena āyuṣmatā ca mahānandena āyuṣmatā ca upanandena āyuṣmatā ca sundaranandena āyuṣmatā ca pūrṇamaitrāyaṇīputreṇa āyuṣmatā ca subhūtinā āyuṣmatā ca rāhulena | [SDhPS, 1 2.2]
ebhiścānyaiśca mahāśrāvakaiḥ āyuṣmatā ca ānandena śaikṣeṇa | [SDhPS, 1 2.3]
anyābhyāṃ ca dvābhyāṃ bhikṣusahasrābhyāṃ śaikṣāśaikṣābhyām | [SDhPS, 1 2.4]
mahāprajāpatīpramukhaiśca ṣaḍbhirbhikṣuṇīsahasraiḥ | [SDhPS, 1 2.5]
yaśodharayā ca bhikṣuṇyā rāhulamātrā saparivārayā | [SDhPS, 1 2.6]
aśītyā ca bodhisattvasahasraiḥ sārdhaṃ sarvair avaivartikair ekajātipratibaddhair yad uta anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau dhāraṇīpratilabdhairmahāpratibhānapratiṣṭhitair avaivartyadharmacakrapravartakair bahubuddhaśataparyupāsitair bahubuddhaśatasahasrāvaropitakuśalamūlair buddhaśatasahasrasaṃstutair maitrīparibhāvitakāyacittais tathāgatajñānāvatāraṇakuśalair mahāprajñaiḥ prajñāpāramitāgatiṃgatair bahulokadhātuśatasahasraviśrutair bahuprāṇikoṭīnayutaśatasahasrasaṃtārakaiḥ | [SDhPS, 1 2.7]
tad yathā mañjuśriyā ca kumārabhūtena bodhisattvena mahāsattvena avalokiteśvareṇa ca mahāsthāmaprāptena ca sarvārthanāmnā ca nityodyuktena ca anikṣiptadhureṇa ca ratnapāṇinā ca bhaiṣajyarājena ca bhaiṣajyasamudgatena ca vyūharājena ca pradānaśūreṇa ca ratnacandreṇa ca ratnaprabheṇa ca pūrṇacandreṇa ca mahāvikrāmiṇā ca anantavikrāmiṇā ca trailokyavikrāmiṇā ca mahāpratibhānena ca satatasamitābhiyuktena ca dharaṇīdhareṇa ca akṣayamatinā ca padmaśriyā ca nakṣatrarājena ca maitreyeṇa ca bodhisattvena mahāsattvena siṃhena ca bodhisattvena mahāsattvena | [SDhPS, 1 2.8]
bhadrapālapūrvaṃgamaiśca ṣoḍaśabhiḥ satpuruṣaiḥ sārdham | [SDhPS, 1 2.9]
tadyathā bhadrapālena ca ratnākareṇa ca susārthavāhena ca naradattena ca guhyaguptena ca varuṇadattena ca indradattena ca uttaramatinā ca viśeṣamatinā ca vardhamānamatinā ca amoghadarśinā ca susaṃprasthitena ca suvikrāntavikrāmiṇā ca anupamamatinā ca sūryagarbheṇa ca dharaṇīṃdhareṇa ca | [SDhPS, 1 2.10]
evaṃpramukhairaśītyā ca bodhisattvasahasraiḥ sārdham | [SDhPS, 1 2.11]
śakreṇa ca devānāmindreṇa sārdhaṃ viṃśatidevaputrasahasraparivāreṇa | [SDhPS, 1 2.12]
tadyathā candreṇa ca devaputreṇa sūryeṇa ca devaputreṇa samantagandhena ca devaputreṇa ratnaprabheṇa ca devaputreṇa avabhāsaprabheṇa ca devaputreṇa | [SDhPS, 1 2.13]
evaṃpramukhairviṃśatyā ca devaputrasahasraiḥ | [SDhPS, 1 2.14]
caturbhiśca mahārājaiḥ sārdhaṃ triṃśaddevaputrasahasraparivāraiḥ | [SDhPS, 1 2.15]
tadyathā virūḍhakena ca mahārājena virūpākṣeṇa ca mahārājena dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa ca mahārājena vaiśravaṇena ca mahārājena | [SDhPS, 1 2.16]
īśvareṇa ca devaputreṇa ca maheśvareṇa ca devaputreṇa triṃśaddevaputrasahasraparivārābhyām | [SDhPS, 1 2.17]
brahmaṇā ca sahāṃpatinā sārdhaṃ dvādaśabrahmakāyikadevaputrasahasraparivāreṇa | [SDhPS, 1 2.18]
tadyathā śikhinā ca brahmaṇā jyotiṣprabheṇa ca brahmaṇā | [SDhPS, 1 2.19]
evaṃpramukhairdvādaśabhiśca brahmakāyikadevaputrasahasraiḥ | [SDhPS, 1 2.20]
aṣṭābhiśca nāgarājaiḥ sārdhaṃ bahunāgakoṭīśatasahasraparivāraiḥ | [SDhPS, 1 2.21]
tadyathā nandena ca nāgarājena upanandena ca nāgarājena sāgareṇa ca vāsukinā ca takṣakeṇa ca manasvinā ca anavataptena ca utpalakena ca nāgarājena | [SDhPS, 1 2.22]
caturbhiśca kinnararājaiḥ sārdhaṃ bahukinnarakoṭīśatasahasraparivāraiḥ | [SDhPS, 1 2.23]
tadyathā drumeṇa ca kinnararājena mahādharmeṇa ca kinnararājena sudharmeṇa ca kinnararājena dharmadhareṇa ca kinnararājena | [SDhPS, 1 2.24]
caturbhiśca gandharvakāyikadevaputraiḥ sārdhaṃ bahugandharvaśatasahasraparivāraiḥ | [SDhPS, 1 3.1]
tadyathā manojñena ca gandharveṇa manojñasvareṇa ca madhureṇa ca madhurasvareṇa ca gandharveṇa | [SDhPS, 1 4.1]
caturbhiścāsurendraiḥ sārdhaṃ bahvasurakoṭīśatasahasraparivāraiḥ | [SDhPS, 1 5.1]
tadyathā balinā ca asurendreṇa kharaskandhena ca asurendreṇa vemacitriṇā ca asurendreṇa rāhuṇā ca asurendreṇa | [SDhPS, 1 6.1]
caturbhiśca garuḍendraiḥ sārdhaṃ bahugaruḍakoṭīśatasahasraparivāraiḥ | [SDhPS, 1 7.1]
tadyathā mahātejasā ca garuḍendreṇa mahākāyena ca mahāpūrṇena ca maharddhiprāptena ca garuḍendreṇa | [SDhPS, 1 8.1]
rājñā ca ajātaśatruṇā māgadhena vaidehīputreṇa sārdham | [SDhPS, 1 9.1]
tena khalu punaḥ samayena bhagavāṃścatasṛbhiḥ parṣadbhiḥ parivṛtaḥ puraskṛtaḥ satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito 'rcito 'pacāyito mahānirdeśaṃ nāma dharmaparyāyaṃ sūtrāntaṃ mahāvaipulyaṃ bodhisattvāvavādaṃ sarvabuddhaparigrahaṃ bhāṣitvā tasminneva mahādharmāsane paryaṅkamābhujya anantanirdeśapratiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpanno 'bhūd aniñjamānena kāyena sthito 'niñjaprāptena ca cittena | [SDhPS, 1 10.1]
samanantarasamāpannasya khalu punarbhagavato māndāravamahāmāndāravāṇāṃ mañjūṣakamahāmañjūṣakāṇāṃ divyānāṃ puṣpāṇāṃ mahatpuṣpavarṣamabhiprāvarṣat bhagavantaṃ tāśca catasraḥ parṣado 'bhyavākiran | [SDhPS, 1 11.1]
sarvāvacca buddhakṣetraṃ ṣaḍvikāraṃ prakampitamabhūccalitaṃ saṃpracalitaṃ vedhitaṃ saṃpravedhitaṃ kṣubhitaṃ samprakṣubhitam | [SDhPS, 1 12.1]
tena khalu punaḥ samayena tasyāṃ parṣadi bhikṣubhikṣuṇyupāsakopāsikā devanāgayakṣagandharvāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragamanuṣyāmanuṣyāḥ saṃnipatitā abhūvan saṃniṣaṇṇāḥ rājānaśca maṇḍalino balacakravartinaś caturdvīpakacakravartinaśca | [SDhPS, 1 13.1]
te sarve saparivārā bhagavantaṃ vyavalokayanti sma āścaryaprāptā adbhutaprāptā audbilyaprāptāḥ | [SDhPS, 1 14.1]
atha khalu tasyāṃ velāyāṃ bhagavato bhrūvivarāntarād ūrṇākośād ekā raśmirniścaritā | [SDhPS, 1 15.1]
sā pūrvasyāṃ diśi aṣṭādaśabuddhakṣetrasahasrāṇi prasṛtā | [SDhPS, 1 16.1]
tāni ca sarvāṇi buddhakṣetrāṇi tasyā raśmeḥ prabhayā suparisphuṭāni saṃdṛśyante sma yāvadavīcirmahānirayo yāvacca bhavāgram | [SDhPS, 1 17.1]
ye ca teṣu buddhakṣetreṣu ṣaṭsu gatiṣu sattvāḥ saṃvidyante sma te sarve 'śeṣeṇa saṃdṛśyante sma | [SDhPS, 1 18.1]
ye ca teṣu buddhakṣetreṣu buddhā bhagavantastiṣṭhanti dhriyante yāpayanti ca te 'pi sarve saṃdṛśyante sma | [SDhPS, 1 19.1]
yaṃ ca te buddhā bhagavanto dharmaṃ deśayanti sa ca sarvo nikhilena śrūyate sma | [SDhPS, 1 20.1]
ye ca teṣu buddhakṣetreṣu bhikṣubhikṣuṇyupāsakopāsikā yogino yogācārāḥ prāptaphalāś cāprāptaphalāś ca te 'pi sarve saṃdṛśyante sma | [SDhPS, 1 21.1]
ye ca teṣu buddhakṣetreṣu bodhisattvā mahāsattvā anekavividhaśravaṇārambaṇādhimuktihetukāraṇair upāyakauśalyair bodhisattvacaryāṃ caranti te 'pi sarve saṃdṛśyante sma | [SDhPS, 1 22.1]
ye ca teṣu buddhakṣetreṣu buddhā bhagavantaḥ parinirvṛtāḥ te 'pi sarve saṃdṛśyante sma | [SDhPS, 1 23.1]
ye ca teṣu buddhakṣetreṣu parinirvṛtānāṃ buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ dhātustūpā ratnamayāḥ te 'pi sarve saṃdṛśyante sma | [SDhPS, 1 24.1]
atha khalu maitreyasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasyaitad abhūn mahānimittaṃ prātihāryaṃ batedaṃ tathāgatena kṛtam | [SDhPS, 1 25.1]
ko nvatra heturbhaviṣyati kiṃ kāraṇaṃ yadbhagavatā idamevaṃrūpaṃ mahānimittaṃ prātihāryaṃ kṛtaṃ bhagavāṃśca samādhiṃ samāpannaḥ | [SDhPS, 1 26.1]
imāni caivaṃrūpāṇi mahāścaryādbhutācintyāni maharddhiprātihāryāṇi saṃdṛśyante sma | [SDhPS, 1 27.1]
kiṃ nu khalvahametamarthaṃ paripraṣṭavyaṃ paripṛccheyaṃ ko nvatra samarthaḥ syādetamarthaṃ visarjayitum | [SDhPS, 1 28.1]
tasyaitadabhūd ayaṃ mañjuśrīḥ kumārabhūtaḥ pūrvajinakṛtādhikāro 'varopitakuśalamūlo bahubuddhaparyupāsitaḥ | [SDhPS, 1 28.2]
dṛṣṭapūrvāṇi ca anena mañjuśriyā kumārabhūtena pūrvakāṇāṃ tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāmevaṃrūpāṇi nimittāni bhaviṣyanty anubhūtapūrvāṇi ca mahādharmasāṃkathyāni | [SDhPS, 1 29.1]
yannvahaṃ mañjuśriyaṃ kumārabhūtametamarthaṃ paripṛccheyam | [SDhPS, 1 30.1]
tāsāṃ catasṛṇāṃ parṣadāṃ bhikṣubhikṣuṇyupāsakopāsikānāṃ bahūnāṃ ca devanāgayakṣagandharvāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragamanuṣyāmanuṣyāṇām imamevaṃrūpaṃ bhagavato mahānimittaṃ prātihāryāvabhāsaṃ dṛṣṭvā āścaryaprāptānām adbhutaprāptānāṃ kautūhalaprāptānām etadabhavat kiṃ nu khalu vayamimamevaṃrūpaṃ bhagavato maharddhiprātihāryāvabhāsaṃ kṛtaṃ paripṛcchema | [SDhPS, 1 31.1]
atha khalu maitreyo bodhisattvo mahāsattvastasminneva kṣaṇalavamuhūrte tāsāṃ catasṛṇāṃ parṣadāṃ cetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya ātmanā ca dharmasaṃśayaprāptastasyāṃ velāyāṃ mañjuśriyaṃ kumārabhūtametadavocat | [SDhPS, 1 32.1]
ko nvatra mañjuśrīrhetuḥ kaḥ pratyayo yadayamevaṃrūpa āścaryādbhuto bhagavatā ṛddhyavabhāsaḥ kṛtaḥ imāni cāṣṭādaśabuddhakṣetrasahasrāṇi vicitrāṇi darśanīyāni paramadarśanīyāni tathāgatapūrvaṃgamāni tathāgatapariṇāyakāni saṃdṛśyante | [SDhPS, 1 32.2]
atha khalu maitreyo bodhisattvo mahāsattvo mañjuśriyaṃ kumārabhūtam ābhirgāthābhiradhyabhāṣata | [SDhPS, 1 33.1]
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ mañjuśirī iyaṃ hi raśmiḥ pramuktā naranāyakena | [SDhPS, 1 34.1]
prabhāsayantī bhramukāntarātu ūrṇāya kośād iyamekaraśmiḥ | [SDhPS, 1 34.2]
māndāravāṇāṃ ca mahanta varṣaṃ puṣpāṇi muñcanti surāḥ suhṛṣṭāḥ | [SDhPS, 1 35.1]
mañjūṣakāṃścandanacūrṇamiśrān divyān sugandhāṃśca manoramāṃśca | [SDhPS, 1 35.2]
yehī mahī śobhatiyaṃ samantāt parṣāśca catvāra sulabdhaharṣāḥ | [SDhPS, 1 36.1]
sarvaṃ ca kṣetraṃ imu samprakampitaṃ ṣaḍbhirvikārehi subhīṣmarūpam | [SDhPS, 1 36.2]
sā caiva raśmī purimādiśāya aṣṭādaśakṣetrasahasra pūrṇāḥ | [SDhPS, 1 37.1]
avabhāsayī ekakṣaṇena sarve suvarṇavarṇā iva bhonti kṣetrāḥ | [SDhPS, 1 37.2]
yāvānavīcī paramaṃ bhavāgraṃ kṣetreṣu yāvanti ca teṣu sattvāḥ | [SDhPS, 1 38.1]
ṣaṭsū gatīṣū tahi vidyamānā cyavanti ye cāpyupapadyi tatra | [SDhPS, 1 38.2]
karmāṇi citrā vividhāni teṣāṃ gatīṣu dṛśyanti sukhā dukhā ca | [SDhPS, 1 39.1]
hīnā praṇītā tatha madhyamā ca iha sthito addaśi sarvametat | [SDhPS, 1 39.2]
buddhāṃśca paśyāmi narendrasiṃhān prakāśayanto vivaranti dharmam | [SDhPS, 1 40.1]
praśāsamānān bahusattvakoṭīḥ udāharanto madhurasvarāṃ giram | [SDhPS, 1 40.2]
atha khalu mañjuśrīḥ kumārabhūto maitreyaṃ bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvaṃ taṃ ca sarvāvantaṃ bodhisattvagaṇamāmantrayate sma mahādharmaśravaṇasāṃkathyamidaṃ kulaputrāstathāgatasya kartumabhiprāyaḥ | [SDhPS, 1 90.1]
mahādharmavṛṣṭyabhipravarṣaṇaṃ ca mahādharmadundubhisaṃpravādanaṃ ca mahādharmadhvajasamucchrayaṇaṃ ca mahādharmolkāsaṃprajvālanaṃ ca mahādharmaśaṅkhābhiprapūraṇaṃ ca mahādharmabherīparāhaṇanaṃ ca mahādharmanirdeśaṃ ca adya kulaputrāstathāgatasya kartumabhiprāyaḥ | [SDhPS, 1 90.2]
yathā mama kulaputrāḥ pratibhāti yathā ca mayā pūrvakāṇāṃ tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāmidamevaṃrūpaṃ pūrvanimittaṃ dṛṣṭamabhūt teṣāmapi pūrvakāṇāṃ tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāmevaṃ raśmipramocanāvabhāso 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 1 91.1]
tenaivaṃ prajānāmi mahādharmaśravaṇasāṃkathyaṃ tathāgataḥ kartukāmo mahādharmaśravaṇaṃ śrāvayitukāmaḥ yathedamevaṃrūpaṃ pūrvanimittaṃ prāduṣkṛtavān | [SDhPS, 1 92.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 1 93.1]
sarvalokavipratyanīyakadharmaparyāyaṃ śrāvayitukāmastathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ yathedamevaṃrūpaṃ mahāprātihāryaṃ raśmipramocanāvabhāsaṃ ca pūrvanimittamupadarśayati | [SDhPS, 1 93.2]
anusmarāmyahaṃ kulaputrā atīte 'dhvani asaṃkhyeyaiḥ kalpairasaṃkhyeyatarair vipulairaprameyairacintyair aparimitairapramāṇaistataḥpareṇa parataraṃ yadāsīt tena kālena tena samayena candrasūryapradīpo nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loka udapādi vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān | [SDhPS, 1 94.1]
sa dharmaṃ deśayati sma ādau kalyāṇaṃ madhye kalyāṇaṃ paryavasāne kalyāṇam | [SDhPS, 1 95.1]
svarthaṃ suvyañjanaṃ kevalaṃ paripūrṇaṃ pariśuddhaṃ paryavadātaṃ brahmacaryaṃ saṃprakāśayati sma | [SDhPS, 1 96.1]
yaduta śrāvakāṇāṃ caturāryasatyasamprayuktaṃ pratītyasamutpādapravṛttaṃ dharmaṃ deśayati sma jātijarāvyādhimaraṇaśokaparidevaduḥkhadaurmanasyopāyāsānāṃ samatikramāya nirvāṇaparyavasānam | [SDhPS, 1 97.1]
bodhisattvānāṃ ca mahāsattvānāṃ ca ṣaṭpāramitāpratisaṃyuktamanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimārabhya sarvajñajñānaparyavasānaṃ dharmaṃ deśayati sma | [SDhPS, 1 98.1]
tasya khalu punaḥ kulaputrāḥ candrasūryapradīpasya tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasya pareṇa parataraṃ candrasūryapradīpa eva nāmnā tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loka udapādi | [SDhPS, 1 99.1]
iti hi ajita etena paraṃparodāhāreṇa candrasūryapradīpanāmakānāṃ tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānām ekanāmadheyānām ekakulagotrāṇāṃ yad idaṃ bharadvājasagotrāṇāṃ viṃśatitathāgatasahasrāṇyabhūvan | [SDhPS, 1 100.1]
tatra ajita teṣāṃ viṃśatitathāgatasahasrāṇāṃ pūrvakaṃ tathāgatamupādāya yāvat paścimakastathāgataḥ so 'pi candrasūryapradīpanāmadheya eva tathāgato 'bhūdarhan samyaksaṃbuddho vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān | [SDhPS, 1 101.1]
so 'pi dharmaṃ deśitavān ādau kalyāṇaṃ madhye kalyāṇaṃ paryavasāne kalyāṇam | [SDhPS, 1 102.1]
svarthaṃ suvyañjanaṃ kevalaṃ paripūrṇaṃ pariśuddhaṃ paryavadātaṃ brahmacaryaṃ saṃprakāśitavān | [SDhPS, 1 103.1]
yaduta śrāvakāṇāṃ caturāryasatyasaṃyuktaṃ pratītyasamutpādapravṛttaṃ dharmaṃ deśitavān jātijarāvyādhimaraṇaśokaparidevaduḥkhadaurmanasyopāyāsānāṃ samatikramāya nirvāṇaparyavasānam | [SDhPS, 1 104.1]
bodhisattvānāṃ ca mahāsattvānāṃ ca ṣaṭpāramitāpratisaṃyuktamanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimārabhya sarvajñajñānaparyavasānaṃ dharmaṃ deśitavān | [SDhPS, 1 105.1]
tasya khalu punarajita bhagavataścandrasūryapradīpasya tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasya pūrvaṃ kumārabhūtasyānabhiniṣkrāntagṛhāvāsasya aṣṭau putrā abhūvan | [SDhPS, 1 106.1]
tadyathā matiśca nāma rājakumāro 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 1 107.1]
sumatiśca nāma rājakumāro 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 1 108.1]
anantamatiśca nāma ratnamatiśca nāma viśeṣamatiśca nāma vimatisamudghāṭī ca nāma ghoṣamatiśca nāma dharmamatiśca nāma rājakumāro 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 1 109.1]
teṣāṃ khalu punarajita aṣṭānāṃ rājakumārāṇāṃ tasya bhagavataścandrasūryapradīpasya tathāgatasya putrāṇāṃ vipularddhirabhūt | [SDhPS, 1 110.1]
ekaikasya catvāro mahādvīpāḥ paribhogo 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 1 111.1]
teṣveva ca rājyaṃ kārayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 1 112.1]
te taṃ bhagavantam abhiniṣkrāntagṛhāvāsaṃ viditvā anuttarāṃ ca samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddhaṃ śrutvā sarvarājyaparibhogānutsṛjya taṃ bhagavantamanu pravrajitāḥ | [SDhPS, 1 113.1]
sarve ca anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃprasthitā dharmabhāṇakāścābhuvan | [SDhPS, 1 114.1]
sadā ca brahmacāriṇo bahubuddhaśatasahasrāvaropitakuśalamūlāśca te rājakumārā abhuvan | [SDhPS, 1 115.1]
tena khalu punarajita samayena sa bhagavāṃścandrasūryapradīpastathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho mahānirdeśaṃ nāma dharmaparyāyaṃ sūtrāntaṃ mahāvaipulyaṃ bodhisattvāvavādaṃ sarvabuddhaparigrahaṃ bhāṣitvā tasminneva kṣaṇalavamuhūrte tasminneva parṣatsaṃnipāte tasminneva mahādharmāsane paryaṅkamābhujya anantanirdeśapratiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpanno 'bhūd aniñjamānena kāyena sthitena aniñjamānena cittena | [SDhPS, 1 116.1]
samanantarasamāpannasya khalu punastasya bhagavato māndāravamahāmāndāravāṇāṃ mañjūṣakamahāmañjūṣakāṇāṃ ca divyānāṃ puṣpāṇāṃ mahatpuṣpavarṣamabhiprāvarṣat | [SDhPS, 1 117.1]
taṃ bhagavantaṃ saparṣadamabhyavākirat sarvāvacca tad buddhakṣetraṃ ṣaḍvikāraṃ prakampitamabhūt calitaṃ saṃpracalitaṃ vedhitaṃ saṃpravedhitaṃ kṣubhitaṃ samprakṣubhitam | [SDhPS, 1 118.1]
tena khalu punarajita samayena tena kālena ye tasyāṃ parṣadi bhikṣubhikṣuṇyupāsakopāsikā devanāgayakṣagandharvāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragamanuṣyāmanuṣyāḥ saṃnipatitā abhūvan saṃniṣaṇṇāḥ rājānaśca maṇḍalino balacakravartinaścaturdvīpakacakravartinaśca te sarve saparivārāstaṃ bhagavantaṃ vyavalokayanti sma āścaryaprāptā adbhutaprāptā audbilyaprāptāḥ | [SDhPS, 1 119.1]
atha khalu tasyāṃ velāyāṃ tasya bhagavataścandrasūryapradīpasya tathāgatasya bhrūvivarāntarādūrṇākośādekā raśmirniścaritā | [SDhPS, 1 120.1]
sā pūrvasyāṃ diśi aṣṭādaśabuddhakṣetrasahasrāṇi prasṛtā | [SDhPS, 1 121.1]
tāni ca buddhakṣetrāṇi sarvāṇi tasyā raśmeḥ prabhayā suparisphuṭāni saṃdṛśyante sma tadyathāpi nāma ajita etarhyetāni buddhakṣetrāṇi saṃdṛśyante | [SDhPS, 1 122.1]
tena khalu punarajita samayena tasya bhagavato viṃśatibodhisattvakoṭyaḥ samanubaddhā abhuvan | [SDhPS, 1 123.1]
ye tasyāṃ parṣadi dharmaśravaṇikāḥ te āścaryaprāptā abhūvan adbhutaprāptā audbilyaprāptāḥ kautūhalasamutpannā etena mahāraśmyavabhāsenāvabhāsitaṃ lokaṃ dṛṣṭvā | [SDhPS, 1 124.1]
tena khalu punarajita samayena tasya bhagavataḥ śāsane varaprabho nāma bodhisattvo 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 1 125.1]
tasyāṣṭau śatānyantevāsināmabhūvan | [SDhPS, 1 126.1]
sa ca bhagavāṃstataḥ samādhervyutthāya taṃ varaprabhaṃ bodhisattvamārabhya saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ nāma dharmaparyāyaṃ saṃprakāśayāmāsa | [SDhPS, 1 127.1]
yāvat paripūrṇān ṣaṣṭyantarakalpān bhāṣitavān ekāsane niṣaṇṇo 'saṃpravedhamānena kāyena aniñjamānena cittena | [SDhPS, 1 128.1]
sā ca sarvāvatī parṣadekāsane niṣaṇṇā tān ṣaṣṭyantarakalpāṃstasya bhagavato 'ntikāddharmaṃ śṛṇoti sma | [SDhPS, 1 129.1]
na ca tasyāṃ parṣadi ekasattvasyāpi kāyaklamatho 'bhūt na ca cittaklamathaḥ | [SDhPS, 1 130.1]
atha sa bhagavāṃścandrasūryapradīpastathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ ṣaṣṭyantarakalpānāmatyayāt taṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ sūtrāntaṃ mahāvaipulyaṃ bodhisattvāvavādaṃ sarvabuddhaparigrahaṃ nirdiśya tasminneva kṣaṇalavamuhūrte parinirvāṇam ārocitavān sadevakasya lokasya samārakasya sabrahmakasya saśramaṇabrāhmaṇikāyāḥ prajāyāḥ sadevamānuṣāsurāyāḥ purastāt | [SDhPS, 1 131.1]
adya bhikṣavo 'syāmeva rātryāṃ madhyame yāme tathāgato 'nupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau parinirvāsyatīti | [SDhPS, 1 131.2]
atha khalvajita sa bhagavāṃścandrasūryapradīpastathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ śrīgarbhaṃ nāma bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvamanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau vyākṛtya tāṃ sarvāvatīṃ parṣadamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 1 132.1]
ayaṃ bhikṣavaḥ śrīgarbho bodhisattvo mamānantaramanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbhotsyate | [SDhPS, 1 132.2]
vimalanetro nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 1 133.1]
atha khalvajita sa bhagavāṃścandrasūryapradīpastathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhastasyāmeva rātryāṃ madhyame yāme 'nupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau parinirvṛtaḥ | [SDhPS, 1 134.1]
taṃ ca saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ sa varaprabho bodhisattvo mahāsattvo dhāritavān | [SDhPS, 1 135.1]
aśītiṃ cāntarakalpāṃstasya bhagavataḥ parinirvṛtasya śāsanaṃ sa varaprabho bodhisattvo mahāsattvo dhāritavān saṃprakāśitavān | [SDhPS, 1 136.1]
tatra ajita ye tasya bhagavato 'ṣṭau putrā abhūvan matipramukhāḥ te tasyaiva varaprabhasya bodhisattvasyāntevāsino 'bhūvan | [SDhPS, 1 137.1]
te tenaiva paripācitā abhūvannanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 1 138.1]
taiśca tataḥ paścādbahūni buddhakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi dṛṣṭāni satkṛtāni ca | [SDhPS, 1 139.1]
sarve ca te 'nuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddhāḥ | [SDhPS, 1 140.1]
paścimakaśca teṣāṃ dīpaṃkaro 'bhūttathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ | [SDhPS, 1 141.1]
teṣāṃ ca aṣṭānāmantevāsiśatānāmeko bodhisattvo 'dhimātraṃ lābhaguruko 'bhūt satkāraguruko jñātaguruko yaśaskāmaḥ | [SDhPS, 1 142.1]
tasyoddiṣṭoddiṣṭāni padavyañjanānyantardhīyante na saṃtiṣṭhante sma | [SDhPS, 1 143.1]
tasya yaśaskāma ityeva saṃjñābhūt | [SDhPS, 1 144.1]
tenāpi tena kuśalamūlena bahūni buddhakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇyārāgitānyabhūvan | [SDhPS, 1 145.1]
ārāgayitvā ca satkṛtāni gurukṛtāni mānitāni pūjitānyarcitānyapacāyitāni | [SDhPS, 1 146.1]
syātkhalu punaste ajita kāṅkṣā vā vimatirvā vicikitsā vā | [SDhPS, 1 147.1]
anyaḥ sa tena kālena tena samayena varaprabho nāma bodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'bhūddharmabhāṇakaḥ | [SDhPS, 1 147.2]
na khalu punarevaṃ draṣṭavyam | [SDhPS, 1 148.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 1 149.1]
ahaṃ sa tena kālena tena samayena varaprabho nāma bodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'bhūddharmabhāṇakaḥ | [SDhPS, 1 149.2]
yaścāsau yaśaskāmo nāma bodhisattvo 'bhūt kausīdyaprāptaḥ tvameva ajita sa tena kālena tena samayena yaśaskāmo nāma bodhisattvo 'bhūt kausīdyaprāptaḥ | [SDhPS, 1 150.1]
iti hi ajita ahamanena paryāyeṇedaṃ bhagavataḥ pūrvanimittaṃ dṛṣṭvā evaṃrūpāṃ raśmimutsṛṣṭāmevaṃ parimīmāṃse yathā bhagavānapi taṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ sūtrāntaṃ mahāvaipulyaṃ bodhisattvāvavādaṃ sarvabuddhaparigrahaṃ bhāṣitukāmaḥ | [SDhPS, 1 151.1]
atha khalu mañjuśrīḥ kumārabhūta etamevārthaṃ bhūyasyā mātrayā pradarśayamānastasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 1 152.1]
{SDhPS, 2}
atha khalu bhagavān smṛtimān samprajānaṃstataḥ samādhervyutthitaḥ | [SDhPS, 2 1.1]
vyutthāya āyuṣmantaṃ śāriputramāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 2 2.1]
gambhīraṃ śāriputra durdṛśaṃ duranubodhaṃ buddhajñānaṃ tathāgatairarhadbhiḥ samyaksaṃbuddhaiḥ pratibuddham | [SDhPS, 2 2.2]
durvijñeyaṃ sarvaśrāvakapratyekabuddhaiḥ | [SDhPS, 2 2.3]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 2 3.1]
bahubuddhakoṭīnayutaśatasahasraparyupāsitāvino hi śāriputra tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhā bahubuddhakoṭīnayutaśatasahasracīrṇacaritāvino 'nuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau dūrānugatāḥ kṛtavīryā āścaryādbhutadharmasamanvāgatā durvijñeyadharmasamanvāgatā durvijñeyadharmānujñātāvinaḥ | [SDhPS, 2 3.2]
durvijñeyaṃ śāriputra saṃdhābhāṣyaṃ tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānām | [SDhPS, 2 4.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 2 5.1]
svapratyayān dharmān prakāśayanti vividhopāyakauśalyajñānadarśanahetukāraṇanirdeśanārambaṇaniruktiprajñaptibhis tairupāyakauśalyaistasmiṃstasmiṃllagnān sattvān pramocayitum | [SDhPS, 2 5.2]
mahopāyakauśalyajñānadarśanaparamapāramitāprāptāḥ śāriputra tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ | [SDhPS, 2 6.1]
asaṅgāpratihatajñānadarśanabalavaiśāradyāveṇikendriyabalabodhyaṅgadhyānavimokṣasamādhisamāpattyadbhutadharmasamanvāgatā vividhadharmasaṃprakāśakāḥ | [SDhPS, 2 7.1]
mahāścaryādbhutaprāptāḥ śāriputra tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ | [SDhPS, 2 8.1]
alaṃ śāriputra etāvadeva bhāṣituṃ bhavatu | [SDhPS, 2 9.1]
paramāścaryaprāptāḥ śāriputra tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ | [SDhPS, 2 9.2]
tathāgata eva śāriputra tathāgatasya dharmān deśayed yān dharmāṃstathāgato jānāti | [SDhPS, 2 10.1]
sarvadharmānapi śāriputra tathāgata eva deśayati | [SDhPS, 2 11.1]
sarvadharmānapi tathāgata eva jānāti ye ca te dharmāḥ yathā ca te dharmāḥ yādṛśāśca te dharmāḥ yallakṣaṇāśca te dharmāḥ yatsvabhāvāśca te dharmāḥ ye ca yathā ca yādṛśāśca yallakṣaṇāśca yatsvabhāvāśca te dharmā iti | [SDhPS, 2 12.1]
teṣu dharmeṣu tathāgata eva pratyakṣo 'parokṣaḥ | [SDhPS, 2 13.1]
atha khalu bhagavānetamevārthaṃ bhūyasyā mātrayā saṃdarśayamānastasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 2 14.1]
atha khalu ye tatra parṣatsaṃnipāte mahāśrāvakā ājñātakauṇḍinyapramukhā arhantaḥ kṣīṇāsravā dvādaśa vaśībhūtaśatāni ye cānye śrāvakayānikā bhikṣubhikṣuṇyupāsakopāsikā ye ca pratyekabuddhayānasamprasthitās teṣāṃ sarveṣāmetadabhavat | [SDhPS, 2 36.1]
ko nu hetuḥ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ yad bhagavānadhimātramupāyakauśalyaṃ tathāgatānāṃ saṃvarṇayati | [SDhPS, 2 36.2]
gambhīraścāyaṃ mayā dharmo 'bhisaṃbuddha iti saṃvarṇayati | [SDhPS, 2 36.3]
durvijñeyaśca sarvaśrāvakapratyekabuddhairiti saṃvarṇayati | [SDhPS, 2 36.4]
yathā tāvad bhagavatā ekaiva vimuktirākhyātā vayamapi buddhadharmāṇāṃ lābhino nirvāṇaprāptāḥ | [SDhPS, 2 36.5]
asya ca vayaṃ bhagavato bhāṣitasyārthaṃ na jānīmaḥ | [SDhPS, 2 37.1]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputrastāsāṃ catasṛṇāṃ parṣadāṃ vicikitsākathaṃkathāṃ viditvā cetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya ātmanā ca dharmasaṃśayaprāptastasyāṃ velāyāṃ bhagavantametadavocat | [SDhPS, 2 38.1]
ko bhagavan hetuḥ kaḥ pratyayo yad bhagavānadhimātraṃ punaḥ punastathāgatānām upāyakauśalyajñānadarśanadharmadeśanāṃ saṃvarṇayati gambhīraśca me dharmo 'bhisaṃbuddha iti | [SDhPS, 2 38.2]
durvijñeyaṃ ca saṃdhābhāṣyam iti punaḥ punaḥ saṃvarṇayati | [SDhPS, 2 39.1]
na ca me bhagavato 'ntikādevaṃrūpo dharmaparyāyaḥ śrutapūrvaḥ | [SDhPS, 2 40.1]
imāśca bhagavaṃścatasraḥ parṣado vicikitsākathaṃkathāprāptāḥ | [SDhPS, 2 41.1]
tatsādhu bhagavānnirdiśatu yatsaṃghāya tathāgato gambhīrasya tathāgatadharmasya punaḥ punaḥ saṃvarṇanāṃ karoti | [SDhPS, 2 42.1]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputrastasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 2 43.1]
evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat | [SDhPS, 2 55.1]
alaṃ śāriputra | [SDhPS, 2 55.2]
kimanenārthena bhāṣitena | [SDhPS, 2 56.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 2 56.2]
uttrasiṣyati śāriputra ayaṃ sadevako loko 'sminnarthe vyākriyamāṇe | [SDhPS, 2 56.3]
dvaitīyakamapyāyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantamadhyeṣate sma | [SDhPS, 2 57.1]
bhāṣatāṃ bhagavān bhāṣatāṃ sugata etamevārtham | [SDhPS, 2 57.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 2 58.1]
santi bhagavaṃstasyāṃ parṣadi bahūni prāṇiśatāni bahūni prāṇisahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇiśatasahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇikoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi pūrvabuddhadarśāvīni prajñāvanti yāni bhagavato bhāṣitaṃ śraddhāsyanti pratīyiṣyanti udgrahīṣyanti | [SDhPS, 2 58.2]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantamanayā gāthayādhyabhāṣata | [SDhPS, 2 59.1]
atha khalu bhagavān dvaitīyakamapyāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat | [SDhPS, 2 61.1]
alaṃ śāriputra anenārthena prakāśitena | [SDhPS, 2 61.2]
uttrasiṣyati śāriputra ayaṃ sadevako loko 'sminnarthe vyākriyamāṇe | [SDhPS, 2 62.1]
abhimānaprāptāśca bhikṣavo mahāprapātaṃ prapatiṣyanti | [SDhPS, 2 63.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimāṃ gāthāmabhāṣata | [SDhPS, 2 64.1]
traitīyakam apyāyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantamadhyeṣate sma | [SDhPS, 2 66.1]
bhāṣatāṃ bhagavān bhāṣatāṃ sugata etamevārtham | [SDhPS, 2 66.2]
mādṛśānāṃ bhagavanniha parṣadi bahūni prāṇiśatāni saṃvidyante anyāni ca bhagavan bahūni prāṇiśatāni bahūni prāṇisahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇiśatasahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇikoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi yāni bhagavatā pūrvabhaveṣu paripācitāni tāni bhagavato bhāṣitaṃ śraddhāsyanti pratīyiṣyanti udgrahīṣyanti | [SDhPS, 2 67.1]
teṣāṃ tad bhaviṣyati dīrgharātramarthāya hitāya sukhāyeti | [SDhPS, 2 68.1]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputrastasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 2 69.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstraitīyakamapyāyuṣmataḥ śāriputrasyādhyeṣaṇāṃ viditvā āyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat | [SDhPS, 2 73.1]
yadidānīṃ tvaṃ śāriputra yāvat traitīyakamapi tathāgatamadhyeṣase | [SDhPS, 2 73.2]
evam adhyeṣamāṇaṃ tvāṃ śāriputra kiṃ vakṣyāmi | [SDhPS, 2 74.1]
tena hi śāriputra śṛṇu sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuru | [SDhPS, 2 74.2]
bhāṣiṣye 'haṃ te | [SDhPS, 2 75.1]
samanantarabhāṣitā ceyaṃ bhagavatā vāk | [SDhPS, 2 76.1]
atha khalu tataḥ parṣada ābhimānikānāṃ bhikṣūṇāṃ bhikṣuṇīnām upāsakānām upāsikānāṃ pañcamātrāṇi sahasrāṇyutthāya āsanebhyo bhagavataḥ pādau śirasābhivanditvā tataḥ parṣado 'pakrāmanti sma | [SDhPS, 2 76.2]
yathāpīdamabhimānākuśalamūlena aprāpte prāptasaṃjñino 'nadhigate 'dhigatasaṃjñinaḥ | [SDhPS, 2 76.3]
te ātmānaṃ savraṇaṃ jñātvā tataḥ parṣado 'pakrāntāḥ | [SDhPS, 2 77.1]
bhagavāṃśca tūṣṇīṃbhāvenādhivāsayati sma | [SDhPS, 2 78.1]
atha khalu bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputramāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 2 79.1]
niṣpalāvā me śāriputra parṣat apagataphalguḥ śraddhāsāre pratiṣṭhitā | [SDhPS, 2 79.2]
sādhu śāriputra eteṣām ābhimānikānām ato 'pakramaṇam | [SDhPS, 2 80.1]
tena hi śāriputra bhāṣiṣye etamartham | [SDhPS, 2 81.1]
sādhu bhagavannityāyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt | [SDhPS, 2 82.1]
bhagavānetadavocat | [SDhPS, 2 83.1]
kadācit karhicicchāriputra tathāgata evaṃrūpāṃ dharmadeśanāṃ kathayati | [SDhPS, 2 83.2]
tadyathāpi nāma śāriputra udumbarapuṣpaṃ kadācit karhicit saṃdṛśyate evameva śāriputra tathāgato 'pi kadācit karhicit evaṃrūpāṃ dharmadeśanāṃ kathayati | [SDhPS, 2 84.1]
śraddadhata me śāriputra bhūtavādyahamasmi tathāvādyahamasmi ananyathāvādyahamasmi | [SDhPS, 2 85.1]
durbodhyaṃ śāriputra tathāgatasya saṃdhābhāṣyam | [SDhPS, 2 86.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 2 87.1]
nānāniruktinirdeśābhilāpanirdeśanairmayā śāriputra vividhairupāyakauśalyaśatasahasrairdharmaḥ saṃprakāśitaḥ | [SDhPS, 2 87.2]
atarko 'tarkāvacaras tathāgatavijñeyaḥ śāriputra saddharmaḥ | [SDhPS, 2 88.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 2 89.1]
ekakṛtyena śāriputra ekakaraṇīyena tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loka utpadyate mahākṛtyena mahākaraṇīyena | [SDhPS, 2 89.2]
katamaṃ ca śāriputra tathāgatasya ekakṛtyamekakaraṇīyaṃ mahākṛtyaṃ mahākaraṇīyaṃ yena kṛtyena tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loka utpadyate | [SDhPS, 2 90.1]
yadidaṃ tathāgatajñānadarśanasamādāpanahetunimittaṃ sattvānāṃ tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loka utpadyate | [SDhPS, 2 90.2]
tathāgatajñānadarśanasaṃdarśanahetunimittaṃ sattvānāṃ tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loka utpadyate | [SDhPS, 2 91.1]
tathāgatajñānadarśanāvatāraṇahetunimittaṃ sattvānāṃ tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loka utpadyate | [SDhPS, 2 92.1]
tathāgatajñānapratibodhanahetunimittaṃ sattvānāṃ tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loka utpadyate | [SDhPS, 2 93.1]
tathāgatajñānadarśanamārgāvatāraṇahetunimittaṃ sattvānāṃ tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loka utpadyate | [SDhPS, 2 94.1]
idaṃ tacchāriputra tathāgatasya ekakṛtyamekakaraṇīyaṃ mahākṛtyaṃ mahākaraṇīyamekaprayojanaṃ loke prādurbhāvāya | [SDhPS, 2 95.1]
iti hi śāriputra yattathāgatasya ekakṛtyamekakaraṇīyaṃ mahākṛtyaṃ mahākaraṇīyaṃ tattathāgataḥ karoti | [SDhPS, 2 96.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 2 97.1]
tathāgatajñānadarśanasamādāpaka evāhaṃ śāriputra tathāgatajñānadarśanasaṃdarśaka evāhaṃ śāriputra tathāgatajñānadarśanāvatāraka evāhaṃ śāriputra tathāgatajñānadarśanapratibodhaka evāhaṃ śāriputra tathāgatajñānadarśanamārgāvatāraka evāhaṃ śāriputra | [SDhPS, 2 97.2]
ekamevāhaṃ śāriputra yānamārabhya sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśayāmi yadidaṃ buddhayānam | [SDhPS, 2 98.1]
na kiṃcicchāriputra dvitīyaṃ vā tṛtīyaṃ vā yānaṃ saṃvidyate | [SDhPS, 2 99.1]
sarvatraiṣā śāriputra dharmatā daśadigloke | [SDhPS, 2 100.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 2 101.1]
ye 'pi tu śāriputra atīte 'dhvanyabhūvan daśasu dikṣvaprameyeṣvasaṃkhyeyeṣu lokadhātuṣu tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhā bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāyai mahato janakāyasyārthāya hitāya sukhāya devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca | [SDhPS, 2 101.2]
ye nānābhinirhāranirdeśavividhahetukāraṇanidarśanārambaṇaniruktyupāyakauśalyair nānādhimuktānāṃ sattvānāṃ nānādhātvāśayānām āśayaṃ viditvā dharmaṃ deśitavantaḥ | [SDhPS, 2 102.1]
te 'pi sarve śāriputra buddhā bhagavanta ekameva yānamārabhya sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśitavantaḥ yadidaṃ buddhayānaṃ sarvajñatāparyavasānaṃ yadidaṃ tathāgatajñānadarśanasamādāpanam eva sattvānāṃ tathāgatajñānadarśanasaṃdarśanameva tathāgatajñānadarśanāvatāraṇameva tathāgatajñānadarśanapratibodhanameva tathāgatajñānadarśanamārgāvatāraṇameva sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśitavantaḥ | [SDhPS, 2 103.1]
yairapi śāriputra sattvaisteṣāmatītānāṃ tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāmantikāt saddharmaḥ śrutas te 'pi sarve 'nuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodherlābhino 'bhūvan | [SDhPS, 2 104.1]
ye 'pi te śāriputra anāgate 'dhvani bhaviṣyanti daśasu dikṣvaprameyeṣvasaṃkhyeyeṣu lokadhātuṣu tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhā bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāyai mahato janakāyasyārthāya hitāya sukhāya devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca ye ca nānābhinihāranirdeśavividhahetukāraṇanidarśanārambaṇaniruktyupāyakauśalyair nānādhimuktānāṃ sattvānāṃ nānādhātvāśayānām āśayaṃ viditvā dharmaṃ deśayiṣyanti te 'pi sarve śāriputra buddhā bhagavanta ekameva yānamārabhya sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśayiṣyanti yadidaṃ buddhayānaṃ sarvajñatāparyavasānaṃ yadidaṃ tathāgatajñānadarśanasamādāpanam eva sattvānāṃ tathāgatajñānadarśanasaṃdarśanameva tathāgatajñānadarśanāvatāraṇameva tathāgatajñānadarśanapratibodhanameva tathāgatajñānadarśanamārgāvatāraṇameva sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśayiṣyanti | [SDhPS, 2 105.1]
ye 'pi te śāriputra sattvās teṣām anāgatānāṃ tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāmantikāt taṃ dharmaṃ śroṣyanti te 'pi sarve 'nuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodherlābhino bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 2 106.1]
ye 'pi te śāriputra etarhi pratyutpanne 'dhvani daśasu dikṣvaprameyeṣvasaṃkhyeyeṣu lokadhātuṣu tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāstiṣṭhanti dhriyante yāpayanti dharmaṃ ca deśayanti bahujanahitāya bahujanahitāya lokānukampāyai mahato janakāyasyārthāya hitāya sukhāya devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca ye nānābhinirhāranirdeśavividhahetukāraṇanidarśanārambaṇaniruktyupāyakauśalyair nānādhimuktānāṃ sattvānāṃ nānādhātvāśayānām āśayaṃ viditvā dharmaṃ deśayanti te 'pi sarve śāriputra buddhā bhagavanta ekameva yānamārabhya sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśayanti yadidaṃ buddhayānaṃ sarvajñatāparyavasānaṃ yadidaṃ tathāgatajñānadarśanasamādāpanam eva sattvānāṃ tathāgatajñānadarśanasaṃdarśanameva tathāgatajñānadarśanāvatāraṇameva tathāgatajñānadarśanapratibodhanameva tathāgatajñānadarśanamārgāvatāraṇameva sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśayanti | [SDhPS, 2 107.1]
ye 'pi te śāriputra sattvāsteṣāṃ pratyutpannānāṃ tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāmantikāt taṃ dharmaṃ śṛṇvanti te 'pi sarve 'nuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodherlābhino bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 2 108.1]
ahamapi śāriputra etarhi tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāyai mahato janakāyasyārthāya hitāya sukhāya devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca nānābhinirhāranirdeśavividhahetukāraṇanidarśanārambaṇaniruktyupāyakauśalyairnānādhimuktānāṃ sattvānāṃ nānādhātvāśayānām āśayaṃ viditvā dharmaṃ deśayāmi | [SDhPS, 2 109.1]
ahamapi śāriputra ekameva yānamārabhya sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśayāmi yadidaṃ buddhayānaṃ sarvajñatāparyavasānaṃ yadidaṃ tathāgatajñānadarśanasamādāpanam eva sattvānāṃ tathāgatajñānadarśanasaṃdarśanameva tathāgatajñānadarśanāvatāraṇam eva tathāgatajñānadarśanapratibodhanameva tathāgatajñānadarśanamārgāvatāraṇam eva sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśayāmi | [SDhPS, 2 110.1]
ye 'pi te śāriputra sattvā etarhi mamemaṃ dharmaṃ śṛṇvanti te 'pi sarve 'nuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodherlābhino bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 2 111.1]
tadanenāpi śāriputra paryāyeṇa evaṃ veditavyaṃ yathā nāsti dvitīyasya yānasya kvaciddaśasu dikṣu loke prajñaptiḥ kutaḥ punastṛtīyasya | [SDhPS, 2 112.1]
api tu khalu punaḥ śāriputra yadā tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ kalpakaṣāye votpadyante sattvakaṣāye vā kleśakaṣāye vā dṛṣṭikaṣāye vā āyuṣkaṣāye votpadyante | [SDhPS, 2 113.1]
evaṃrūpeṣu śāriputra kalpasaṃkṣobhakaṣāyeṣu bahusattveṣu lubdheṣvalpakuśalamūleṣu tadā śāriputra tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhā upāyakauśalyena tadevaikaṃ buddhayānaṃ triyānanirdeśena nirdiśanti | [SDhPS, 2 114.1]
tatra śāriputra ye śrāvakā arhantaḥ pratyekabuddhā vā imāṃ kriyāṃ tathāgatasya buddhayānasamādāpanāṃ na śṛṇvanti nāvataranti nāvabudhyanti na te śāriputra tathāgatasya śrāvakā veditavyā nāpyarhanto nāpi pratyekabuddhā veditavyāḥ | [SDhPS, 2 115.1]
api tu khalu punaḥ śāriputra yaḥ kaścid bhikṣurvā bhikṣuṇī vā arhattvaṃ pratijānīyād anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau praṇidhānam aparigṛhya ucchinno 'smi buddhayānāditi vaded etāvanme samucchrayasya paścimakaṃ parinirvāṇaṃ vaded ābhimānikaṃ taṃ śāriputra prajānīyāḥ | [SDhPS, 2 116.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 2 117.1]
asthānametacchāriputra anavakāśo yadbhikṣurarhan kṣīṇāsravaḥ saṃmukhībhūte tathāgate imaṃ dharmaṃ śrutvā na śraddadhyāt sthāpayitvā parinirvṛtasya tathāgatasya | [SDhPS, 2 117.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 2 118.1]
na hi śāriputra śrāvakāstasmin kāle tasmin samaye parinirvṛte tathāgate eteṣāmevaṃrūpāṇāṃ sūtrāntānāṃ dhārakā vā deśakā vā bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 2 118.2]
anyeṣu punaḥ śāriputra tathāgateṣvarhatsu samyaksaṃbuddheṣu niḥsaṃśayā bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 2 119.1]
imeṣu buddhadharmeṣu śraddadhādhvaṃ me śāriputra pattīyata avakalpayata | [SDhPS, 2 120.1]
na hi śāriputra tathāgatānāṃ mṛṣāvādaḥ saṃvidyate | [SDhPS, 2 121.1]
ekamevedaṃ śāriputra yānaṃ yadidaṃ buddhayānam | [SDhPS, 2 122.1]
atha khalu bhagavānetamevārthaṃ bhūyasyā mātrayā saṃdarśayamānastasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 2 123.1]
{SDhPS, 3}
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputrastasyāṃ velāyāṃ tuṣṭa udagra āttamanāḥ pramuditaḥ prītisaumanasyajāto yena bhagavāṃstenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavato 'bhimukho bhagavantameva vyavalokayamāno bhagavantametadavocat | [SDhPS, 3 1.1]
āścaryādbhutaprāpto 'smi bhagavan audbilyaprāptaḥ idamevaṃrūpaṃ bhagavato 'ntikād ghoṣaṃ śrutvā | [SDhPS, 3 1.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 3 2.1]
aśrutvaiva tāvadahaṃ bhagavan idamevaṃrūpaṃ bhagavato 'ntikād dharmaṃ tadanyān bodhisattvān dṛṣṭvā bodhisattvānāṃ ca anāgate 'dhvani buddhanāma śrutvā atīva śocāmi atīva saṃtapye bhraṣṭo 'smyevaṃrūpāt tathāgatajñānagocarājjñānadarśanāt | [SDhPS, 3 2.2]
yadā cāhaṃ bhagavan abhīkṣṇaṃ gacchāmi parvatagirikandarāṇi vanaṣaṇḍānyārāmanadīvṛkṣamūlānyekāntāni divāvihārāya tadāpyahaṃ bhagavan yadbhūyastvena anenaiva vihāreṇa viharāmi | [SDhPS, 3 3.1]
tulye nāma dharmadhātupraveśe vayaṃ bhagavatā hīnena yānena niryātitāḥ | [SDhPS, 3 4.1]
evaṃ ca me bhagavaṃstasmin samaye bhavati | [SDhPS, 3 5.1]
asmākamevaiṣo 'parādho naiva bhagavato 'parādhaḥ | [SDhPS, 3 5.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 3 6.1]
sacedbhagavānasmābhiḥ pratīkṣitaḥ syāt sāmutkarṣikīṃ dharmadeśanāṃ kathayamāno yadidamanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimārabhya teṣveva vayaṃ bhagavan dharmeṣu niryātāḥ syāma | [SDhPS, 3 6.2]
yatpunarbhagavan asmābhir anupasthiteṣu bodhisattveṣu saṃdhābhāṣyaṃ bhagavato 'jānamānais tvaramāṇaiḥ prathamabhāṣitaiva tathāgatasya dharmadeśanā śrutvodgṛhītā dhāritā bhāvitā cintitā manasikṛtā | [SDhPS, 3 7.1]
so 'haṃ bhagavan ātmaparibhāṣaṇayaiva bhūyiṣṭhena rātriṃdivānyatināmayāmi | [SDhPS, 3 8.1]
adyāsmi bhagavan nirvāṇaprāptaḥ | [SDhPS, 3 9.1]
adyāsmi bhagavan parinirvṛtaḥ | [SDhPS, 3 10.1]
adya me bhagavan arhattvaṃ prāptam | [SDhPS, 3 11.1]
adyāhaṃ bhagavan bhagavataḥ putro jyeṣṭha auraso mukhato jāto dharmajo dharmanirmito dharmadāyādo dharmanirvṛttaḥ | [SDhPS, 3 12.1]
apagataparidāho 'smyadya bhagavan imamevaṃrūpamadbhutadharmam aśrutapūrvaṃ bhagavato 'ntikād ghoṣaṃ śrutvā | [SDhPS, 3 13.1]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputrastasyāṃ velāyāṃ bhagavantamābhirgāthābhiradhyabhāṣata | [SDhPS, 3 14.1]
evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat | [SDhPS, 3 37.1]
ārocayāmi te śāriputra prativedayāmi te asya sadevakasya lokasya purataḥ samārakasya sabrahmakasya saśramaṇabrāhmaṇikāyāḥ prajāyāḥ purataḥ | [SDhPS, 3 37.2]
mayā tvaṃ śāriputra viṃśatīnāṃ buddhakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇāmantike paripācito 'nuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 3 38.1]
mama ca tvaṃ śāriputra dīrgharātram anuśikṣito 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 3 39.1]
sa tvaṃ śāriputra bodhisattvasaṃmantritena bodhisattvarahasyena iha mama pravacane upapannaḥ | [SDhPS, 3 40.1]
sa tvaṃ śāriputra bodhisattvādhiṣṭhānena tatpaurvakaṃ caryāpraṇidhānaṃ bodhisattvasaṃmantritaṃ bodhisattvarahasyaṃ na samanusmarasi | [SDhPS, 3 41.1]
nirvṛto 'smīti manyase | [SDhPS, 3 42.1]
so 'haṃ tvāṃ śāriputra pūrvacaryāpraṇidhānajñānānubodham anusmārayitukāma imaṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ sūtrāntaṃ mahāvaipulyaṃ bodhisattvāvavādaṃ sarvabuddhaparigrahaṃ śrāvakāṇāṃ saṃprakāśayāmi | [SDhPS, 3 43.1]
api khalu punaḥ śāriputra bhaviṣyasi tvamanāgate 'dhvani aprameyaiḥ kalpair acintyairapramāṇair bahūnāṃ tathāgatakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇāṃ saddharmaṃ dhārayitvā vividhāṃ ca pūjāṃ kṛtvā imāmeva bodhisattvacaryāṃ paripūrya padmaprabho nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loke bhaviṣyasi vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān | [SDhPS, 3 44.1]
tena khalu punaḥ śāriputra samayena tasya bhagavataḥ padmaprabhasya tathāgatasya virajaṃ nāma buddhakṣetraṃ bhaviṣyati samaṃ ramaṇīyaṃ prāsādikaṃ paramasudarśanīyaṃ pariśuddhaṃ ca sphītaṃ ca ṛddhaṃ ca kṣemaṃ ca subhikṣaṃ ca bahujananārīgaṇākīrṇaṃ ca maruprakīrṇaṃ ca vaiḍūryamayaṃ suvarṇasūtrāṣṭāpadanibaddham | [SDhPS, 3 45.1]
teṣu ca aṣṭāpadeṣu ratnavṛkṣā bhaviṣyanti saptānāṃ ratnānāṃ puṣpaphalaiḥ satatasamitaṃ samarpitāḥ | [SDhPS, 3 46.1]
so 'pi śāriputra padmaprabhastathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhastrīṇyeva yānānyārabhya dharmaṃ deśayiṣyati | [SDhPS, 3 47.1]
kiṃcāpi śāriputra sa tathāgato na kalpakaṣāya utpatsyate | [SDhPS, 3 48.1]
api tu praṇidhānavaśena dharmaṃ deśayiṣyati | [SDhPS, 3 48.2]
mahāratnapratimaṇḍitaśca nāma śāriputra sa kalpo bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 3 49.1]
tatkiṃ manyase śāriputra kena kāraṇena sa kalpo mahāratnapratimaṇḍita ityucyate | [SDhPS, 3 50.1]
ratnāni śāriputra buddhakṣetre bodhisattvā ucyante | [SDhPS, 3 50.2]
te tasmin kāle tasyāṃ virajāyāṃ lokadhātau bahavo bodhisattvā bhaviṣyantyaprameyā asaṃkhyeyā acintyā atulyā amāpyā gaṇanāṃ samatikrāntā anyatra tathāgatagaṇanayā | [SDhPS, 3 51.1]
tena kāraṇena sa kalpo mahāratnapratimaṇḍita ityucyate | [SDhPS, 3 52.1]
tena khalu punaḥ śāriputra samayena bodhisattvāstasmin buddhakṣetre yadbhūyasā ratnapadmavikrāmiṇo bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 3 53.1]
anādikarmikāśca te bodhisattvā bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 3 54.1]
ciracaritakuśalamūlā bahubuddhaśatasahasracīrṇabrahmacaryās tathāgataparisaṃstutā buddhajñānābhiyuktā mahābhijñāparikarmanirjātāḥ sarvadharmanayakuśalā mārdavāḥ smṛtimantaḥ | [SDhPS, 3 55]
bhūyiṣṭhena śāriputra evaṃrūpāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ paripūrṇaṃ tadbuddhakṣetraṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 3 56.1]
tasya khalu punaḥ śāriputra padmaprabhasya tathāgatasya dvādaśāntarakalpā āyuṣpramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati sthāpayitvā kumārabhūtatvam | [SDhPS, 3 57.1]
teṣāṃ ca sattvānāmaṣṭāntarakalpā āyuṣpramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 3 58.1]
sa ca śāriputra padmaprabhastathāgato dvādaśānām antarakalpānām atyayena dhṛtiparipūrṇaṃ nāma bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvaṃ vyākṛtya anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau parinirvāsyati | [SDhPS, 3 59.1]
ayaṃ bhikṣavo dhṛtiparipūrṇo bodhisattvo mahāsattvo mamānantaramanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbhotsyate | [SDhPS, 3 60.1]
padmavṛṣabhavikrāmī nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loke bhaviṣyati vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān | [SDhPS, 3 61.1]
tasyāpi śāriputra padmavṛṣabhavikrāmiṇastathāgatasya evaṃrūpameva buddhakṣetraṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 3 62.1]
tasya khalu punaḥ śāriputra padmaprabhasya tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya dvātriṃśadantarakalpān saddharmaḥ sthāsyati | [SDhPS, 3 63.1]
tatastasya tasmin saddharme kṣīṇe dvātriṃśadantarakalpān saddharmapratirūpakaḥ sthāsyati | [SDhPS, 3 64.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 3 65.1]
atha khalu tāścatasraḥ parṣado bhikṣubhikṣuṇyupāsakopāsikā devanāgayakṣagandharvāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragamanuṣyāmanuṣyā āyuṣmataḥ śāriputrasyedaṃ vyākaraṇamanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau bhagavato 'ntikāt saṃmukhaṃ śrutvā tuṣṭā udagrā āttamanasaḥ pramuditāḥ prītisaumanasyajātāḥ svakasvakaiścīvarairbhagavantam abhicchādayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 3 76.1]
śakraśca devānāmindro brahmā ca sahāṃpatiranyāśca devaputraśatasahasrakoṭyo bhagavantaṃ divyairvastrair abhicchādayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 3 77.1]
divyaiśca māndāravairmahāmāndaravaiśca puṣpairabhyavakiranti sma | [SDhPS, 3 78.1]
divyāni ca vastrāṇyuparyantarīkṣe bhrāmayanti sma | [SDhPS, 3 79.1]
divyāni ca tūryaśatasahasrāṇi dundubhayaścoparyantarīkṣe parāhananti sma | [SDhPS, 3 80.1]
mahāntaṃ ca puṣpavarṣam abhipravarṣayitvā evaṃ ca vācaṃ bhāṣante sma | [SDhPS, 3 81.1]
pūrvaṃ bhagavatā vārāṇasyāmṛṣipatane mṛgadāve dharmacakraṃ pravartitam | [SDhPS, 3 81.2]
idaṃ punarbhagavatā adya anuttaraṃ dvitīyaṃ dharmacakraṃ pravartitam | [SDhPS, 3 82.1]
te ca devaputrāstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣanta | [SDhPS, 3 83.1]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat | [SDhPS, 3 90.1]
niṣkāṅkṣo 'smi bhagavan vigatakathaṃkatho bhagavato 'ntikāt saṃmukhamidamātmano vyākaraṇaṃ śrutvā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 3 90.2]
yāni ca imāni bhagavan dvādaśa vaśībhūtaśatāni bhagavatā pūrvaṃ śaikṣabhūmau sthāpitāni evamavavaditāni evamanuśiṣṭānyabhūvan etatparyavasāno me bhikṣavo dharmavinayo yadidaṃ jātijarāvyādhimaraṇaśokasamatikramo nirvāṇasamavasaraṇaḥ | [SDhPS, 3 91.1]
ime ca bhagavan dve bhikṣusahasre śaikṣāśaikṣāṇāṃ bhagavataḥ śrāvakāṇāṃ sarveṣām ātmadṛṣṭibhavadṛṣṭivibhavadṛṣṭisarvadṛṣṭivivarjitānāṃ nirvāṇabhūmisthitāḥ smaḥ ityātmanaḥ saṃjānatām | [SDhPS, 3 92.1]
te bhagavato 'ntikādimamevaṃrūpam aśrutapūrvaṃ dharmaṃ śrutvā kathaṃkathāmāpannāḥ | [SDhPS, 3 92.2]
tatsādhu bhagavān bhāṣatāmeṣāṃ bhikṣūṇāṃ kaukṛtyavinodanārthaṃ yathā bhagavannetāścatasraḥ parṣado niṣkāṅkṣā nirvicikitsā bhaveyuḥ | [SDhPS, 3 93.1]
evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat | [SDhPS, 3 94.1]
nanu te mayā śāriputra pūrvamevākhyātaṃ yathā nānābhinirhāranirdeśavividhahetukāraṇanidarśanārambaṇaniruktyupāyakauśalyair nānādhimuktānāṃ sattvānāṃ nānādhātvāśayānām āśayaṃ viditvā tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho dharmaṃ deśayati | [SDhPS, 3 94.2]
imāmevānuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimārabhya sarvadharmadeśanābhir bodhisattvayānam eva samādāpayati | [SDhPS, 3 95.1]
api tu khalu punaḥ śāriputra aupamyaṃ te kariṣyāmi asyaivārthasya bhūyasyā mātrayā saṃdarśanārtham | [SDhPS, 3 96.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 3 97.1]
upamayā iha ekatyā vijñapuruṣā bhāṣitasyārthamājānanti | [SDhPS, 3 97.2]
tadyathāpi nāma śāriputra iha syāt kasmiṃścideva grāme vā nagare vā nigame vā janapade vā janapadapradeśe vā rāṣṭre vā rājadhānyāṃ vā gṛhapatirjīrṇo vṛddho mahallako 'bhyatītavayo'nuprāpta āḍhyo mahādhano mahābhogaḥ | [SDhPS, 3 98.1]
mahaccāsya niveśanaṃ bhaveducchritaṃ ca vistīrṇaṃ ca cirakṛtaṃ ca jīrṇaṃ ca dvayorvā trayāṇāṃ vā caturṇāṃ vā pañcānāṃ vā prāṇiśatānāmāvāsaḥ | [SDhPS, 3 99.1]
ekadvāraṃ ca tanniveśanaṃ bhavet | [SDhPS, 3 100.1]
tṛṇasaṃchannaṃ ca bhavet | [SDhPS, 3 101.1]
vigalitaprāsādaṃ ca bhavet | [SDhPS, 3 102.1]
pūtistambhamūlaṃ ca bhavet | [SDhPS, 3 103.1]
saṃśīrṇakuḍyakaṭalepanaṃ ca bhavet | [SDhPS, 3 104.1]
tacca sahasaiva mahatāgniskandhena sarvapārśveṣu sarvāvantaṃ niveśanaṃ pradīptaṃ bhavet | [SDhPS, 3 105.1]
tasya ca puruṣasya bahavaḥ kumārakāḥ syuḥ pañca vā daśa vā viṃśatirvā | [SDhPS, 3 106.1]
sa ca puruṣastasmānniveśanād bahirnirgataḥ syāt | [SDhPS, 3 107.1]
atha khalu śāriputra sa puruṣastaṃ svakaṃ niveśanaṃ mahatāgniskandhena samantāt samprajvalitaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhītastrasta udvignacitto bhaved evaṃ cānuvicintayet | [SDhPS, 3 108.1]
pratibalo 'hamanena mahatāgniskandhenāsaṃspṛṣṭo 'paridagdhaḥ kṣiprameva svastinā asmād gṛhādādīptād dvāreṇa nirgantuṃ nirdhāvitum | [SDhPS, 3 108.2]
api tu ya ime mamaiva putrā bālakāḥ kumārakā asminneva niveśane ādīpte taistaiḥ krīḍanakaiḥ krīḍanti ramanti paricārayantīmaṃ cāgāramādīptaṃ na jānanti na budhyante na vidanti na cetayanti nodvegamāpadyante saṃtapyamānā apyanena mahatāgniskandhena mahatā ca duḥkhaskandhena spṛṣṭāḥ samānā na duḥkhaṃ manasi kurvanti nāpi nirgamanamanasikāramutpādayanti | [SDhPS, 3 109.1]
sa ca śāriputra puruṣo balavān bhaved bāhubalikaḥ | [SDhPS, 3 110.1]
sa evamanuvicintayet | [SDhPS, 3 111.1]
ahamasmi balavān bāhubalikaśca | [SDhPS, 3 111.2]
yannvahaṃ sarvānimān kumārakānekapiṇḍayitvā utsaṅgenādāya asmād gṛhānnirgamayeyam | [SDhPS, 3 112.1]
sa punarevamanuvicintayet | [SDhPS, 3 113.1]
idaṃ khalu niveśanamekapraveśaṃ saṃvṛtadvārameva | [SDhPS, 3 113.2]
kumārakāścapalāścañcalā bālajātīyāśca | [SDhPS, 3 114.1]
mā haiva paribhrameyuḥ | [SDhPS, 3 115.1]
te 'nena mahatāgniskandhenānayavyasanamāpadyeran | [SDhPS, 3 116.1]
yannūnamahametān saṃcodayeyam | [SDhPS, 3 117.1]
iti pratisaṃkhyāya tān kumārakānāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 3 118.1]
āgacchata bhavantaḥ kumārakā nirgacchata | [SDhPS, 3 118.2]
ādīptamidaṃ gṛhaṃ mahatā agniskandhena | [SDhPS, 3 119.1]
mā haivātraiva sarve 'nena mahatāgniskandhena dhakṣyatha anayavyasanamāpatsyatha | [SDhPS, 3 120.1]
atha khalu te kumārakā evaṃ tasya hitakāmasya puruṣasya tadbhāṣitaṃ nāvabudhyante nodvijanti nottrasanti na saṃtrasanti na saṃtrāsamāpadyante na vicintayanti na nirdhāvanti nāpi jānanti na vijānanti kimetadādīptaṃ nāmeti | [SDhPS, 3 121.1]
anyatra tena tenaiva dhāvanti vidhāvanti punaḥ punaśca taṃ pitaramavalokayanti | [SDhPS, 3 122.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 3 123.1]
yathāpīdaṃ bālabhāvatvāt | [SDhPS, 3 123.2]
atha khalu sa puruṣa evamanuvicintayet | [SDhPS, 3 124.1]
ādīptamidaṃ niveśanaṃ mahatāgniskandhena saṃpradīptam | [SDhPS, 3 124.2]
mā haivāhaṃ ceme ca kumārakā ihaivānena mahatāgniskandhena anayavyasanamāpatsyāmahe | [SDhPS, 3 125.1]
yannvahamupāyakauśalyenemān kumārakān asmād gṛhāt niṣkrāmayeyam | [SDhPS, 3 126.1]
sa ca puruṣasteṣāṃ kumārakāṇāmāśayajño bhaved adhimuktiṃ ca vijānīyāt | [SDhPS, 3 127.1]
teṣāṃ ca kumārakāṇāmanekavidhānyanekāni krīḍanakāni bhaveyurvividhāni ca ramaṇīyakānīṣṭāni kāntāni priyāṇi manaāpāni tāni ca durlabhāni bhaveyuḥ | [SDhPS, 3 128.1]
atha khalu sa puruṣasteṣāṃ kumārakāṇāmāśayaṃ jānaṃstān kumārakānetadavocat | [SDhPS, 3 129.1]
yāni tāni kumārakā yuṣmākaṃ krīḍanakāni ramaṇīyakānyāścaryādbhutāni yeṣāmalābhāt saṃtapyatha nānāvarṇāni bahuprakārāṇi | [SDhPS, 3 129.2]
tadyathā gorathakāny ajarathakāni mṛgarathakāni | [SDhPS, 3 130.1]
yāni bhavatāmiṣṭāni kāntāni priyāṇi manaāpāni | [SDhPS, 3 131.1]
tāni ca mayā sarvāṇi bahirniveśanadvāre sthāpitāni yuṣmākaṃ krīḍanahetoḥ | [SDhPS, 3 132.1]
āgacchantu bhavanto nirdhāvantvasmānniveśanāt | [SDhPS, 3 133.1]
ahaṃ vo yasya yasya yenārtho yena prayojanaṃ bhaviṣyati tasmai tasmai tatpradāsyāmi | [SDhPS, 3 134.1]
āgacchata śīghraṃ teṣāṃ kāraṇaṃ nirdhāvata | [SDhPS, 3 135.1]
atha khalu te kumārakāsteṣāṃ krīḍanakānāṃ ramaṇīyakānāmarthāya yathepsitānāṃ yathāsaṃkalpitānāmiṣṭānāṃ kāntānāṃ priyāṇāṃ manaāpānāṃ nāmadheyāni śrutvā tasmādādīptādagārāt kṣipramevārabdhavīryā balavatā javena anyonyam apratīkṣamāṇāḥ kaḥ prathamaṃ kaḥ prathamataramityanyonyaṃ saṃghaṭṭitakāyās tasmād ādīptādagārāt kṣiprameva nirdhāvitāḥ | [SDhPS, 3 136.1]
atha sa puruṣaḥ kṣemasvastinā tān kumārakān nirgatān dṛṣṭvā abhayaprāptāniti viditvā ākāśe grāmacatvare upaviṣṭaḥ prītiprāmodyajāto nirupādāno vigatanīvaraṇo 'bhayaprāpto bhavet | [SDhPS, 3 137.1]
atha khalu te kumārakā yena sa pitā tenopasaṃkrāman upasaṃkramyaivaṃ vadeyuḥ | [SDhPS, 3 138.1]
dehi nastāta tāni vividhāni krīḍanakāni ramaṇīyāni | [SDhPS, 3 138.2]
tadyathā | [SDhPS, 3 139.1]
gorathakānyajarathakāni mṛgarathakāni | [SDhPS, 3 139.2]
atha khalu śāriputra sa puruṣasteṣāṃ svakānāṃ putrāṇāṃ vātajavasampannān gorathakān evānuprayacchet saptaratnamayān savedikān sakiṅkiṇījālābhipralambitānuccān pragṛhītānāścaryādbhutaratnālaṃkṛtān ratnadāmakṛtaśobhān puṣpamālyālaṃkṛtāṃstūlikāgoṇikāstaraṇān dūṣyapaṭapratyāstīrṇān ubhayato lohitopadhānān śvetaiḥ prapāṇḍuraiḥ śīghrajavairgoṇairyojitān bahupuruṣaparigṛhītān | [SDhPS, 3 140.1]
savaijayantān gorathakāneva vātabalajavasampannān ekavarṇān ekavidhān ekaikasya dārakasya dadyāt | [SDhPS, 3 141.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 3 142.1]
tathā hi śāriputra sa puruṣa āḍhyaśca bhavenmahādhanaśca prabhūtakoṣṭhāgāraśca | [SDhPS, 3 142.2]
sa evaṃ manyeta | [SDhPS, 3 143.1]
alaṃ ma eṣāṃ kumārakāṇām anyair yānair dattairiti | [SDhPS, 3 143.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 3 144.1]
sarva evaite kumārakā mamaiva putrāḥ sarve ca me priyā manaāpāḥ | [SDhPS, 3 144.2]
saṃvidyante ca me imānyevaṃrūpāṇi mahāyānāni | [SDhPS, 3 145.1]
samaṃ ca mayaite kumārakāḥ sarve cintayitavyā na viṣamam | [SDhPS, 3 146.1]
ahamapi bahukośakoṣṭhāgāraḥ | [SDhPS, 3 147.1]
sarvasattvānāmapyahamimānyevaṃrūpāṇi mahāyānāni dadyāṃ kimaṅga punaḥ svakānāṃ putrāṇām | [SDhPS, 3 148.1]
te ca dārakāstasmin samaye teṣu mahāyāneṣvabhiruhya āścaryādbhutaprāptā bhaveyuḥ | [SDhPS, 3 149.1]
tatkiṃ manyase śāriputra mā haiva tasya puruṣasya mṛṣāvādaḥ syād yena teṣāṃ dārakāṇāṃ pūrvaṃ trīṇi yānānyupadarśayitvā paścātsarveṣāṃ mahāyānānyeva dattāny udārayānānyeva dattāni | [SDhPS, 3 150.1]
na hyetad bhagavan na hyetat sugata | [SDhPS, 3 151.1]
anenaiva tāvad bhagavan kāraṇena sa puruṣo na mṛṣāvādī bhaved yattena puruṣeṇopāyakauśalyena te dārakāstasmādādīptād gṛhānniṣkāsitā jīvitena ca abhicchāditāḥ | [SDhPS, 3 152.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 3 153.1]
ātmabhāvapratilambhenaiva bhagavan sarvakrīḍanakāni labdhāni bhavanti | [SDhPS, 3 153.2]
yadyapi tāvad bhagavan sa puruṣasteṣāṃ kumārakāṇāmekarathamapi na dadyāt tathāpi tāvad bhagavan sa puruṣo na mṛṣāvādī bhavet | [SDhPS, 3 154.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 3 155.1]
tathā hi bhagavaṃstena puruṣeṇa pūrvameva evamanuvicintitam | [SDhPS, 3 155.2]
upāyakauśalyena ahamimān kumārakāṃstasmānmahato duḥkhaskandhāt parimocayiṣyāmīti | [SDhPS, 3 155.3]
anenāpi bhagavan paryāyeṇa tasya puruṣasya na mṛṣāvādo bhavet | [SDhPS, 3 156.1]
kaḥ punarvādo yattena puruṣeṇa prabhūtakośakoṣṭhāgāramastīti kṛtvā putrapriyatāmeva manyamānena ślāghamānenaikavarṇānyekayānāni dattāni yaduta mahāyānāni | [SDhPS, 3 157.1]
nāsti bhagavaṃstasya puruṣasya mṛṣāvādaḥ | [SDhPS, 3 158.1]
evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat | [SDhPS, 3 159.1]
sādhu sādhu śāriputra | [SDhPS, 3 159.2]
evametacchāriputraivametad yathā vadasi | [SDhPS, 3 160.1]
evameva śāriputra tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ sarvabhayavinivṛttaḥ sarvopadravopāyāsopasargaduḥkhadaurmanasyāvidyāndhakāratamastimirapaṭalaparyavanāhebhyaḥ sarveṇa sarvaṃ sarvathā vipramuktaḥ | [SDhPS, 3 161.1]
tathāgato jñānabalavaiśāradyāveṇikabuddhadharmasamanvāgataḥ ṛddhibalenātibalavāṃllokapitā mahopāyakauśalyajñānaparamapāramitāprāpto mahākāruṇiko 'parikhinnamānaso hitaiṣī anukampakaḥ | [SDhPS, 3 162.1]
sa traidhātuke mahatā duḥkhadaurmanasyaskandhena ādīptajīrṇapaṭalaśaraṇaniveśanasadṛśa utpadyate sattvānāṃ jātijarāvyādhimaraṇaśokaparidevaduḥkhadaurmanasyopāyāsāvidyāndhakāratamastimirapaṭalaparyavanāhapratiṣṭhānāṃ rāgadveṣamohaparimocanahetor anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau samādāpanahetoḥ | [SDhPS, 3 163.1]
sa utpannaḥ samānaḥ paśyati sattvān dahyataḥ pacyamānāṃstapyamānān paritapyamānān jātijarāvyādhimaraṇaśokaparidevaduḥkhadaurmanasyopāyāsaiḥ paribhoganimittaṃ ca kāmahetunidānaṃ ca anekavidhāni duḥkhāni pratyanubhavanti | [SDhPS, 3 164.1]
dṛṣṭadhārmikaṃ ca paryeṣṭinidānaṃ parigrahanidānaṃ sāṃparāyikaṃ narakatiryagyoniyamalokeṣvanekavidhāni duḥkhāni pratyanubhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 3 165.1]
devamanuṣyadāridryam aniṣṭasaṃyogam iṣṭavinābhāvikāni ca duḥkhāni pratyanubhavanti | [SDhPS, 3 166.1]
tatraiva ca duḥkhaskandhe parivartamānāḥ krīḍanti ramante paricārayanti nottrasanti na saṃtrasanti na saṃtrāsamāpadyante na budhyante na cetayanti nodvijanti na niḥsaraṇaṃ paryeṣante | [SDhPS, 3 167.1]
tatraiva ca ādīptāgārasadṛśe traidhātuke 'bhiramanti tena tenaiva vidhāvanti | [SDhPS, 3 168.1]
tena ca mahatā duḥkhaskandhena abhyāhatā na duḥkhamanasikārasaṃjñām utpādayanti | [SDhPS, 3 169.1]
tatra śāriputra tathāgata evaṃ paśyati | [SDhPS, 3 170.1]
ahaṃ khalveṣāṃ sattvānāṃ pitā | [SDhPS, 3 170.2]
mayā hyete sattvā asmādevaṃrūpānmahato duḥkhaskandhāt parimocayitavyā mayā caiṣāṃ sattvānāmaprameyamacintyaṃ buddhajñānasukhaṃ dātavyaṃ yenaite sattvāḥ krīḍiṣyanti ramiṣyanti paricārayiṣyanti vikrīḍitāni ca kariṣyanti | [SDhPS, 3 171.1]
tatra śāriputra tathāgata evaṃ paśyati | [SDhPS, 3 172.1]
sacedahaṃ jñānabalo 'smīti kṛtvā ṛddhibalo 'smīti kṛtvā anupāyenaiṣāṃ sattvānāṃ tathāgatajñānabalavaiśāradyāni saṃśrāvayeyam | [SDhPS, 3 172.2]
naite sattvā ebhirdharmair niryāyeyuḥ | [SDhPS, 3 172.3]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 3 173.1]
adhyavasitā hyamī sattvāḥ pañcasu kāmaguṇeṣu traidhātukaratyām | [SDhPS, 3 173.2]
aparimuktā jātijarāvyādhimaraṇaśokaparidevaduḥkhadaurmanasyopāyāsebhyaḥ | [SDhPS, 3 174.1]
dahyante pacyante tapyante paritapyante | [SDhPS, 3 175.1]
anirdhāvitās traidhātukād ādīptajīrṇapaṭalaśaraṇaniveśanasadṛśāt kathamete buddhajñānaṃ paribhotsyante | [SDhPS, 3 176.1]
tatra śāriputra tathāgato yadyathāpi nāma sa puruṣo bāhubalikaḥ sthāpayitvā bāhubalam upāyakauśalyena tān kumārakāṃstasmād ādīptād agārānniṣkāsayet | [SDhPS, 3 177.1]
niṣkāsayitvā sa teṣāṃ paścādudārāṇi mahāyānāni dadyāt | [SDhPS, 3 177.2]
evameva śāriputra tathāgato 'pyarhan samyaksaṃbuddhas tathāgatajñānabalavaiśāradyasamanvāgataḥ sthāpayitvā tathāgatajñānabalavaiśāradyam upāyakauśalyajñānenādīptajīrṇapaṭalaśaraṇaniveśanasadṛśāt traidhātukāt sattvānāṃ niṣkāsanahetostrīṇi yānānyupadarśayati yaduta śrāvakayānaṃ pratyekabuddhayānaṃ bodhisattvayānamiti | [SDhPS, 3 177.3]
tribhiśca yānaiḥ sattvāṃllobhayati | [SDhPS, 3 178.1]
evaṃ caiṣāṃ vadati | [SDhPS, 3 178.2]
mā bhavanto 'sminnādīptāgārasadṛśe traidhātuke 'bhiramadhvaṃ hīneṣu rūpaśabdagandharasasparśeṣu | [SDhPS, 3 178.3]
atra hi yūyaṃ traidhātuke 'bhiratāḥ pañcakāmaguṇasahagatayā tṛṣṇayā dahyatha tapyatha paritapyatha | [SDhPS, 3 179.1]
nirdhāvadhvam asmāt traidhātukāt | [SDhPS, 3 180.1]
trīṇi yānānyanuprāpsyatha yadidaṃ śrāvakayānaṃ pratyekabuddhayānaṃ bodhisattvayānamiti | [SDhPS, 3 181.1]
ahaṃ vo 'tra sthāne pratibhūḥ | [SDhPS, 3 182.1]
ahaṃ vo dāsyāmyetāni trīṇi yānāni | [SDhPS, 3 183.1]
abhiyujyadhve traidhātukānniḥsaraṇahetoḥ | [SDhPS, 3 184.1]
evaṃ caitāṃllobhayāmi | [SDhPS, 3 185.1]
etāni bhoḥ sattvā yāni āryāṇi ca āryapraśastāni ca mahāramaṇīyakasamanvāgatāni ca | [SDhPS, 3 185.2]
akṛpaṇam etair bhavantaḥ krīḍiṣyatha ramiṣyatha paricārayiṣyatha | [SDhPS, 3 186.1]
indriyabalabodhyaṅgadhyānavimokṣasamādhisamāpattibhiśca mahatīṃ ratiṃ pratyanubhaviṣyatha | [SDhPS, 3 187.1]
mahatā ca sukhasaumanasyena samanvāgatā bhaviṣyatha | [SDhPS, 3 188.1]
tatra śāriputra ye sattvāḥ paṇḍitajātīyā bhavanti te tathāgatasya lokapitur abhiśraddadhanti | [SDhPS, 3 189.1]
abhiśraddadhitvā ca tathāgataśāsane 'bhiyujyante udyogamāpadyante | [SDhPS, 3 190.1]
tatra kecit sattvāḥ paraghoṣaśravānugamanam ākāṅkṣamāṇā ātmaparinirvāṇahetoś caturāryasatyānubodhāya tathāgataśāsane 'bhiyujyante | [SDhPS, 3 191.1]
te ucyante śrāvakayānamākāṅkṣamāṇāḥ traidhātukānnirdhāvanti | [SDhPS, 3 192.1]
tadyathāpi nāma tasmād ādīptād agārādanyatare dārakā mṛgarathamākāṅkṣamāṇā nirdhāvitāḥ | [SDhPS, 3 193.1]
anye sattvā anācāryakaṃ jñānaṃ damaśamathamākāṅkṣamāṇā ātmaparinirvāṇahetorhetupratyayānubodhāya tathāgataśāsane 'bhiyujyante | [SDhPS, 3 194.1]
te ucyante pratyekabuddhayānam ākāṅkṣamāṇās traidhātukānnirdhāvanti | [SDhPS, 3 194.2]
tadyathāpi nāma tasmād ādīptādagārādanyatare dārakā ajaratham ākāṅkṣamāṇā nirdhāvitāḥ | [SDhPS, 3 195.1]
apare punaḥ sattvāḥ sarvajñajñānaṃ buddhajñānaṃ svayaṃbhūjñānam anācāryakaṃ jñānamākāṅkṣamāṇā bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāyai mahato janakāyasyārthāya hitāya sukhāya devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca sarvasattvaparinirvāṇahetos tathāgatajñānabalavaiśāradyānubodhāya tathāgataśāsane 'bhiyujyante | [SDhPS, 3 196.1]
te ucyante mahāyānam ākāṅkṣamāṇās traidhātukānnirdhāvanti | [SDhPS, 3 197.1]
tena kāraṇenocyante bodhisattvā mahāsattvā iti | [SDhPS, 3 198.1]
tadyathāpi nāma tasmād ādīptādagārādanyatare dārakā gorathamākāṅkṣamāṇānirdhāvitāḥ | [SDhPS, 3 199.1]
tadyathāpi nāma śāriputra sa puruṣastān kumārakāṃstasmād ādīptādagārānnirdhāvitān dṛṣṭvā kṣemasvastibhyāṃ parimuktānabhayaprāptāniti viditvā ātmānaṃ ca mahādhanaṃ viditvā teṣāṃ dārakāṇāmekameva yānamudāramanuprayacchet | [SDhPS, 3 200.1]
evameva śāriputra tathāgato 'pyarhan samyaksaṃbuddho yadā paśyati | [SDhPS, 3 200.2]
anekāḥ sattvakoṭīstraidhātukāt parimuktā duḥkhabhayabhairavopadravaparimuktās tathāgataśāsanadvāreṇa nirdhāvitāḥ parimuktāḥ sarvabhayopadravakāntārebhyo nirvṛtisukhaprāptāḥ | [SDhPS, 3 200.3]
tānetān śāriputra tasmin samaye tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ prabhūto mahājñānabalavaiśāradyakośa iti viditvā sarve caite mamaiva putrā iti jñātvā buddhayānenaiva tān sattvān parinirvāpayati | [SDhPS, 3 201.1]
na ca kasyacit sattvasya pratyātmikaṃ parinirvāṇaṃ vadati | [SDhPS, 3 202.1]
sarvāṃśca tān sattvāṃstathāgataparinirvāṇena mahāparinirvāṇena parinirvāpayati | [SDhPS, 3 203.1]
ye cāpi te śāriputra sattvāstraidhātukāt parimuktā bhavanti teṣāṃ tathāgato dhyānavimokṣasamādhisamāpattīr āryāṇi paramasukhāni krīḍanakāni ramaṇīyakāni dadāti sarvāṇyetānyekavarṇāni | [SDhPS, 3 204.1]
tadyathāpi nāma śāriputra tasya puruṣasya na mṛṣāvādo bhaved yena trīṇi yānānyupadarśayitvā teṣāṃ kumārakāṇāmekameva mahāyānaṃ sarveṣāṃ dattaṃ saptaratnamayaṃ sarvālaṃkāravibhūṣitam ekavarṇameva udārayānameva sarveṣāmagrayānameva dattaṃ bhavet | [SDhPS, 3 205]
evameva śāriputra tathāgato 'pyarhan samyaksaṃbuddho na mṛṣāvādī bhavati yena pūrvamupāyakauśalyena trīṇi yānānyupadarśayitvā paścānmahāyānenaiva sattvān parinirvāpayati | [SDhPS, 3 206.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 3 207.1]
tathāgato hi śāriputra prabhūtajñānabalavaiśāradyakośakoṣṭhāgārasamanvāgataḥ pratibalaḥ sarvasattvānāṃ sarvajñajñānasahagataṃ dharmamupadarśayitum | [SDhPS, 3 207.2]
anenāpi śāriputra paryāyeṇaivaṃ veditavyaṃ yathā upāyakauśalyajñānābhinirhāraistathāgata ekameva mahāyānaṃ deśayati | [SDhPS, 3 208.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 3 209.1]
{SDhPS, 4}
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirāyuṣmāṃśca mahākātyāyanaḥ āyuṣmāṃśca mahākāśyapaḥ āyuṣmāṃśca mahāmaudgalyāyanaḥ imamevaṃrūpam aśrutapūrvaṃ dharmaṃ śrutvā bhagavato 'ntikāt saṃmukhamāyuṣmataśca śāriputrasya vyākaraṇaṃ śrutvā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau āścaryaprāptā adbhutaprāptā audbilyaprāptāstasyāṃ velāyāmutthāyāsanebhyo yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāman | [SDhPS, 4 1.1]
upasaṃkramya ekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇaṃ jānuṃ pṛthivyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yena bhagavāṃstenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantamabhimukham ullokayamānā avanatakāyā abhinatakāyāḥ praṇatakāyāstasyāṃ velāyāṃ bhagavantametadavocan | [SDhPS, 4 2.1]
vayaṃ hi bhagavan jīrṇā vṛddhā mahallakā asmin bhikṣusaṃghe sthavirasaṃmatā jarājīrṇībhūtā nirvāṇaprāptāḥ sma iti bhagavan nirudyamā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhāvapratibalāḥ smo 'prativīryārambhāḥ smaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 2.2]
yadāpi bhagavān dharmaṃ deśayati ciraṃ niṣaṇṇaśca bhagavān bhavati vayaṃ ca tasyāṃ dharmadeśanāyāṃ pratyupasthitā bhavāmas tadāpyasmākaṃ bhagavan ciraṃ niṣaṇṇānāṃ bhagavantaṃ ciraṃ paryupāsitānāmaṅgapratyaṅgāni duḥkhanti saṃdhivisaṃdhayaśca duḥkhanti | [SDhPS, 4 3.1]
tato vayaṃ bhagavan bhagavato dharmaṃ deśayamānasya śūnyatānimittāpraṇihitaṃ sarvamāviṣkurmaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 3.2]
nāsmābhireṣu buddhadharmeṣu buddhakṣetravyūheṣu vā bodhisattvavikrīḍiteṣu vā tathāgatavikrīḍiteṣu vā spṛhotpāditā | [SDhPS, 4 4.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 4 5.1]
yaccāsmādbhagavaṃstraidhātukānnirdhāvitā nirvāṇasaṃjñino vayaṃ ca jarājīrṇāḥ | [SDhPS, 4 5.2]
tato bhagavan asmābhirapyanye bodhisattvā avavaditā abhūvannanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhāv anuśiṣṭāśca | [SDhPS, 4 6.1]
na ca bhagavaṃstatrāsmābhirekamapi spṛhācittamutpāditamabhūt | [SDhPS, 4 7.1]
te vayaṃ bhagavannetarhi bhagavato 'ntikācchrāvakāṇāmapi vyākaraṇamanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau bhavatīti śrutvā āścaryādbhutaprāptā mahālābhaprāptāḥ smaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 8.1]
bhagavannadya sahasaivemamevaṃrūpam aśrutapūrvaṃ tathāgataghoṣaṃ śrutvā mahāratnapratilabdhāśca smaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 9.1]
bhagavan aprameyaratnapratilabdhāśca smaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 10.1]
bhagavan amārgitam aparyeṣṭam acintitam aprārthitaṃ cāsmābhirbhagavannidamevaṃ rūpaṃ mahāratnaṃ pratilabdham | [SDhPS, 4 11.1]
pratibhāti no bhagavan pratibhāti naḥ sugata | [SDhPS, 4 12.1]
tadyathāpi nāma bhagavan kaścideva puruṣaḥ piturantikādapakrāmet | [SDhPS, 4 13.1]
so 'pakramya anyataraṃ janapadapradeśaṃ gacchet | [SDhPS, 4 14.1]
sa tatra bahūni varṣāṇi vipravased viṃśatiṃ vā triṃśadvā catvāriṃśadvā pañcāśadvā | [SDhPS, 4 15.1]
atha sa bhagavan mahān puruṣo bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 16.1]
sa ca daridraḥ syāt | [SDhPS, 4 17.1]
sa ca vṛttiṃ paryeṣamāṇa āhāracīvarahetordiśo vidiśaḥ prakrāman anyataraṃ janapadapradeśaṃ gacchet | [SDhPS, 4 18.1]
tasya ca sa pitā anyatamaṃ janapadaṃ prakrāntaḥ syāt | [SDhPS, 4 19.1]
bahudhanadhānyahiraṇyakośakoṣṭhāgāraśca bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 20.1]
bahusuvarṇarūpyamaṇimuktāvaiḍūryaśaṅkhaśilāpravālajātarūparajatasamanvāgataśca bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 21.1]
bahudāsīdāsakarmakarapauruṣeyaśca bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 22.1]
bahuhastyaśvarathagaveḍakasamanvāgataśca bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 23.1]
mahāparivāraśca bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 24.1]
mahājanapadeṣu ca dhanikaḥ syāt | [SDhPS, 4 25.1]
āyogaprayogakṛṣivaṇijyaprabhūtaśca bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 26.1]
atha khalu bhagavan sa daridrapuruṣa āhāracīvaraparyeṣṭihetor grāmanagaranigamajanapadarāṣṭrarājadhānīṣu paryaṭamāno 'nupūrveṇa yatrāsau puruṣo bahudhanahiraṇyasuvarṇakośakoṣṭhāgāras tasyaiva pitā vasati tannagaramanuprāpto bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 27.1]
atha khalu bhagavan sa daridrapuruṣasya pitā bahudhanahiraṇyakośakoṣṭhāgāras tasmin nagare vasamānastaṃ pañcāśadvarṣanaṣṭaṃ putraṃ satatasamitamanusmaret | [SDhPS, 4 28.1]
samanusmaramāṇaśca na kasyacid ācakṣed anyatraika evātmanādhyātmaṃ saṃtapyet | [SDhPS, 4 29.1]
evaṃ ca cintayet | [SDhPS, 4 29.2]
ahamasmi jīrṇo vṛddho mahallakaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 29.3]
prabhūtaṃ me hiraṇyasuvarṇadhanadhānyakośakoṣṭhāgāraṃ saṃvidyate | [SDhPS, 4 30.1]
na ca me putraḥ kaścidasti | [SDhPS, 4 31.1]
mā haiva mama kālakriyā bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 32.1]
sarvamidam aparibhuktaṃ vinaśyet | [SDhPS, 4 33.1]
sa taṃ punaḥ punaḥ putramanusmaret | [SDhPS, 4 34.1]
aho nāmāhaṃ nirvṛtiprāpto bhaveyaṃ yadi me sa putra imaṃ dhanaskandhaṃ paribhuñjīta | [SDhPS, 4 34.2]
atha khalu bhagavan sa daridrapuruṣa āhāracīvaraṃ paryeṣamāṇo 'nupūrveṇa yena tasya prabhūtahiraṇyasuvarṇadhanadhānyakośakoṣṭhāgārasya samṛddhasya puruṣasya niveśanaṃ tenopasaṃkrāmet | [SDhPS, 4 35.1]
atha khalu bhagavan sa tasya daridrapuruṣasya pitā svake niveśanadvāre mahatyā brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviṭśūdrapariṣadā parivṛtaḥ puraskṛto mahāsiṃhāsane sapādapīṭhe suvarṇarūpyapratimaṇḍite upaviṣṭo hiraṇyakoṭīśatasahasrairvyavahāraṃ kurvan vālavyajanena vījyamāno vitatavitāne pṛthivīpradeśe muktakusumābhikīrṇe ratnadāmābhipralambite mahatyarddhyopaviṣṭaḥ syāt | [SDhPS, 4 36.1]
adrākṣīt sa bhagavan daridrapuruṣastaṃ svakaṃ pitaraṃ svake niveśanadvāre evaṃrūpayā ṛddhyā upaviṣṭaṃ mahatā janakāyena parivṛtaṃ gṛhapatikṛtyaṃ kurvāṇam | [SDhPS, 4 37.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punarbhītastrastaḥ saṃvignaḥ saṃhṛṣṭaromakūpajātaḥ udvignamānasaḥ evam anuvicintayāmāsa | [SDhPS, 4 38.1]
sahasaivāyaṃ mayā rājā vā rājamātro vā āsāditaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 38.2]
nāstyasmākamiha kiṃcit karma | [SDhPS, 4 39.1]
gacchāmo vayaṃ yena daridravīthī tatrāsmākamāhāracīvaramalpakṛcchreṇaiva utpatsyate | [SDhPS, 4 40.1]
alaṃ me ciraṃ vilambitena | [SDhPS, 4 41.1]
mā haivāhamiha vaiṣṭiko vā gṛhyeyānyataraṃ vā doṣamanuprāpnuyām | [SDhPS, 4 42.1]
atha khalu bhagavan sa daridrapuruṣo duḥkhaparaṃparāmanasikārabhayabhītastvaramāṇaḥ prakrāmet palāyet | [SDhPS, 4 43.1]
na tatra saṃtiṣṭhet | [SDhPS, 4 43.2]
atha khalu bhagavan sa āḍhyaḥ puruṣaḥ svake niveśanadvāre siṃhāsane upaviṣṭastaṃ svakaṃ putraṃ sahadarśanenaiva pratyabhijānīyāt | [SDhPS, 4 44.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punastuṣṭa udagra āttamanaskaḥ pramuditaḥ prītisaumanasyajāto bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 45.1]
evaṃ ca cintayet | [SDhPS, 4 45.2]
āścaryaṃ yāvad yatra hi nāma asya mahato hiraṇyasuvarṇadhanadhānyakośakoṣṭhāgārasya paribhoktā upalabdhaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 45.3]
ahaṃ caitameva punaḥ punaḥ samanusmarāmi | [SDhPS, 4 46.1]
ayaṃ ca svayamevehāgataḥ | [SDhPS, 4 47.1]
ahaṃ ca jīrṇo vṛddho mahallakaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 48.1]
atha khalu bhagavan sa puruṣaḥ putratṛṣṇāsaṃpīḍitastasmin kṣaṇalavamuhūrte javanān puruṣān saṃpreṣayet | [SDhPS, 4 49.1]
gacchata mārṣā etaṃ puruṣaṃ śīghramānayadhvam | [SDhPS, 4 49.2]
atha khalu bhagavaṃste puruṣāḥ sarva eva javena pradhāvitāstaṃ daridrapuruṣam adhyālambeyuḥ | [SDhPS, 4 50.1]
atha khalu daridrapuruṣastasyāṃ velāyāṃ bhītastrastaḥ saṃvignaḥ saṃhṛṣṭaromakūpajātaḥ udvignamānaso dāruṇamārtasvaraṃ muñced āraved viravet | [SDhPS, 4 51.1]
nāhaṃ yuṣmākaṃ kiṃcidaparādhyāmīti vācaṃ bhāṣeta | [SDhPS, 4 52.1]
atha khalu te puruṣā balātkāreṇa taṃ daridrapuruṣaṃ viravantamapyākarṣeyuḥ | [SDhPS, 4 53.1]
atha khalu sa daridrapuruṣo bhītastrastaḥ saṃvigna udvignamānasa evaṃ ca cintayet | [SDhPS, 4 54.1]
mā tāvadahaṃ vadhyo daṇḍyo bhaveyam | [SDhPS, 4 54.2]
naśyāmīti | [SDhPS, 4 55.1]
sa mūrchito dharaṇyāṃ prapatet | [SDhPS, 4 56.1]
visaṃjñaśca syāt | [SDhPS, 4 56.2]
āsanne cāsya sa pitā bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 57.1]
sa tān puruṣānevaṃ vadet | [SDhPS, 4 58.1]
mā bhavanta etaṃ puruṣamānayantviti | [SDhPS, 4 58.2]
tamenaṃ śītalena vāriṇā parisiñcitvā na bhūya ālapet | [SDhPS, 4 59.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 4 60.1]
jānāti sa gṛhapatistasya daridrapuruṣasya hīnādhimuktikatām ātmanaś codārasthāmatām | [SDhPS, 4 60.2]
jānīte ca mamaiṣa putra iti | [SDhPS, 4 61.1]
atha khalu bhagavan sa gṛhapatirupāyakauśalyena na kasyacidācakṣet | [SDhPS, 4 62.1]
mamaiṣa putra iti | [SDhPS, 4 62.2]
atha khalu bhagavan sa gṛhapatiranyataraṃ puruṣamāmantrayet | [SDhPS, 4 63.1]
gaccha tvaṃ bhoḥ puruṣa | [SDhPS, 4 63.2]
enaṃ daridrapuruṣamevaṃ vadasva | [SDhPS, 4 64.1]
gaccha tvaṃ bhoḥ puruṣa yenākāṅkṣasi | [SDhPS, 4 64.2]
mukto 'si | [SDhPS, 4 65.1]
evaṃ vadati sa puruṣastasmai pratiśrutya yena sa daridrapuruṣastenopasaṃkrāmet | [SDhPS, 4 66.1]
upasaṃkramya taṃ daridrapuruṣamevaṃ vadet | [SDhPS, 4 67.1]
gaccha tvaṃ bhoḥ puruṣa yenākāṅkṣasi | [SDhPS, 4 67.2]
mukto 'sīti | [SDhPS, 4 68.1]
atha khalu sa daridrapuruṣa idaṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā āścaryādbhutaprāpto bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 69.1]
sa utthāya tasmāt pṛthivīpradeśādyena daridravīthī tenopasaṃkrāmedāhāracīvaraparyeṣṭihetoḥ | [SDhPS, 4 70.1]
atha khalu sa gṛhapatistasya daridrapuruṣasyākarṣaṇahetorupāyakauśalyaṃ prayojayet | [SDhPS, 4 71.1]
sa tatra dvau puruṣau prayojayet durvarṇāvalpaujaskau | [SDhPS, 4 72.1]
gacchatāṃ bhavantau yo 'sau puruṣa ihāgato 'bhūt taṃ yuvāṃ dviguṇayā divasamudrayā ātmavacanenaiva bharayitveha mama niveśane karma kārāpayethām | [SDhPS, 4 72.2]
sacet sa evaṃ vadet | [SDhPS, 4 73.1]
kiṃ karma kartavyamiti sa yuvābhyāmevaṃ vaktavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 73.2]
saṃkāradhānaṃ śodhayitavyaṃ sahāvābhyāmiti | [SDhPS, 4 73.3]
atha tau puruṣau taṃ daridrapuruṣaṃ paryeṣayitvā tayā kriyayā saṃpādayetām | [SDhPS, 4 74.1]
atha khalu tau dvau puruṣau sa ca daridrapuruṣo vetanaṃ gṛhītvā tasya mahādhanasya puruṣasyāntikāttasminneva niveśane saṃkāradhānaṃ śodhayeyuḥ | [SDhPS, 4 75.1]
tasyaiva ca mahādhanasya puruṣasya gṛhaparisare kaṭapalikuñcikāyāṃ vāsaṃ kalpayeyuḥ | [SDhPS, 4 76.1]
sa cāḍhyaḥ puruṣo gavākṣavātāyanena taṃ svakaṃ putraṃ paśyet saṃkāradhānaṃ śodhayamānam | [SDhPS, 4 77.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punarāścaryaprāpto bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 78.1]
atha khalu sa gṛhapatiḥ svakānniveśanādavatīrya apanayitvā mālyābharaṇāny apanayitvā mṛdukāni vastrāṇi caukṣāṇyudārāṇi malināni vastrāṇi prāvṛtya dakṣiṇena pāṇinā piṭakaṃ parigṛhya pāṃsunā svagātraṃ dūṣayitvā dūrata eva sambhāṣamāṇo yena sa daridrapuruṣastenopasaṃkrāmet | [SDhPS, 4 79.1]
upasaṃkramyaivaṃ vadet | [SDhPS, 4 80.1]
vahantu bhavantaḥ piṭakāni mā tiṣṭhata harata pāṃsūni | [SDhPS, 4 80.2]
anenopāyena taṃ putramālapet saṃlapecca | [SDhPS, 4 81.1]
enaṃ vadet | [SDhPS, 4 82.1]
ihaiva tvaṃ bhoḥ puruṣa karma kuruṣva | [SDhPS, 4 82.2]
mā bhūyo 'nyatra gamiṣyasi | [SDhPS, 4 83.1]
saviśeṣaṃ te 'haṃ vetanakaṃ dāsyāmi | [SDhPS, 4 84.1]
yena yena ca te kāryaṃ bhavet tadviśrabdhaṃ māṃ yācer yadi vā kuṇḍamūlyena yadi vā kuṇḍikāmūlyena yadi vā sthālikāmūlyena yadi vā kāṣṭhamūlyena yadi vā lavaṇamūlyena yadi vā bhojanena yadi vā prāvaraṇena | [SDhPS, 4 85.1]
asti me bhoḥ puruṣa jīrṇaśāṭī | [SDhPS, 4 86.1]
sacettayā te kāryaṃ syād yācer ahaṃ te 'nupradāsyāmi | [SDhPS, 4 87.1]
yena yena te bhoḥ puruṣa kāryamevaṃrūpeṇa pariṣkāreṇa taṃ tamevāhaṃ te sarvamanupradāsyāmi | [SDhPS, 4 88.1]
nirvṛtastvaṃ bhoḥ puruṣa bhava | [SDhPS, 4 89.1]
yādṛśaste pitā tādṛśaste 'haṃ mantavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 90.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 4 91.1]
ahaṃ ca vṛddhaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 91.2]
tvaṃ ca daharaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 91.3]
mama ca tvayā bahu karma kṛtamimaṃ saṃkāradhānaṃ śodhayatā | [SDhPS, 4 92.1]
na ca tvayā bhoḥ puruṣa atra karma kurvatā śāṭhyaṃ vā vakratā vā kauṭilyaṃ vā māno vā mrakṣo vā kṛtapūrvaḥ karoṣi vā | [SDhPS, 4 93.1]
sarvathā te bhoḥ puruṣa na samanupaśyāmyekamapi pāpakarma yathaiṣāmanyeṣāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ karma kurvatāmime doṣāḥ saṃvidyante | [SDhPS, 4 94.1]
yādṛśo me putra aurasas tādṛśastvaṃ mama adyāgreṇa bhavasi | [SDhPS, 4 95.1]
atha khalu bhagavan sa gṛhapatistasya daridrapuruṣasya putra iti nāma kuryāt | [SDhPS, 4 96.1]
sa ca daridrapuruṣastasya gṛhapaterantike pitṛsaṃjñāmutpādayet | [SDhPS, 4 97.1]
anena bhagavan paryāyeṇa sa gṛhapatiḥ putrakāmatṛṣito viṃśativarṣāṇi taṃ putraṃ saṃkāradhānaṃ śodhāpayet | [SDhPS, 4 98.1]
atha viṃśatervarṣāṇāmatyayena sa daridrapuruṣastasya gṛhapaterniveśane viśrabdho bhavenniṣkramaṇapraveśe tatraiva ca kaṭapalikuñcikāyāṃ vāsaṃ kalpayet | [SDhPS, 4 99.1]
atha khalu bhagavaṃstasya gṛhapaterglānyaṃ pratyupasthitaṃ bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 100.1]
sa maraṇakālasamayaṃ ca ātmanaḥ pratyupasthitaṃ samanupaśyet | [SDhPS, 4 101.1]
sa taṃ daridrapuruṣamevaṃ vadet | [SDhPS, 4 102.1]
āgaccha tvaṃ bhoḥ puruṣa | [SDhPS, 4 102.2]
idaṃ mama prabhūtaṃ hiraṇyasuvarṇadhanadhānyakośakoṣṭhāgāramasti | [SDhPS, 4 103.1]
ahaṃ bāḍhaglānaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 104.1]
icchāmyetaṃ yasya dātavyaṃ yataśca grahītavyaṃ yacca nidhātavyaṃ bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 105.1]
sarvaṃ saṃjānīyāḥ | [SDhPS, 4 105.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 4 106.1]
yādṛśa eva ahamasya dravyasya svāmī tādṛśastvamapi | [SDhPS, 4 106.2]
mā ca me tvaṃ kiṃcidato vipraṇāśayiṣyasi | [SDhPS, 4 107.1]
atha khalu bhagavan sa daridrapuruṣo 'nena paryāyeṇa tacca tasya gṛhapateḥ prabhūtaṃ hiraṇyasuvarṇadhanadhānyakośakoṣṭhāgāraṃ saṃjānīyāt | [SDhPS, 4 108.1]
ātmanā ca tato niḥspṛho bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 109.1]
na ca tasmāt kiṃcit prārthayed antaśaḥ saktuprasthamūlyamātramapi | [SDhPS, 4 110.1]
tatraiva ca kaṭapalikuñcikāyāṃ vāsaṃ kalpayet tāmeva daridracintāmanuvicintayamānaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 111.1]
atha khalu bhagavan sa gṛhapatistaṃ putraṃ śaktaṃ paripālakaṃ paripakvaṃ viditvā avamarditacittamudārasaṃjñayā ca paurvikayā daridracintayā ārtīyantaṃ jehrīyamāṇaṃ jugupsamānaṃ viditvā maraṇakālasamaye pratyupasthite taṃ daridrapuruṣamānāyya mahato jñātisaṃghasyopanāmayitvā rājño vā rājamātrasya vā purato naigamajānapadānāṃ ca saṃmukhamevaṃ saṃśrāvayet | [SDhPS, 4 112.1]
śṛṇvantu bhavantaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 112.2]
ayaṃ mama putra auraso mayaiva janitaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 112.3]
amukaṃ nāma nagaram | [SDhPS, 4 113.1]
tasmādeṣa pañcāśadvarṣo naṣṭaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 114.1]
amuko nāmaiṣa nāmnā | [SDhPS, 4 115.1]
ahamapyamuko nāma | [SDhPS, 4 116.1]
tataścāhaṃ nagarādetameva mārgamāṇa ihāgataḥ | [SDhPS, 4 117.1]
eṣa mama putraḥ | [SDhPS, 4 118.1]
ahamasya pitā | [SDhPS, 4 118.2]
yaḥ kaścinmamopabhogo 'sti taṃ sarvamasmai puruṣāya niryātayāmi | [SDhPS, 4 119.1]
yacca me kiṃcidasti pratyātmakaṃ dhanaṃ tatsarvameṣa eva jānāti | [SDhPS, 4 120]
atha khalu bhagavan sa daridrapuruṣastasmin samaye imamevaṃrūpaṃ ghoṣaṃ śrutvā āścaryādbhutaprāpto bhavet | [SDhPS, 4 121.1]
evaṃ ca vicintayet | [SDhPS, 4 122.1]
sahasaiva mayedameva tāvaddhiraṇyasuvarṇadhanadhānyakośakoṣṭhāgāraṃ pratilabdhamiti | [SDhPS, 4 122.2]
evameva bhagavan vayaṃ tathāgatasya putrapratirūpakāḥ | [SDhPS, 4 123.1]
tathāgataśca asmākamevaṃ vadati | [SDhPS, 4 124.1]
putrā mama yūyamiti yathā sa gṛhapatiḥ | [SDhPS, 4 124.2]
vayaṃ ca bhagavaṃstisṛbhirduḥkhatābhiḥ saṃpīḍitā abhūma | [SDhPS, 4 125.1]
katamābhistisṛbhiḥ | [SDhPS, 4 126.1]
yaduta duḥkhaduḥkhatayā saṃskāraduḥkhatayā vipariṇāmaduḥkhatayā ca | [SDhPS, 4 126.2]
saṃsāre ca hīnādhimuktikāḥ | [SDhPS, 4 127.1]
tato vayaṃ bhagavatā bahūn dharmān pratyavarān saṃkāradhānasadṛśān anuvicintayitāḥ | [SDhPS, 4 128.1]
teṣu cāsma prayuktā ghaṭamānā vyāyacchamānāḥ | [SDhPS, 4 129.1]
nirvāṇamātraṃ ca vayaṃ bhagavan divasamudrāmiva paryeṣamāṇā mārgāmaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 130.1]
tena ca vayaṃ bhagavan nirvāṇena pratilabdhena tuṣṭā bhavāmaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 131.1]
bahu ca labdham iti manyāmahe tathāgatasyāntikāt eṣu dharmeṣvabhiyuktā ghaṭitvā vyāyamitvā | [SDhPS, 4 132.1]
prajānāti ca tathāgato 'smākaṃ hīnādhimuktikatāṃ tataśca bhagavānasmānupekṣate na sambhinatti nācaṣṭe | [SDhPS, 4 133.1]
yo 'yaṃ tathāgatasya jñānakośa eṣa eva yuṣmākaṃ bhaviṣyatīti | [SDhPS, 4 133.2]
bhagavāṃścāsmākamupāyakauśalyena asmiṃstathāgatajñānakośe dāyādān saṃsthāpayati | [SDhPS, 4 134.1]
niḥspṛhāśca vayaṃ bhagavan | [SDhPS, 4 135.1]
tata evaṃ jānīma | [SDhPS, 4 136.1]
etadevāsmākaṃ bahukaraṃ yadvayaṃ tathāgatasyāntikāddivasamudrāmiva nirvāṇaṃ pratilabhāmahe | [SDhPS, 4 136.2]
te vayaṃ bhagavan bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāṃ tathāgatajñānadarśanamārabhya udārāṃ dharmadeśanāṃ kurmaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 137.1]
tathāgatajñānaṃ vivarāmo darśayāma upadarśayāmaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 138.1]
vayaṃ bhagavaṃstato niḥspṛhāḥ samānāḥ | [SDhPS, 4 139.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 4 140.1]
upāyakauśalyena tathāgato 'smākamadhimuktiṃ prajānāti | [SDhPS, 4 140.2]
tacca vayaṃ na jānīmo na budhyāmahe yadidaṃ bhagavatā etarhi kathitam | [SDhPS, 4 141.1]
yathā vayaṃ bhagavato bhūtāḥ putrā bhagavāṃścāsmākaṃ smārayati tathāgatajñānadāyādān | [SDhPS, 4 141.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 4 142.1]
yathāpi nāma vayaṃ tathāgatasya bhūtāḥ putrāḥ ity api tu khalu punarhīnādhimuktāḥ | [SDhPS, 4 142.2]
saced bhagavānasmākaṃ paśyedadhimuktibalaṃ bodhisattvaśabdaṃ bhagavānasmākamudāharet | [SDhPS, 4 143.1]
vayaṃ punarbhagavatā dve kārye kārāpitāḥ | [SDhPS, 4 144.1]
bodhisattvānāṃ cāgrato hīnādhimuktikā ityuktāḥ | [SDhPS, 4 144.2]
te codārāyāṃ buddhabodhau samādāpitāḥ | [SDhPS, 4 144.3]
asmākaṃ cedānīṃ bhagavānadhimuktibalaṃ jñātvā idamudāhṛtavān | [SDhPS, 4 144.4]
anena vayaṃ bhagavan paryāyeṇaivaṃ vadāmaḥ | [SDhPS, 4 145.1]
sahasaivāsmābhir niḥspṛhair ākāṅkṣitam amārgitam aparyeṣitam acintitam aprārthitaṃ sarvajñatāratnaṃ pratilabdhaṃ yathāpīdaṃ tathāgatasya putraiḥ | [SDhPS, 4 145.2]
atha khalvāyuṣmān mahākāśyapastasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣat | [SDhPS, 4 146.1]
{SDhPS, 5}
atha khalu bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ mahākāśyapaṃ tāṃścānyān sthavirān mahāśrāvakān āmantrayāmāsa | [SDhPS, 5 1.1]
sādhu sādhu mahākāśyapa | [SDhPS, 5 1.2]
sādhu khalu punaryuṣmākaṃ kāśyapa yadyūyaṃ tathāgatasya bhūtān guṇavarṇān bhāṣadhve | [SDhPS, 5 2.1]
ete ca kāśyapa tathāgatasya bhūtā guṇāḥ | [SDhPS, 5 3.1]
ataścānye 'prameyā asaṃkhyeyā yeṣāṃ na sukaraḥ paryanto 'dhigantumaparimitānapi kalpān bhāṣamāṇaiḥ | [SDhPS, 5 4.1]
dharmasvāmī kāśyapa tathāgataḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ rājā prabhurvaśī | [SDhPS, 5 5.1]
yaṃ ca kāśyapa tathāgato dharmaṃ yatropanikṣipati sa tathaiva bhavati | [SDhPS, 5 6.1]
sarvadharmāṃśca kāśyapa tathāgato yuktyopanikṣipati | [SDhPS, 5 7.1]
tathāgatajñānenopanikṣipati | [SDhPS, 5 8.1]
yathā te dharmāḥ sarvajñabhūmimeva gacchanti | [SDhPS, 5 9.1]
sarvadharmārthagatiṃ ca tathāgato vyavalokayati | [SDhPS, 5 10.1]
sarvadharmārthavaśitāprāptaḥ sarvadharmādhyāśayaprāptaḥ sarvadharmaviniścayakauśalyajñānaparamapāramitāprāptaḥ sarvajñajñānasaṃdarśakaḥ sarvajñajñānāvatārakaḥ sarvajñajñānopanikṣepakaḥ kāśyapa tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ | [SDhPS, 5 11.1]
tadyathāpi nāma kāśyapa asyāṃ trisāhasramahāsāhasrāyāṃ lokadhātau yāvantastṛṇagulmauṣadhivanaspatayo nānāvarṇā nānāprakārā oṣadhigrāmā nānānāmadheyāḥ pṛthivyāṃ jātāḥ parvatagirikandareṣu vā | [SDhPS, 5 12.1]
meghaśca mahāvāriparipūrṇa unnamed unnamitvā sarvāvatīṃ trisāhasramahāsāhasrāṃ lokadhātuṃ saṃchādayet | [SDhPS, 5 13.1]
saṃchādya ca sarvatra samakālaṃ vāri pramuñcet | [SDhPS, 5 14.1]
tatra kāśyapa ye tṛṇagulmauṣadhivanaspatayo 'syāṃ trisāhasramahāsāhasralokadhātau tatra ye taruṇāḥ komalanālaśākhāpatrapalāśās tṛṇagulmauṣadhivanaspatayo drumā mahādrumāḥ sarve te tato mahāmeghapramuktādvāriṇo yathābalaṃ yathāviṣayam abdhātuṃ pratyāpibanti | [SDhPS, 5 15.1]
te caikarasena vāriṇā prabhūtena meghapramuktena yathābījamanvayaṃ vivṛddhiṃ virūḍhiṃ vipulatāmāpadyante tathā ca puṣpaphalāni prasavanti | [SDhPS, 5 16.1]
te ca pṛthak pṛthaṅ nānānāmadheyāni pratilabhante | [SDhPS, 5 17.1]
ekadharaṇīpratiṣṭhitāśca te sarve oṣadhigrāmā bījagrāmā ekarasatoyābhiṣyanditāḥ | [SDhPS, 5 18.1]
evameva kāśyapa tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loka utpadyate | [SDhPS, 5 19.1]
yathā mahāmeghaḥ unnamate tathā tathāgato 'pyutpadya sarvāvantaṃ sadevamānuṣāsuraṃ lokaṃ svareṇābhivijñāpayati | [SDhPS, 5 20.1]
tadyathāpi nāma kāśyapa mahāmeghaḥ sarvāvatīṃ trisāhasramahāsāhasrāṃ lokadhātumavacchādayaty evameva kāśyapa tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ sadevamānuṣāsurasya lokasya purata evaṃ śabdamudīrayati ghoṣamanuśrāvayati | [SDhPS, 5 21.1]
tathāgato 'smi bhavanto devamanuṣyāḥ arhan samyaksaṃbuddhas tīrṇastārayāmi mukto mocayāmy āśvasta āśvāsayāmi parinirvṛtaḥ parinirvāpayāmi | [SDhPS, 5 21.2]
ahamimaṃ ca lokaṃ paraṃ ca lokaṃ samyak prajñayā yathābhūtaṃ prajānāmi sarvajñaḥ sarvadarśī | [SDhPS, 5 22.1]
upasaṃkrāmantu māṃ bhavanto devamanuṣyā dharmaśravaṇāya | [SDhPS, 5 23.1]
ahaṃ mārgasyākhyātā mārgadeśiko mārgavit mārgakovidaḥ | [SDhPS, 5 24.1]
tatra kāśyapa bahūni prāṇikoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi tathāgatasya dharmaśravaṇāyopasaṃkrāmanti | [SDhPS, 5 25.1]
atha tathāgato 'pi teṣāṃ sattvānām indriyavīryaparāparavaimātratāṃ jñātvā tāṃstān dharmaparyāyānupasaṃharati tāṃ tāṃ dharmakathāṃ kathayati bahvīṃ vicitrāṃ harṣaṇīyāṃ paritoṣaṇīyāṃ prāmodyakaraṇīyāṃ hitasukhasaṃvartanakaraṇīyām | [SDhPS, 5 26.1]
yayā kathayā te sattvāḥ dṛṣṭa eva dharme sukhitā bhavanti kālaṃ ca kṛtvā sugatīṣūpapadyante yatra prabhūtāṃśca kāmān paribhuñjante dharmaṃ ca śṛṇvanti | [SDhPS, 5 27.1]
śrutvā ca taṃ dharmaṃ vigatanīvaraṇā bhavanti | [SDhPS, 5 28.1]
anupūrveṇa ca sarvajñadharmeṣvabhiyujyante yathābalaṃ yathāviṣayaṃ yathāsthānam | [SDhPS, 5 29.1]
tadyathāpi nāma kāśyapa mahāmeghaḥ sarvāvatīṃ trisāhasramahāsāhasrāṃ lokadhātuṃ saṃchādya samaṃ vāri pramuñcati sarvāṃśca tṛṇagulmauṣadhivanaspatīn vāriṇā saṃtarpayati | [SDhPS, 5 30.1]
yathābalaṃ yathāviṣayaṃ yathāsthāmaṃ ca te tṛṇagulmauṣadhivanaspatayo vāryāpibanti svakasvakāṃ ca jātipramāṇatāṃ gacchanti | [SDhPS, 5 31.1]
evameva kāśyapa tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho yaṃ dharmaṃ bhāṣate sarvaḥ sa dharma ekaraso yaduta vimuktiraso virāgaraso nirodharasaḥ sarvajñajñānaparyavasānaḥ | [SDhPS, 5 32.1]
tatra kāśyapa ye te sattvāstathāgatasya dharmaṃ bhāṣamāṇasya śṛṇvanti dhārayanti abhisaṃyujyante na te ātmanātmānaṃ jānanti vā vedayanti vā budhyanti vā | [SDhPS, 5 33.1]
