tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 5 34.1]
tathāgata eva kāśyapa tān sattvāṃstathā jānāti ye ca te yathā ca te yādṛśāśca te | [SDhPS, 5 34.2]
yaṃ ca te cintayanti yathā ca te cintayanti yena ca te cintayanti | [SDhPS, 5 35.1]
yaṃ ca te bhāvayanti yathā ca te bhāvayanti yena ca te bhāvayanti | [SDhPS, 5 36.1]
yaṃ ca te prāpnuvanti yathā ca te prāpnuvanti yena ca te prāpnuvanti | [SDhPS, 5 37.1]
tathāgata eva kāśyapa tatra pratyakṣaḥ pratyakṣadarśī yathā ca darśī teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ tāsu tāsu bhūmiṣu sthitānāṃ tṛṇagulmauṣadhivanaspatīnāṃ hīnotkṛṣṭamadhyamānām | [SDhPS, 5 38.1]
so 'haṃ kāśyapa ekarasadharmaṃ viditvā yaduta vimuktirasaṃ nirvṛtirasaṃ nirvāṇaparyavasānaṃ nityaparinirvṛtamekabhūmikamākāśagatikamadhimuktiṃ sattvānām anurakṣamāṇo na sahasaiva sarvajñajñānaṃ saṃprakāśayāmi | [SDhPS, 5 39.1]
āścaryaprāptā adbhutaprāptā yūyaṃ kāśyapa yadyūyaṃ saṃdhābhāṣitaṃ tathāgatasya na śaknutha avataritum | [SDhPS, 5 40.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 5 41.1]
durvijñeyaṃ kāśyapa tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāṃ saṃdhābhāṣitamiti | [SDhPS, 5 41.2]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimamevārthaṃ bhūyasyā mātrayā saṃdarśayamāna imā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 5 42.1]
punaraparaṃ kāśyapa tathāgataḥ sattvavinaye samo na cāsamaḥ | [SDhPS, 5 87.1]
tadyathā kāśyapa candrasūryaprabhā sarvalokamavabhāsayati kuśalakāriṇam akuśalakāriṇaṃ cordhvāvasthitamadharāvasthitaṃ ca sugandhi durgandhi sā sarvatra samaṃ prabhā nipatati na viṣamam evameva kāśyapa tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāṃ sarvajñajñānacittaprabhā sarveṣu pañcagatyupapanneṣu sattveṣu yathādhimuktiṃ mahāyānikapratyekabuddhayānikaśrāvakayānikeṣu saddharmadeśanā samaṃ pravartate | [SDhPS, 5 88.1]
na ca tathāgatasya jñānaprabhāyā ūnatā vā atiriktatā vā yathāpuṇyajñānasamudāgamāya sambhavati | [SDhPS, 5 89.1]
na santi kāśyapa trīṇi yānāni | [SDhPS, 5 90.1]
kevalamanyonyacaritāḥ sattvāḥ | [SDhPS, 5 91.1]

evameva kāśyapa ekamevedaṃ yānaṃ yaduta buddhayānam | [SDhPS, 5 94.1]

evamukte āyuṣmān mahākāśyapo bhagavantametadavocat | [SDhPS, 5 96.1]

te na śakyaṃ tvayā jñātum abhimānaḥ kuto 'sti te | [SDhPS, 5 199.2]
krośamātre 'pi gantavye padavīṃ na vinā gatiḥ | [SDhPS, 5 200.1]
mātuḥ kukṣau ca yadvṛttaṃ vismṛtaṃ tattadeva te | [SDhPS, 5 200.2]
abhijñā yasya pañcaitāḥ sa sarvajña ihocyate | [SDhPS, 5 201.1]
tvaṃ mohād apyakiṃcijjñaḥ sarvajño 'smīti bhāṣase | [SDhPS, 5 201.2]
sarvajñatvaṃ prārthayase yadyabhijñābhinirhareḥ | [SDhPS, 5 202.1]
taṃ cābhijñābhinirhāramaraṇyastho vicintaya | [SDhPS, 5 202.2]
dharmaṃ viśuddhaṃ tena tvamabhijñāḥ pratilapsyase | [SDhPS, 5 202.3]
so 'rthaṃ gṛhya gato 'raṇyaṃ cintayet susamāhitaḥ | [SDhPS, 5 203.1]
abhijñāḥ prāptavān pañca nacireṇa guṇānvitaḥ | [SDhPS, 5 203.2]
tathaiva śrāvakāḥ sarve prāptanirvāṇasaṃjñinaḥ | [SDhPS, 5 204.1]
jino 'tha deśayettasmai viśrāmo 'yaṃ na nirvṛtiḥ | [SDhPS, 5 204.2]
upāya eṣa buddhānāṃ vadanti yadimaṃ nayam | [SDhPS, 5 205.1]
sarvajñatvamṛte nāsti nirvāṇaṃ tatsamārabha | [SDhPS, 5 205.2]
tryadhvajñānamanantaṃ ca ṣaṭ ca pāramitāḥ śubhāḥ | [SDhPS, 5 206.1]
śūnyatāmanimittaṃ ca praṇidhānavivarjitam | [SDhPS, 5 206.2]
bodhicittaṃ ca ye cānye dharmā nirvāṇagāminaḥ | [SDhPS, 5 207.1]
sāsravānāsravāḥ śāntāḥ sarve gaganasaṃnibhāḥ | [SDhPS, 5 207.2]
brahmavihārāścatvāraḥ saṃgrahā ye ca kīrtitāḥ | [SDhPS, 5 208.1]
sattvānāṃ vinayārthāya kīrtitāḥ paramarṣibhiḥ | [SDhPS, 5 208.2]
yaśca dharmān vijānāti māyāsvapnasvabhāvakān | [SDhPS, 5 209.1]
kadalīskandhaniḥsārān pratiśrutkāsamānakān | [SDhPS, 5 209.2]
tatsvabhāvaṃ ca jānāti traidhātukamaśeṣataḥ | [SDhPS, 5 210.1]
abaddham avimuktaṃ ca na vijānāti nirvṛtim | [SDhPS, 5 210.2]
sarvadharmān samān śūnyānnirnānākaraṇātmakān | [SDhPS, 5 211.1]
na caitān prekṣate nāpi kiṃciddharmaṃ vipaśyati | [SDhPS, 5 211.2]
sa paśyati mahāprajño dharmakāyamaśeṣataḥ | [SDhPS, 5 212.1]
nāsti yānatrayaṃ kiṃcidekayānamihāsti tu | [SDhPS, 5 212.2]
sarvadharmāḥ samāḥ sarve samāḥ samasamāḥ sadā | [SDhPS, 5 213.1]
evaṃ jñātvā vijānāti nirvāṇamamṛtaṃ śivam | [SDhPS, 5 213.2]
{SDhPS, 6}
atha khalu bhagavānimā gāthā bhāṣitvā sarvāvantaṃ bhikṣusaṃghamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 6 1.1]
ārocayāmi vo bhikṣavaḥ prativedayāmi | [SDhPS, 6 1.2]
ayaṃ mama śrāvakaḥ kāśyapo bhikṣustriṃśato buddhakoṭīsahasrāṇāmantike satkāraṃ kariṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 2.1]
gurukāraṃ mānanāṃ pūjanām arcanām apacāyanāṃ kariṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 2.2]
teṣāṃ ca buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ saddharmaṃ dhārayiṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 2.3]
sa paścime samucchraye avabhāsaprāptāyāṃ lokadhātau mahāvyūhe kalpe raśmiprabhāso nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loke bhaviṣyati vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān | [SDhPS, 6 3.1]
dvādaśa cāsyāntarakalpānāyuṣpramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 4.1]
viṃśatiṃ cāsyāntarakalpān saddharmaḥ sthāsyati | [SDhPS, 6 5.1]
viṃśatimevāntarakalpān saddharmapratirūpakaḥ sthāsyati | [SDhPS, 6 6.1]
taccāsya buddhakṣetraṃ śuddhaṃ bhaviṣyati śuci apagatapāṣāṇaśarkarakaṭhalyam apagataśvabhraprapātam apagatasyandanikāgūthoḍigallaṃ samaṃ ramaṇīyaṃ prāsādikaṃ darśanīyaṃ vaiḍūryamayaṃ ratnavṛkṣapratimaṇḍitaṃ suvarṇasūtrāṣṭāpadanibaddhaṃ puṣpābhikīrṇam | [SDhPS, 6 7.1]
bahūni ca tatra bodhisattvaśatasahasrāṇyutpatsyante | [SDhPS, 6 8.1]
aprameyāṇi ca tatra śrāvakakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 6 9.1]
na ca tatra māraḥ pāpīyānavatāraṃ lapsyate | [SDhPS, 6 10.1]
na ca māraparṣat prajñāsyate | [SDhPS, 6 10.2]
bhaviṣyanti tatra khalu punarmāraśca māraparṣadaśca | [SDhPS, 6 11.1]
api tu khalu punastatra lokadhātau tasyaiva bhagavato raśmiprabhāsasya tathāgatasya śāsane saddharmaparigrahāyābhiyuktā bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 6 12.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 6 13.1]
atha khalvāyuṣmān mahāmaudgalyāyanaḥ sthavira āyuṣmāṃśca subhūtirāyuṣmāṃśca mahākātyāyanaḥ pravepamānaiḥ kāyairbhagavantamanimiṣairnetrairvyavalokayanti sma | [SDhPS, 6 23.1]
tasyāṃ ca velāyāṃ pṛthak pṛthaṅmanaḥsaṃgītyā imā gāthā abhāṣanta | [SDhPS, 6 24.1]
arhanta he mahāvīra śākyasiṃha narottama | [SDhPS, 6 25.1]
asmākamanukampāya buddhaśabdamudīraya | [SDhPS, 6 25.2]
avaśyamavasaraṃ jñātvā asmākaṃ pi narottama | [SDhPS, 6 26.1]
amṛteneva siñcitvā vyākuruṣva vibhojana | [SDhPS, 6 26.2]
durbhikṣādāgataḥ kaścinnaro labdhvā subhojanam | [SDhPS, 6 27.1]
pratīkṣa bhūya ucyeta hastaprāptasmi bhojane | [SDhPS, 6 27.2]
evamevotsukā asmo hīnayānaṃ vicintaya | [SDhPS, 6 28.1]
duṣkālabhuktasattvā vā buddhajñānaṃ labhāmahe | [SDhPS, 6 28.2]
na tāvadasmān saṃbuddho vyākaroti mahāmuniḥ | [SDhPS, 6 29.1]
yathā hastasmi prakṣiptaṃ na tadbhuñjīta bhojanam | [SDhPS, 6 29.2]
evaṃ ca utsukā vīra śrutvā ghoṣamanuttaram | [SDhPS, 6 30.1]
vyākṛtā yada bheṣyāmastadā bheṣyāma nirvṛtāḥ | [SDhPS, 6 30.2]
atha khalu bhagavāṃsteṣāṃ mahāśrāvakāṇāṃ sthavirāṇāmimamevaṃrūpaṃ cetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya punarapi sarvāvantaṃ bhikṣusaṃghamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 6 32.1]
ayaṃ me bhikṣavo mahāśrāvakaḥ sthaviraḥ subhūtistriṃśata eva buddhakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇāṃ satkāraṃ kariṣyati gurukāraṃ mānanāṃ pūjanām arcanām apacāyanāṃ kariṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 32.2]
tatra ca brahmacaryaṃ cariṣyati bodhiṃ ca samudānayiṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 33.1]
evaṃrūpāṃścādhikārān kṛtvā paścime samucchraye śaśiketurnāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loke bhaviṣyati vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān | [SDhPS, 6 34.1]
ratnasaṃbhavaṃ ca nāmāsya tad buddhakṣetraṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 35.1]
ratnāvabhāsaśca nāma sa kalpo bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 36.1]
samaṃ ca tad buddhakṣetraṃ bhaviṣyati ramaṇīyaṃ sphaṭikamayaṃ ratnavṛkṣavicitritamapagataśvabhraprapātamapagatagūtholigallaṃ manojñaṃ puṣpābhikīrṇam | [SDhPS, 6 37.1]
kūṭāgāraparibhogeṣu cātra puruṣā vāsaṃ kalpayiṣyanti | [SDhPS, 6 38.1]
bahavaścāsya śrāvakā bhaviṣyantyaparimāṇā yeṣāṃ na śakyaṃ gaṇanayā paryanto 'dhigantum | [SDhPS, 6 39.1]
bahūni cātra bodhisattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 6 40.1]
tasya ca bhagavato dvādaśāntarakalpān āyuṣpramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 41.1]
viṃśatiṃ cāntarakalpān saddharmaḥ sthāsyati | [SDhPS, 6 42.1]
viṃśatimevāntarakalpān saddharmapratirūpakaḥ sthāsyati | [SDhPS, 6 43.1]
sa ca bhagavān vaihāyasamantarīkṣe sthitvā abhīkṣṇaṃ dharmaṃ deśayiṣyati bahūni ca bodhisattvaśatasahasrāṇi bahūni ca śrāvakaśatasahasrāṇi vineṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 44.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 6 45.1]
ārocayāmi ahamadya bhikṣavaḥ prativedayāmyadya mamā śṛṇotha | [SDhPS, 6 46.1]
sthaviraḥ subhūtirmama śrāvako 'yaṃ bhaviṣyate buddha anāgate 'dhvani | [SDhPS, 6 46.2]
buddhāṃśca paśyitva mahānubhāvān triṃśacca pūrṇānayutāna koṭīḥ | [SDhPS, 6 47.1]
cariṣyate carya tadānulomikīmimasya jñānasya kṛtena caiṣaḥ | [SDhPS, 6 47.2]
atha khalu bhagavān punareva sarvāvantaṃ bhikṣusaṃghamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 6 54.1]
ārocayāmi vo bhikṣavaḥ prativedayāmi | [SDhPS, 6 54.2]
ayaṃ mama śrāvakaḥ sthaviro mahākātyāyano 'ṣṭānāṃ buddhakoṭīśatasahasrāṇāmantike satkāraṃ kariṣyati gurukāraṃ mānanāṃ pūjanām arcanām apacāyanāṃ kariṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 55.1]
parinirvṛtānāṃ ca teṣāṃ tathāgatānāṃ stūpān kariṣyati yojanasahasraṃ samucchrayeṇa pañcāśadyojanāni pariṇāhena saptānāṃ ratnānām | [SDhPS, 6 56.1]
tadyathā suvarṇasya rūpyasya vaiḍūryasya sphaṭikasya lohitamukter aśmagarbhasya musāragalvasya saptamasya ratnasya | [SDhPS, 6 57.1]
teṣāṃ ca stūpānāṃ pūjāṃ kariṣyati puṣpadhūpagandhamālyavilepanacūrṇacīvaracchatradhvajapatākāvaijayantībhiśca | [SDhPS, 6 58.1]
tataśca bhūyaḥ pareṇa paratareṇa punar viṃśatīnāṃ buddhakoṭīnāmantike evaṃrūpameva satkāraṃ kariṣyati gurukāraṃ mānanāṃ pūjanām arcanām apacāyanāṃ kariṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 59.1]
sa paścime samucchraye paścime ātmabhāvapratilambhe jāmbūnadaprabhāso nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loke bhaviṣyati vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān | [SDhPS, 6 60.1]
pariśuddhaṃ cāsya buddhakṣetraṃ bhaviṣyati samaṃ ramaṇīyaṃ prāsādikaṃ darśanīyaṃ sphaṭikamayaṃ ratnavṛkṣābhivicitritaṃ suvarṇasūtrāchoḍitaṃ puṣpasaṃstarasaṃstṛtam apagatanirayatiryagyoniyamalokāsurakāyaṃ bahunaradevapratipūrṇaṃ bahuśrāvakaśatasahasropaśobhitaṃ bahubodhisattvaśatasahasrālaṃkṛtam | [SDhPS, 6 61.1]
dvādaśa cāsya antarakalpānāyuṣpramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 62.1]
viṃśatiṃ cāsya antarakalpān saddharmaḥ sthāsyati | [SDhPS, 6 63.1]
viṃśatimevāntarakalpān saddharmapratirūpakaḥ sthāsyati | [SDhPS, 6 64.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 6 65.1]
atha khalu bhagavān punareva sarvāvantaṃ bhikṣusaṃghamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 6 71.1]
ārocayāmi vo bhikṣavaḥ prativedayāmi | [SDhPS, 6 71.2]
ayaṃ mama śrāvakaḥ sthaviro mahāmaudgalyāyano 'ṣṭāviṃśatibuddhasahasrāṇyārāgayiṣyati teṣāṃ ca buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ vividhaṃ satkāraṃ kariṣyati gurukāraṃ mānanāṃ pūjanām arcanām apacāyanāṃ kariṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 72.1]
parinirvṛtānāṃ ca teṣāṃ buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ stūpān kārayiṣyati saptaratnamayān | [SDhPS, 6 73.1]
tadyathā suvarṇasya rūpyasya vaidūryasya sphaṭikasya lohitamukteraśmagarbhasya musāragalvasya | [SDhPS, 6 74.1]
yojanasahasraṃ samucchrayeṇa pañcayojanaśatāni pariṇāhena | [SDhPS, 6 75.1]
teṣāṃ ca stūpānāṃ vividhāṃ pūjāṃ kariṣyati puṣpadhūpagandhamālyavilepanacūrṇacīvaracchatradhvajapatākāvaijayantībhiḥ | [SDhPS, 6 76.1]
tataśca bhūyaḥ pareṇa paratareṇa viṃśaterbuddhakoṭīśatasahasrāṇāmevaṃrūpameva satkāraṃ kariṣyati gurukāraṃ mānanāṃ pūjanām arcanām apacāyanāṃ kariṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 77.1]
paścime ca ātmabhāvapratilambhe tamālapatracandanagandho nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loke bhaviṣyati vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān | [SDhPS, 6 78.1]
manobhirāmaṃ ca nāmāsya tadbuddhakṣetraṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 79.1]
ratiprapūrṇaśca nāma sa kalpo bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 80.1]
pariśuddhaṃ cāsya tadbuddhakṣetraṃ bhaviṣyati samaṃ ramaṇīyaṃ prāsādikaṃ sudarśanīyaṃ sphaṭikamayaṃ ratnavṛkṣābhivicitritaṃ muktakusumābhikīrṇaṃ bahunaradevapratipūrṇamṛṣiśatasahasraniṣevitaṃ yaduta śrāvakaiśca bodhisattvaiśca | [SDhPS, 6 81.1]
caturviṃśatiṃ cāsya antarakalpānāyuṣpramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 6 82.1]
catvāriṃśacca antarakalpān saddharmaḥ sthāsyati | [SDhPS, 6 83.1]
catvāriṃśadeva antarakalpān saddharmapratirūpakaḥ sthāsyati | [SDhPS, 6 84.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 6 85.1]
{SDhPS, 7}
bhūtapūrvaṃ bhikṣavo 'tīte 'dhvani asaṃkhyeyaiḥ kalpair asaṃkhyeyatarair vipulairaprameyair acintyair aparimitair apramāṇaistataḥ pareṇa paratareṇa yadāsīt | [SDhPS, 7 1.1]
tena kālena tena samayena mahābhijñājñānābhibhūr nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loka udapādi vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān saṃbhavāyāṃ lokadhātau mahārūpe kalpe | [SDhPS, 7 1.2]
kiyaccirotpannaḥ sa bhikṣavastathāgato 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 7 2]
tadyathāpi nāma bhikṣavo yāvāniha trisāhasramahāsāhasre lokadhātau pṛthivīdhātus taṃ kaścideva puruṣaḥ sarvaṃ cūrṇīkuryān maṣiṃ kuryāt | [SDhPS, 7 3]
atha khalu sa puruṣastasmāllokadhātorekaṃ paramāṇurajo gṛhītvā pūrvasyāṃ diśi lokadhātusahasramatikramya tadekaṃ paramāṇuraja upanikṣipet | [SDhPS, 7 4]
atha sa puruṣo dvitīyaṃ ca paramāṇurajo gṛhītvā tataḥ pareṇa parataraṃ lokadhātusahasramatikramya dvitīyaṃ paramāṇuraja upanikṣipet | [SDhPS, 7 5]
anena paryāyeṇa sa puruṣaḥ sarvāvantaṃ pṛthivīdhātumupanikṣipet pūrvasyāṃ diśi | [SDhPS, 7 6]
tatkiṃ manyadhve bhikṣavaḥ śakyaṃ teṣāṃ lokadhātūnāmanto vā paryanto vā gaṇanayādhigantum | [SDhPS, 7 7]
ta āhuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 8]
no hīdaṃ bhagavan no hīdaṃ sugata | [SDhPS, 7 9]
bhagavānāha | [SDhPS, 7 10]
śakyaṃ punarbhikṣavasteṣāṃ lokadhātūnāṃ kenacid gaṇakena vā gaṇakamahāmātreṇa vā gaṇanayā paryanto 'dhigantuṃ yeṣu vopanikṣiptāni tāni paramāṇurajāṃsi yeṣu vā nopanikṣiptāni | [SDhPS, 7 11]
na tveva teṣāṃ kalpakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇāṃ śakyaṃ gaṇanāyogena paryanto 'dhigantum | [SDhPS, 7 12]
yāvantaḥ kalpāstasya bhagavato mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvas tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasyaitāvān sa kālo 'bhūd evamacintya evamapramāṇaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 13]
taṃ cāhaṃ bhikṣavastathāgataṃ tāvacciraṃ parinirvṛtamanena tathāgatajñānadarśanabalādhānena yathādya śvo vā parinirvṛtamanusmarāmi | [SDhPS, 7 14]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 7 15]
abhū atītā bahu kalpakoṭyo anusmarāmi dvipadānamuttamam | [SDhPS, 7 16.1]
abhijñajñānābhibhūvaṃ mahāmunim abhūṣi tatkālamanuttamo jinaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 16.2]
tasya khalu punarbhikṣavo mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvas tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasya catuṣpañcāśatkalpakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇyāyuṣpramāṇamabhūt | [SDhPS, 7 23]
pūrve ca sa bhagavān mahābhijñājñānābhibhūs tathāgato 'nabhisaṃbuddho 'nuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhiṃ bodhimaṇḍavarāgragata eva sarvāṃ mārasenāṃ prābhañjīt parājaiṣīt | [SDhPS, 7 24]
prabhañjayitvā parājayitvā anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhim abhisaṃbhotsyāmīti | [SDhPS, 7 25.1]
na ca tāvattasya te dharmā āmukhībhavanti sma | [SDhPS, 7 25.2]
sa bodhivṛkṣamūle bodhimaṇḍe ekamantarakalpamasthāt | [SDhPS, 7 26]
dvitīyamapyantarakalpam asthāt | [SDhPS, 7 27]
na ca tāvadanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhyate | [SDhPS, 7 28]
tṛtīyamapi caturthamapi pañcamamapi ṣaṣṭhamapi saptamamapi aṣṭamamapi navamamapi daśamamapyantarakalpaṃ bodhivṛkṣamūle bodhimaṇḍe 'sthāt sakṛdvartanena paryaṅkena antarād avyutthitaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 29]
aniñjamānena cittena acalamānena avepamānena kāyenāsthāt | [SDhPS, 7 30]
na ca tāvadasya te dharmā āmukhībhavanti sma | [SDhPS, 7 31.1]
tasya khalu punarbhikṣavo bhagavato bodhimaṇḍavarāgragatasya devaistrāyastriṃśairmahāsiṃhāsanaṃ prajñaptamabhūd yojanaśatasahasraṃ samucchrayeṇa yatra sa bhagavān niṣadya anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddhaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 32.1]
samanantaraniṣaṇṇasya ca khalu punastasya bhagavato bodhimaṇḍe 'tha brahmakāyikā devaputrā divyaṃ puṣpavarṣamabhipravarṣayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 33.1]
bodhimaṇḍasya parisāmantakena yojanaśatamantarikṣe ca vātān pramuñcanti ye taṃ jīrṇapuṣpam avakarṣayanti | [SDhPS, 7 34.1]
yathāpravarṣitaṃ ca tat puṣpavarṣaṃ tasya bhagavato bodhimaṇḍe niṣaṇṇasya avyucchinnaṃ pravarṣayanti | [SDhPS, 7 35.1]
paripūrṇān daśāntarakalpān taṃ bhagavantamabhyavakiranti sma | [SDhPS, 7 36.1]
tathā pravarṣitaṃ ca tatpuṣpavarṣaṃ pravarṣayanti yāvat parinirvāṇakālasamaye tasya bhagavatastaṃ bhagavantam abhyavakiranti | [SDhPS, 7 37.1]
cāturmahārājakāyikāśca devaputrā divyāṃ devadundubhimabhipravādayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 38.1]
tasya bhagavato bodhimaṇḍavarāgragatasya satkārārthamavyucchinnaṃ pravādayāmāsuḥ paripūrṇān daśāntarakalpān tasya bhagavato niṣaṇṇasya | [SDhPS, 7 39.1]
tata uttari tāni divyāṇi tūryāṇi satatasamitaṃ pravādayāmāsuryāvattasya bhagavato mahāparinirvāṇakālasamayāt | [SDhPS, 7 40.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavo daśānām antarakalpānām atyayena sa bhagavān mahābhijñājñānābhibhūstathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho 'nuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddhaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 41.1]
samanantarābhisaṃbuddhaṃ ca taṃ viditvā ye tasya bhagavataḥ kumārabhūtasya ṣoḍaśa putrā abhūvannaurasā jñānākaro nāma teṣāṃ jyeṣṭho 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 7 42.1]
teṣāṃ ca khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ ṣoḍaśānāṃ rājakumārāṇāmekaikasya ca vividhāni krīḍanakāni rāmaṇīyakānyabhūvan vicitrāṇi darśanīyāni | [SDhPS, 7 43.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaste ṣoḍaśa rājakumārāstāni vividhāni krīḍanakāni rāmaṇīyakāni visarjayitvā taṃ bhagavantaṃ mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvaṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhamanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddhaṃ viditvā mātṛbhirdhātrībhiśca rudantībhiḥ parivṛtāḥ puraskṛtāḥ tena ca mahārājñā cakravartinā āryakeṇa mahākośena rājāmātyaiśca bahubhiśca prāṇikoṭīnayutaśatasahasraiḥ parivṛtāḥ puraskṛtāḥ yena bhagavān mahābhijñājñānābhibhūstathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho bodhimaṇḍavarāgragatas tenopasaṃkrāmanti sma | [SDhPS, 7 44.1]
tasya bhagavataḥ satkārārthāya gurukārārthāya mānanārthāya pūjanārthāya arcanārthāya apacāyanārthāya upasaṃkrāntāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 45.1]
upasaṃkramya tasya bhagavataḥ pādau śirobhirvanditvā taṃ bhagavantaṃ triṣpradakṣiṇīkṛtya añjaliṃ pragṛhya taṃ bhagavantaṃ saṃmukhamābhirgāthābhiḥ sārūpyābhirabhiṣṭuvanti sma | [SDhPS, 7 46.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaste ṣoḍaśa rājakumārāḥ kumārabhūtā eva bālakās taṃ bhagavantaṃ mahābhijñājñānābhimukhaṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhamābhiḥ sārūpyābhir gāthābhiḥ saṃmukhamabhiṣṭutya taṃ bhagavantamadhyeṣante sma dharmacakrapravartanatāyai | [SDhPS, 7 54.1]
deśayatu bhagavān dharmaṃ deśayatu sugato dharmaṃ bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāyai mahato janakāyasyārthāya hitāya sukhāya devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca | [SDhPS, 7 54.2]
tasyāṃ ca velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣanta | [SDhPS, 7 55.1]
tena khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ samayena tena bhagavatā mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvā tathāgatenārhatā samyaksaṃbuddhena anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhyamānena daśasu dikṣvekaikasyāṃ diśi pañcāśallokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi ṣaḍvikāraṃ prakampitānyabhūvan mahatā cāvabhāsena sphuṭānyabhūvan | [SDhPS, 7 59.1]
sarveṣu ca teṣu lokadhātuṣu yā lokāntarikāstāsu ye akṣaṇāḥ saṃvṛtā andhakāratamisrā yatra imāvapi candrasūryau evaṃmaharddhikau evaṃmahānubhāvau evaṃmahaujaskau ābhayāpyābhāṃ nānubhavato varṇenāpi varṇaṃ tejasāpi tejo nānubhavatas tāsvapi tasmin samaye mahato 'vabhāsasya prādurbhāvo 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 7 60.1]
ye 'pi tāsu lokāntarikāsu sattvā upapannās te 'pyanyonyamevaṃ paśyanty anyonyamevaṃ saṃjānanti | [SDhPS, 7 61.1]
anye 'pi bata bhoḥ sattvāḥ santīhopapannāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 61.2]
anye 'pi bata bhoḥ sattvāḥ santīhopapannāḥ iti | [SDhPS, 7 62.1]
sarveṣu ca teṣu lokadhātuṣu yāni devabhavanāni devavimānāni ca yāvad brahmalokāt ṣaḍvikāraṃ prakampitānyabhūvan mahatā cāvabhāsena sphuṭānyabhūvan atikramya devānāṃ devānubhāvam | [SDhPS, 7 63.1]
iti hi bhikṣavastasmin samaye teṣu lokadhātuṣu mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya mahataśca audārikasyāvabhāsasya loke prādurbhāvo 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 7 64.1]
atha pūrvasyāṃ diśi teṣu pañcāśatsu lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu yāni brāhmāṇi vimānāni tānyatīva bhrājanti tapanti virājanti śrīmantyojasvīni ca | [SDhPS, 7 65.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavasteṣāṃ mahābrahmaṇāmetadabhavat | [SDhPS, 7 66.1]
imāni khalu punarbrāhmāṇi vimānānyatīva bhrājanti tapanti virājanti śrīmantyojasvīni ca | [SDhPS, 7 66.2]
kasya khalvidaṃ pūrvanimittaṃ bhaviṣyatīti | [SDhPS, 7 67.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavasteṣu pañcāśatsu lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu ye mahābrahmāṇas te sarve 'nyonyabhavanāni gatvā ārocayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 67.2]
atha khalu bhikṣavaḥ sarvasattvatrātā nāma mahābrahmā taṃ mahāntaṃ brahmagaṇaṃ gāthābhiradhyabhāṣata | [SDhPS, 7 68.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavasteṣu pañcāśatsu lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu ye mahābrahmāṇas te sarve sahitāḥ samagrāstāni divyāni svāni svāni brāhmāṇi vimānānyabhiruhya divyāṃśca sumerumātrān puṣpapuṭān gṛhītvā catasṛṣu dikṣvanucaṃkramanto 'nuvicarantaḥ paścimaṃ digbhāgaṃ prakrāntāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 72.1]
adrākṣuḥ khalu punasteṣu pañcāśatsu lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu bhikṣavaste mahābrahmāṇaḥ paścime digbhāge taṃ bhagavantaṃ mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvaṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ bodhimaṇḍavarāgragataṃ bodhivṛkṣamūle siṃhāsanopaviṣṭaṃ parivṛtaṃ puraskṛtaṃ devanāgayakṣagandharvāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragamanuṣyāmanuṣyais taiśca putraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhī rājakumārairadhyeṣyamāṇaṃ dharmacakrapravartanatāyai | [SDhPS, 7 73.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punaryena sa bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 74.1]
upasaṃkramya tasya bhagavataḥ pādau śirobhirvanditvā taṃ bhagavantamanekaśatasahasrakṛtvaḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya taiśca sumerumātraiḥ puṣpapuṭaistaṃ bhagavantamabhyavakiranti smābhiprakiranti sma taṃ ca bodhivṛkṣaṃ daśayojanapramāṇam | [SDhPS, 7 75.1]
abhyavakīrya tāni brāhmāṇi vimānāni tasya bhagavato niryātayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 76.1]
parigṛhṇātu bhagavānimāni brāhmāṇi vimānāni asmākamanukampāmupādāya | [SDhPS, 7 76.2]
paribhuñjatu sugata imāni brāhmāṇi vimānānyasmākam anukampāmupādāya | [SDhPS, 7 77.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaste mahābrahmāṇastāni svāni svāni vimānāni tasya bhagavato niryātya tasyāṃ velāyāṃ taṃ bhagavantaṃ saṃmukhamābhir gāthābhiḥ sārūpyābhirabhiṣṭuvanti sma | [SDhPS, 7 78.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaste mahābrahmāṇastaṃ bhagavantaṃ mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvaṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ saṃmukhamābhiḥ sārūpyābhirgāthābhirabhiṣṭutya taṃ bhagavantametadūcuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 82.1]
pravartayatu bhagavān dharmacakraṃ pravartayatu sugato dharmacakraṃ loke | [SDhPS, 7 82.2]
deśayatu bhagavān nirvṛtim | [SDhPS, 7 83.1]
tārayatu bhagavān sattvān | [SDhPS, 7 84.1]
anugṛhṇātu bhagavānimaṃ lokam | [SDhPS, 7 85.1]
deśayatu bhagavān dharmasvāmī dharmamasya lokasya samārakasya sabrahmakasya saśramaṇabrāhmaṇikāyāḥ prajāyāḥ sadevamānuṣāsurāyāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 86.1]
tad bhaviṣyati bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāyai mahato janakāyasyārthāya hitāya sukhāya devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca | [SDhPS, 7 87.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavastāni pañcāśad brahmakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇyekasvareṇa samasaṃgītyā taṃ bhagavantamābhiḥ sārūpyābhirgāthābhiradhyabhāṣanta | [SDhPS, 7 88.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaḥ sa bhagavāṃsteṣāṃ mahābrahmaṇāṃ tūṣṇīṃbhāvenādhivāsayati sma | [SDhPS, 7 91.1]
tena khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ samayena pūrvadakṣiṇe digbhāge teṣu pañcāśatsu lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu yāni brāhmāṇi vimānāni tānyatīva bhrājanti tapanti virājanti śrīmanti ojasvīni ca | [SDhPS, 7 92.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavasteṣāṃ brahmaṇāmetadabhavat | [SDhPS, 7 93.1]
imāni khalu punarbrāhmāṇi vimānānyatīva bhrājanti tapanti virājanti śrīmanti ojasvīni ca | [SDhPS, 7 93.2]
kasya khalvidaṃ pūrvanimittaṃ bhaviṣyatīti | [SDhPS, 7 94.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavasteṣu pañcāśatsu lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu ye mahābrahmāṇas te 'pi sarve 'nyonyabhavanāni gatvā ārocayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 94.2]
atha khalu bhikṣavo 'dhimātrakāruṇiko nāma mahābrahmā taṃ mahāntaṃ brahmagaṇaṃ gāthābhiradhyabhāṣata | [SDhPS, 7 95.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavastānyapi pañcāśad brahmakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi tāni svāni svāni divyāni brāhmāṇi vimānānyabhiruhya divyāṃśca sumerumātrān puṣpapuṭān gṛhītvā catasṛṣu dikṣvanucaṃkramanto 'nuvicaranta uttarapaścimaṃ digbhāgaṃ prakrāntāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 101.1]
adrākṣuḥ khalu punarbhikṣavaste mahābrahmāṇa uttarapaścime digbhāge taṃ bhagavantaṃ mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvaṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ bodhimaṇḍavarāgragataṃ bodhivṛkṣamūle siṃhāsanopaviṣṭaṃ parivṛtaṃ puraskṛtaṃ devanāgayakṣagandharvāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragamanuṣyāmanuṣyais taiśca putraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhī rājakumārairadhyeṣyamāṇaṃ dharmacakrapravartanatāyai | [SDhPS, 7 102.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punaryena sa bhagavān mahābhijñājñānābhibhūstathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhastenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 103.1]
upasaṃkramya ca tasya bhagavataḥ pādau śirobhirvanditvā taṃ bhagavantamanekaśatasahasrakṛtvaḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya taiḥ sumerumātraiḥ puṣpapuṭaistaṃ bhagavantamabhyavakiranti smābhiprakiranti sma taṃ ca bodhivṛkṣaṃ daśayojanapramāṇam | [SDhPS, 7 104.1]
abhyavakīrya tāni brāhmāṇi vimānāni tasya bhagavato niryātayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 105.1]
parigṛhṇātu bhagavānimāni brāhmāṇi vimānānyasmākamanukampāmupādāya | [SDhPS, 7 105.2]
paribhuñjatu sugata imāni brāhmāṇi vimānānyasmākamanukampāmupādāya | [SDhPS, 7 106.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaste mahābrahmāṇastāni svāni svāni vimānāni tasya bhagavato niryātya tasyāṃ velāyāṃ taṃ bhagavantaṃ saṃmukhamābhiḥ sārūpyābhirgāthābhirabhiṣṭuvanti sma | [SDhPS, 7 107.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaste mahābrahmāṇastaṃ bhagavantaṃ mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvaṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ saṃmukhamābhiḥ sārūpyābhirgāthābhirabhiṣṭutya taṃ bhagavantametadūcuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 112.1]
pravartayatu bhagavān dharmacakram | [SDhPS, 7 112.2]
pravartayatu sugato dharmacakraṃ loke | [SDhPS, 7 113.1]
deśayatu bhagavān nirvṛtim | [SDhPS, 7 114.1]
tārayatu bhagavān sattvān | [SDhPS, 7 115.1]
anugṛhṇātu bhagavānimaṃ lokam | [SDhPS, 7 116.1]
deśayatu bhagavān dharmamasya lokasya samārakasya sabrahmakasya saśramaṇabrāhmaṇikāyāḥ prajāyāḥ sadevamānuṣāsurāyāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 117.1]
tadbhaviṣyati bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāyai mahato janakāyasyārthāya hitāya sukhāya devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca | [SDhPS, 7 118.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavastāni pañcāśad brahmakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi ekasvareṇa samasaṃgītyā taṃ bhagavantamābhyāṃ sārūpyābhyāṃ gāthābhyāmadhyabhāṣanta | [SDhPS, 7 119.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaḥ sa bhagavāṃsteṣāmapi mahābrahmaṇāṃ tūṣṇībhāvenādhivāsayati sma | [SDhPS, 7 122.1]
tena khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ samayena dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi teṣu pañcāśatsu lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu yāni brāhmāṇi vimānāni tānyatīva bhrājanti tapanti virājanti śrīmanti ojasvīni ca | [SDhPS, 7 123.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavasteṣāṃ mahābrahmaṇāmetadabhavat | [SDhPS, 7 124.1]
imāni khalu punarbrāhmāṇi vimānānyatīva bhrājanti tapanti virājanti śrīmanti ojasvīni ca | [SDhPS, 7 124.2]
kasya khalvidamevaṃrūpaṃ pūrvanimittaṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 7 125.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavasteṣu pañcāśatsu lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu ye mahābrahmāṇas te sarve 'nyonyabhavanāni gatvā ārocayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 125.2]
atha khalu bhikṣavaḥ sudharmo nāma mahābrahmā taṃ mahāntaṃ brahmagaṇaṃ gāthābhyāmadhyabhāṣata | [SDhPS, 7 126.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavasteṣu pañcāśatsu lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu ye mahābrahmāṇaḥ te sarve sahitāḥ samagrāstāni divyāni svāni svāni brāhmāṇi vimānānyabhiruhya divyāṃśca sumerumātrān puṣpapuṭān gṛhītvā catasṛṣu dikṣvanucaṃkramanto 'nuvicaranta uttaraṃ digbhāgaṃ prakrāntāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 129.1]
adrākṣuḥ khalu punarbhikṣavaste mahābrahmāṇa uttaraṃ digbhāgaṃ taṃ bhagavantaṃ mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvaṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ bodhimaṇḍavarāgragataṃ bodhivṛkṣamūle siṃhāsanopaviṣṭaṃ parivṛtaṃ puraskṛtaṃ devanāgayakṣagandharvāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragamanuṣyāmanuṣyais taiśca putraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhī rājakumārairadhyeṣyamāṇaṃ dharmacakrapravartanatāyai | [SDhPS, 7 130.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punaryena sa bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 131.1]
upasaṃkramya tasya bhagavataḥ pādau śirobhirvanditvā taṃ bhagavantamanekaśatasahasrakṛtvaḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya taiḥ sumerumātraiḥ puṣpapuṭaistaṃ bhagavantamabhyavakiranti smābhiprakiranti sma taṃ ca bodhivṛkṣaṃ daśayojanapramāṇam | [SDhPS, 7 132.1]
abhyavakīrya tāni brāhmāṇi divyāni vimānāni tasya bhagavato niryātayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 133.1]
parigṛhṇātu bhagavānimāni brāhmāṇi vimānāni asmākamanukampāmupādāya | [SDhPS, 7 133.2]
paribhuñjatu sugata imāni brāhmāṇi vimānāni asmākamanukampāmupādāya | [SDhPS, 7 134.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaste 'pi mahābrahmāṇastāni svāni svāni vimānāni tasya bhagavato niryātya tasyāṃ velāyāṃ taṃ bhagavantaṃ saṃmukhamābhiḥ sārūpyābhirgāthābhirabhiṣṭuvanti sma | [SDhPS, 7 135.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaste mahābrahmāṇastaṃ bhagavantaṃ mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvaṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ saṃmukhamābhiḥ sārūpyābhirgāthābhirabhiṣṭutya te bhagavantametadūcuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 139.1]
pravartayatu bhagavān dharmacakraṃ loke | [SDhPS, 7 139.2]
deśayatu bhagavān nirvṛtim | [SDhPS, 7 140.1]
tārayatu bhagavān sattvān | [SDhPS, 7 141.1]
anugṛhṇātu bhagavānimaṃ lokam | [SDhPS, 7 142.1]
deśayatu bhagavān dharmamasya lokasya samārakasya sabrahmakasya saśramaṇabrāhmaṇikāyāḥ prajāyāḥ sadevamānuṣāsurāyāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 143.1]
tadbhaviṣyati bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāyai mahato janakāyasyārthāya hitāya sukhāya devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca | [SDhPS, 7 144.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavastāni pañcāśad brahmakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi ekasvareṇa samasaṃgītyā taṃ bhagavantamābhyāṃ sārūpyābhyāṃ gāthābhyāmadhyabhāṣanta | [SDhPS, 7 145.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaḥ sa bhagavāṃsteṣāṃ mahābrahmaṇāṃ tūṣṇīṃbhāvenādhivāsayati sma | [SDhPS, 7 148.1]
peyālam | [SDhPS, 7 149.1]
evaṃ dakṣiṇapaścimāyāṃ diśy evaṃ paścimāyāṃ diśy evaṃ paścimottarasyāṃ diśy evamuttarasyāṃ diśy evamuttarapūrvasyāṃ diśy evamadhodiśi | [SDhPS, 7 150.1]
atha khalu bhikṣava ūrdhvāyāṃ diśi teṣu pañcāśatsu lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu yāni brāhmāṇi vimānāni tānyatīva bhrājanti tapanti virājanti śrīmanti ojasvīni ca | [SDhPS, 7 151.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavasteṣāṃ mahābrahmaṇāmetadabhavat | [SDhPS, 7 152.1]
imāni khalu punarbrāhmāṇi vimānānyatīva bhrājanti tapanti virājanti śrīmanti ojasvīni ca | [SDhPS, 7 152.2]
kasya khalvidamevaṃrūpaṃ pūrvanimittaṃ bhaviṣyatīti | [SDhPS, 7 153.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavasteṣu pañcāśatsu lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu ye mahābrahmāṇas te sarve 'nyonyabhavanāni gatvā ārocayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 153.2]
atha khalu bhikṣavaḥ śikhī nāma mahābrahmā taṃ mahāntaṃ brahmagaṇaṃ gāthābhiradhyabhāṣata | [SDhPS, 7 154.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavasteṣu pañcāśatsu lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu ye mahābrahmāṇas te sarve sahitāḥ samagrāstāni divyāni svāni svāni brāhmāṇi vimānānyabhiruhya divyāṃśca sumerumātrān puṣpapuṭān gṛhītvā catasṛṣu dikṣvanucaṃkramanto 'nuvicaranto yena adhodigbhāgastenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 158.1]
adrākṣuḥ khalu punarbhikṣavaste mahābrahmāṇo 'dhodigbhāge taṃ bhagavantaṃ mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvaṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ bodhimaṇḍavarāgragataṃ bodhivṛkṣamūle siṃhāsanopaviṣṭaṃ parivṛtaṃ puraskṛtaṃ devanāgayakṣagandharvāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragamanuṣyāmanuṣyais taiśca putraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhī rājakumārairadhyeṣyamāṇaṃ dharmacakrapravartanatāyai | [SDhPS, 7 159.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punaryena sa bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 160.1]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirobhirvanditvā taṃ bhagavantamanekaśatasahasrakṛtvaḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya taiḥ sumerumātraiḥ puṣpapuṭaistaṃ bhagavantamabhyavakiranti smābhiprakiranti sma taṃ ca bodhivṛkṣaṃ daśayojanapramāṇam | [SDhPS, 7 161.1]
abhyavakīrya tāni divyāni svāni svāni brāhmāṇi vimānāni tasya bhagavato niryātayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 162.1]
pratigṛhṇātu bhagavānimāni brāhmāṇi vimānānyasmākamanukampāmupādāya | [SDhPS, 7 162.2]
paribhuñjatu sugata imāni brāhmāṇi vimānānyasmākamanukampāmupādāyeti | [SDhPS, 7 163.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaste 'pi mahābrahmāṇastāni svāni svāni vimānāni tasya bhagavato niryātya tasyāṃ velāyāṃ taṃ bhagavantaṃ saṃmukhamābhiḥ sārūpyābhirgāthābhirabhiṣṭuvanti sma | [SDhPS, 7 164.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaste mahābrahmāṇastaṃ bhagavantaṃ mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvaṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ saṃmukhamābhiḥ sārūpyābhirgāthābhirabhiṣṭutya taṃ bhagavantametadūcuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 176.1]
pravartayatu bhagavān dharmacakram | [SDhPS, 7 176.2]
pravartayatu sugato dharmacakram | [SDhPS, 7 177.1]
deśayatu bhagavān nirvṛtim | [SDhPS, 7 178.1]
tārayatu bhagavān sarvasattvān | [SDhPS, 7 179.1]
anugṛhṇātu bhagavānimaṃ lokam | [SDhPS, 7 180.1]
deśayatu bhagavān dharmamasya lokasya samārakasya sabrahmakasya saśramaṇabrāhmaṇikāyāḥ prajāyāḥ sadevamānuṣāsurāyāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 181.1]
tadbhaviṣyati bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāyai mahato janakāyasyārthāya hitāya sukhāya devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca | [SDhPS, 7 182.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavastāni pañcāśad brahmakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇyekasvareṇa samasaṃgītyā taṃ bhagavantamābhyāṃ sārūpyābhyāṃ gāthābhyāmadhyabhāṣanta | [SDhPS, 7 183.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaḥ sa bhagavān mahābhijñājñānābhibhūstathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhasteṣāṃ brahmakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇāmadhyeṣaṇāṃ viditvā teṣāṃ ca ṣoḍaśānāṃ putrāṇāṃ rājakumārāṇāṃ tasyāṃ velāyāṃ dharmacakraṃ pravartayāmāsa triparivartaṃ dvādaśākāram apravartitaṃ śramaṇena vā brāhmaṇena vā devena vā māreṇa vā brahmaṇā vā anyena vā kenacit punarloke saha dharmeṇa | [SDhPS, 7 186.1]
yadidaṃ duḥkham ayaṃ duḥkhasamudayo 'yaṃ duḥkhanirodha iyaṃ duḥkhanirodhagāminī pratipadāryasatyamiti | [SDhPS, 7 187.1]
pratītyasamutpādapravṛttiṃ ca vistareṇa saṃprakāśayāmāsa | [SDhPS, 7 188.1]
iti hi bhikṣavo 'vidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārāḥ saṃskārapratyayaṃ vijñānaṃ vijñānapratyayaṃ nāmarūpaṃ nāmarūpapratyayaṃ ṣaḍāyatanaṃ ṣaḍāyatanapratyayaḥ sparśaḥ sparśapratyayā vedanā vedanāpratyayā tṛṣṇā tṛṣṇāpratyayamupādānam upādānapratyayo bhavo bhavapratyayā jātir jātipratyayā jarāmaraṇaśokaparidevaduḥkhadaurmanasyopāyāsāḥ sambhavanti | [SDhPS, 7 188.2]
evamasya kevalasya mahato duḥkhaskandhasya samudayo bhavati | [SDhPS, 7 189.1]
avidyānirodhāt saṃskāranirodhaḥ saṃskāranirodhād vijñānanirodho vijñānanirodhānnāmarūpanirodho nāmarūpanirodhāt ṣaḍāyatananirodhaḥ ṣaḍāyatananirodhāt sparśanirodhaḥ sparśanirodhād vedanānirodho vedanānirodhāttṛṣṇānirodhas tṛṣṇānirodhādupādānanirodha upādānanirodhād bhavanirodho bhavanirodhājjātinirodho jātinirodhājjarāmaraṇaśokaparidevaduḥkhadaurmanasyopāyāsā nirudhyante | [SDhPS, 7 190.1]
evamasya kevalasya mahato duḥkhaskandhasya nirodho bhavati | [SDhPS, 7 191.1]
sahapravartitaṃ cedaṃ bhikṣavastena bhagavatā mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvā tathāgatenārhatā samyaksaṃbuddhena dharmacakraṃ sadevakasya lokasya samārakasya sabrahmakasya saśramaṇabrāhmaṇikāyāḥ prajāyāḥ sadevamānuṣāsurāyāḥ parṣadaḥ purastāt | [SDhPS, 7 192.1]
atha tasminneva kṣaṇalavamuhūrte ṣaṣṭeḥ prāṇikoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇām anupādāya āsravebhyaścittāni vimuktāni | [SDhPS, 7 192.2]
sarve ca te traividyāḥ ṣaḍabhijñā aṣṭavimokṣadhyāyinaḥ saṃvṛttāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 193.1]
punaranupūrveṇa bhikṣavaḥ sa bhagavān mahābhijñājñānābhibhūstathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho dvitīyāṃ dharmadeśanāmakārṣīt tṛtīyāmapi dharmadeśanāmakārṣīc caturthīmapi dharmadeśanāmakārṣīt | [SDhPS, 7 194.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavastasya bhagavato mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvas tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasyaikaikasyāṃ dharmadeśanāyāṃ gaṅgānadīvālukāsamānāṃ prāṇikoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇām anupādāya āsravebhyaścittāni vimuktāni | [SDhPS, 7 195.1]
tataḥ paścād bhikṣavastasya bhagavato gaṇanāsamatikrāntaḥ śrāvakasaṃgho 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 7 196.1]
tena khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ samayena te ṣoḍaśa rājakumārāḥ kumārabhūtā eva samānāḥ śraddhayā agārād anāgārikāṃ pravrajitāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 197.1]
sarve ca te śrāmaṇerā abhūvan paṇḍitā vyaktā medhāvinaḥ kuśalā bahubuddhaśatasahasracaritāvino 'rthinaścānuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodheḥ | [SDhPS, 7 198.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaste ṣoḍaśa śrāmaṇerāstaṃ bhagavantaṃ mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvaṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhametadūcuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 199.1]
imāni khalu punarbhagavaṃstathāgatasya bahūni śrāvakakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi maharddhikāni mahānubhāvāni maheśākhyāni bhagavato dharmadeśanayā pariniṣpannāni | [SDhPS, 7 199.2]
tat sādhu bhagavāṃstathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho 'smākamanukampāmupādāya anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimārabhya dharmaṃ deśayatu yadvayamapi tathāgatasyānuśikṣemahi | [SDhPS, 7 200.1]
arthino vayaṃ bhagavaṃs tathāgatajñānadarśanena | [SDhPS, 7 201.1]
bhagavānevāsmākamasminnevārthe sākṣī | [SDhPS, 7 202.1]
tvaṃ ca bhagavan sarvasattvāśayajño jānīṣe asmākamadhyāśayamiti | [SDhPS, 7 203.1]
tena khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ samayena tān bālān dārakān rājakumārān pravrajitān śrāmaṇerān dṛṣṭvā yāvāṃstasya rājñaścakravartinaḥ parivāras tato 'rdhaḥ pravrajito 'bhūdaśītiprāṇikoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi | [SDhPS, 7 204.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaḥ sa bhagavān mahābhijñājñānābhibhūstathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhasteṣāṃ śrāmaṇerāṇāmadhyāśayaṃ viditvā viṃśateḥ kalpasahasrāṇāmatyayena saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ nāma dharmaparyāyaṃ sūtrāntaṃ mahāvaipulyaṃ bodhisattvāvavādaṃ sarvabuddhaparigrahaṃ vistareṇa saṃprakāśayāmāsa tāsāṃ sarvāsāṃ catasṛṇāṃ parṣadām | [SDhPS, 7 205.1]
tena khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ samayena tasya bhagavato bhāṣitaṃ te ṣoḍaśa rājakumārāḥ śrāmaṇerā udgṛhītavanto dhāritavanta ārādhitavantaḥ paryāptavantaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 206.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaḥ sa bhagavān mahābhijñājñānābhibhūstathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhastān ṣoḍaśa śrāmaṇerān vyākārṣīdanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 7 207.1]
tasya khalu punarbhikṣavo mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvas tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasyemaṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ bhāṣamāṇasya śrāvakāścādhimuktavantaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 208.1]
te ca ṣoḍaśa śrāmaṇerā bahūni ca prāṇikoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi vicikitsāprāptānyabhūvan | [SDhPS, 7 209.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaḥ sa bhagavān mahābhijñājñānābhibhūstathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddha imaṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ dharmaparyāyamaṣṭau kalpasahasrāṇyaviśrānto bhāṣitvā vihāraṃ praviṣṭaḥ pratisaṃlayanāya | [SDhPS, 7 210.1]
tathā pratisaṃlīnaśca bhikṣavaḥ sa tathāgataścaturaśītikalpasahasrāṇi vihārasthita evāsīt | [SDhPS, 7 211.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaste ṣoḍaśa śrāmaṇerāstaṃ bhagavantaṃ mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvaṃ tathāgataṃ pratisaṃlīnaṃ viditvā pṛthak pṛthag dharmāsanāni siṃhāsanāni prajñāpya teṣu niṣaṇṇāstaṃ bhagavantaṃ mahābhijñājñānābhibhuvaṃ tathāgataṃ namaskṛtya taṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ vistareṇa catasṛṇāṃ parṣadāṃ caturaśītikalpasahasrāṇi saṃprakāśitavantaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 212.1]
tatra bhikṣava ekaikaḥ śrāmaṇero bodhisattvaḥ ṣaṣṭiṣaṣṭigaṅgānadīvālukāsamāni prāṇikoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau paripācitavān samādāpitavān saṃharṣitavān samuttejitavān saṃpraharṣitavān avatāritavān | [SDhPS, 7 213.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaḥ sa bhagavān mahābhijñājñānābhibhūstathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhasteṣāṃ caturaśīteḥ kalpasahasrāṇāmatyayena smṛtimān saṃprajānaṃstasmāt samādher vyuttiṣṭhat | [SDhPS, 7 214.1]
vyutthāya ca sa bhagavān mahābhijñājñānābhibhūstathāgato yena taddharmāsanaṃ tenopasaṃkrāmat | [SDhPS, 7 215.1]
upasaṃkramya prajñapta evāsane nyaṣīdat | [SDhPS, 7 216.1]
samanantaraniṣaṇṇaśca khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ sa bhagavān mahābhijñājñānābhibhūstathāgatastasmin dharmāsane 'tha tāvadeva sarvāvantaṃ parṣanmaṇḍalamavalokya bhikṣusaṃgham āmantrayāmāsa | [SDhPS, 7 217.1]
āścaryaprāptā bhikṣavo 'dbhutaprāptā ime ṣoḍaśa śrāmaṇerāḥ prajñāvanto bahubuddhakoṭīnayutaśatasahasraparyupāsitāścīrṇacaritā buddhajñānaparyupāsakā buddhajñānapratigrāhakā buddhajñānāvatārakā buddhajñānasaṃdarśakāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 217.2]
paryupāsadhvaṃ bhikṣava etān ṣoḍaśa śrāmaṇerān punaḥ punaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 218.1]
ye kecid bhikṣavaḥ śrāvakayānikā vā pratyekabuddhayānikā vā bodhisattvayānikā vā eṣāṃ kulaputrāṇāṃ dharmadeśanāṃ na pratikṣepsyanti | [SDhPS, 7 219.1]
na pratibādhiṣyante | [SDhPS, 7 220.1]
sarve te kṣipramanuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodherlābhino bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 7 220.2]
sarve ca te tathāgatajñānamanuprāpsyanti | [SDhPS, 7 220.3]
taiḥ khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ kulaputraistasya bhagavataḥ śāsane 'yaṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīko dharmaparyāyaḥ punaḥ punaḥ saṃprakāśito 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 7 221.1]
taiḥ khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ śrāmaṇerairbodhisattvairmahāsattvairyāni tānyekaikena bodhisattvena mahāsattvena ṣaṣṭiṣaṣṭigaṅgānadīvālukāsamāni sattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi bodhāya samādāpitānyabhūvan sarvāṇi ca tāni taireva sārdhaṃ tāsu tāsu jātiṣvanupravrajitāni | [SDhPS, 7 222.1]
tānyeva samanupaśyantasteṣāmevāntikāddharmamaśrauṣuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 223.1]
taiścatvāriṃśad buddhakoṭīsahasrāṇyārāgitāni | [SDhPS, 7 224.1]
kecidadyāpyārāgayanti | [SDhPS, 7 225.1]
ārocayāmi vo bhikṣavaḥ prativedayāmi vaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 226.1]
ye te ṣoḍaśa rājakumārāḥ kumārabhūtā ye tasya bhagavataḥ śāsane śrāmaṇerā dharmabhāṇakā abhūvan sarve te 'nuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddhāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 227.1]
sarve ca ta etarhi tiṣṭhanti dhriyante yāpayanti | [SDhPS, 7 228.1]
daśasu dikṣu nānābuddhakṣetreṣu bahūnāṃ śrāvakabodhisattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇāṃ dharmaṃ deśayanti | [SDhPS, 7 229.1]
yaduta pūrvasyāṃ diśi bhikṣavo 'bhiratyāṃ lokadhātāvakṣobhyo nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho merukūṭaśca nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 230.1]
pūrvadakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi bhikṣavaḥ siṃhaghoṣaśca nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ siṃhadhvajaśca nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 231.1]
dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi bhikṣavaḥ ākāśapratiṣṭhitaśca nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho nityaparinirvṛtaśca nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 232.1]
dakṣiṇapaścimāyāṃ diśi bhikṣava indradhvajaśca nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho brahmadhvajaśca nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 233.1]
paścimāyāṃ diśi bhikṣavo 'mitāyuśca nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ sarvalokadhātūpadravodvegapratyuttīrṇaśca nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 234.1]
paścimottarasyāṃ diśi bhikṣavastamālapatracandanagandhābhijñaśca nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho merukalpaśca nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 235.1]
uttarasyāṃ diśi bhikṣavo meghasvaradīpaśca nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho meghasvararājaśca nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 236.1]
uttarapūrvasyāṃ diśi bhikṣavaḥ sarvalokabhayacchambhitatvavidhvaṃsanakaraśca nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 237.1]
ahaṃ ca bhikṣavaḥ śākyamunirnāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ ṣoḍaśamo madhye khalvasyāṃ sahāyāṃ lokadhātāvanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddhaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 238.1]
ye punaste bhikṣavastadā asmākaṃ śrāmaṇerabhūtānāṃ sattvā dharmaṃ śrutavantaḥ tasya bhagavataḥ śāsana ekaikasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya bahūni gaṅgānadīvālukāsamāni sattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi yānyasmābhiḥ samādāpitānyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau tānyetāni bhikṣavo 'dyāpi śrāvakabhūmāvevāvasthitāni | [SDhPS, 7 239.1]
paripācyanta evānuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 7 240.1]
eṣaivaiṣāmānupūrvī anuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodherabhisaṃbodhanāya | [SDhPS, 7 241.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 7 242.1]
evaṃ duradhimocyaṃ hi bhikṣavastathāgatajñānam | [SDhPS, 7 242.2]
katame ca te bhikṣavaḥ sattvā ye mayā bodhisattvena tasya bhagavataḥ śāsane aprameyāṇyasaṃkhyeyāni gaṅgānadīvālukāsamāni sattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi sarvajñatādharmamanuśrāvitāni | [SDhPS, 7 243.1]
yūyaṃ te bhikṣavastena kālena tena samayena sattvā abhūvan | [SDhPS, 7 243.2]
ye ca mama parinirvṛtasya anāgate 'dhvani śrāvakā bhaviṣyanti bodhisattvacaryāṃ ca śroṣyanti na cāvabhotsyante bodhisattvā vayamiti kiṃcāpi te bhikṣavaḥ sarve parinirvāṇasaṃjñinaḥ parinirvāsyanti api tu khalu punarbhikṣavo yadahamanyāsu lokadhātuṣvanyonyairnāmadheyairviharāmi tatra te punarutpatsyante tathāgatajñānaṃ paryeṣamāṇāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 244.1]
tatra ca te punarevaitāṃ kriyāṃ śroṣyanti | [SDhPS, 7 245.1]
ekameva tathāgatānāṃ parinirvāṇam | [SDhPS, 7 246.1]
nāstyanyad dvitīyamito bahirnirvāṇam | [SDhPS, 7 247.1]
tathāgatānāmetadbhikṣava upāyakauśalyaṃ veditavyaṃ dharmadeśanābhinirhāraśca | [SDhPS, 7 248.1]
yasmin bhikṣavaḥ samaye tathāgataḥ parinirvāṇakālasamayamātmanaḥ samanupaśyati pariśuddhaṃ ca parṣadaṃ paśyaty adhimuktisārāṃ śūnyadharmagatiṃ gatāṃ dhyānavatīṃ mahādhyānavatīm atha khalu bhikṣavastathāgato 'yaṃ kāla iti viditvā sarvān bodhisattvān sarvaśrāvakāṃśca saṃnipātya paścādetamarthaṃ saṃśrāvayati | [SDhPS, 7 249.1]
na bhikṣavaḥ kiṃcidasti loke dvitīyaṃ nāma yānaṃ parinirvāṇaṃ vā | [SDhPS, 7 250.1]
kaḥ punarvādastṛtīyasya | [SDhPS, 7 250.2]
upāyakauśalyaṃ khalvidaṃ bhikṣavastathāgatānāmarhatām | [SDhPS, 7 250.3]
dūrapranaṣṭaṃ sattvadhātuṃ viditvā hīnābhiratān kāmapaṅkamagnāṃs tata eṣāṃ bhikṣavastathāgatastannirvāṇaṃ bhāṣate yadadhimucyante | [SDhPS, 7 250.4]
tadyathāpi nāma bhikṣava iha syāt pañcayojanaśatikamaṭavīkāntāram | [SDhPS, 7 251.1]
mahāṃścātra janakāyaḥ pratipanno bhaved ratnadīpaṃ gamanāya | [SDhPS, 7 252.1]
deśikaścaiṣāmeko bhaved vyaktaḥ paṇḍito nipuṇo medhāvī kuśalaḥ khalvaṭavīdurgāṇām | [SDhPS, 7 253.1]
sa ca taṃ sārtham aṭavīmavakrāmayet | [SDhPS, 7 254.1]
atha khalu sa mahājanakāyaḥ śrāntaḥ klānto bhītastrastaḥ evaṃ vadet | [SDhPS, 7 255.1]
yat khalvārya deśika pariṇāyaka jānīyāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 255.2]
vayaṃ hi śrāntāḥ klāntā bhītāstrastā anirvṛtāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 255.3]
punareva pratinivartayiṣyāmaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 256.1]
atidūramito 'ṭavīkāntāramiti | [SDhPS, 7 257.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaḥ sa deśika upāyakuśalastān puruṣān pratinivartitukāmān viditvā evaṃ cintayet | [SDhPS, 7 258.1]
mā khalvime tapasvinastādṛśaṃ mahāratnadvīpaṃ na gaccheyuriti | [SDhPS, 7 258.2]
sa teṣāmanukampārthamupāyakauśalyaṃ prayojayet | [SDhPS, 7 259.1]
tasyā aṭavyā madhye yojanaśataṃ vā dviyojanaśataṃ vā triyojanaśataṃ vā atikramya ṛddhimayaṃ nagaram abhinirmimīyāt | [SDhPS, 7 260.1]
tatastān puruṣānevaṃ vadet | [SDhPS, 7 261.1]
mā bhavanto bhaiṣṭa mā nivartadhvam | [SDhPS, 7 261.2]
ayamasau mahājanapadaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 262.1]
atra viśrāmyata | [SDhPS, 7 263.1]
atra vo yāni kānicit karaṇīyāni tāni sarvāṇi kurudhvam | [SDhPS, 7 264.1]
atra nirvāṇaprāptā viharadhvamatra viśrāntāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 265.1]
yasya punaḥ kāryaṃ bhaviṣyati sa taṃ mahāratnadvīpaṃ gamiṣyati | [SDhPS, 7 266.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaste kāntāraprāptāḥ sattvā āścaryaprāptā adbhutaprāptā bhaveyuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 267.1]
muktā vayamaṭavīkāntārāt | [SDhPS, 7 267.2]
iha nirvāṇaprāptā vihariṣyāma iti | [SDhPS, 7 268.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavaste puruṣāstadṛddhimayaṃ nagaraṃ praviśeyur āgatasaṃjñinaśca bhaveyur nistīrṇasaṃjñinaśca bhaveyuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 269.1]
nirvṛtāḥ śītībhūtāḥ sma iti manyeran | [SDhPS, 7 270.1]
tatastān deśiko viśrāntān viditvā tadṛddhimayaṃ nagaram antardhāpayet | [SDhPS, 7 271.1]
antardhāpayitvā ca tān puruṣānevaṃ vadet | [SDhPS, 7 272.1]
āgacchantu bhavantaḥ sattvāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 272.2]
abhyāsanna eṣa mahāratnadvīpaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 273.1]
idaṃ tu mayā nagaraṃ yuṣmākaṃ viśrāmaṇārthamabhinirmitamiti | [SDhPS, 7 274.1]
evameva bhikṣavastathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho yuṣmākaṃ sarvasattvānāṃ ca deśikaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 275.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavastathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddha evaṃ paśyati | [SDhPS, 7 276.1]
mahadidaṃ kleśakāntāraṃ nirgantavyaṃ niṣkrāntavyaṃ prahātavyam | [SDhPS, 7 276.2]
mā khalvime ekameva buddhajñānaṃ śrutvā draveṇaiva pratinivartayeyur naivopasaṃkrameyuḥ | [SDhPS, 7 277.1]
bahuparikleśamidaṃ buddhajñānaṃ samudānayitavyamiti | [SDhPS, 7 278.1]
tatra tathāgataḥ sattvān durbalāśayān viditvā yathā sa deśikastadṛddhimayaṃ nagaram abhinirmimīte teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ viśrāmaṇārthaṃ viśrāntānāṃ caiṣāmevaṃ kathayatīdaṃ khalu ṛddhimayaṃ nagaramity evameva bhikṣavastathāgato 'pyarhan samyaksaṃbuddho mahopāyakauśalyena antarā dve nirvāṇabhūmī sattvānāṃ viśrāmaṇārthaṃ deśayati saṃprakāśayati yadidaṃ śrāvakabhūmiṃ pratyekabuddhabhūmiṃ ca | [SDhPS, 7 279]
yasmiṃśca bhikṣavaḥ samaye te sattvāstatra sthitā bhavanty atha khalu bhikṣavastathāgato 'pyevaṃ saṃśrāvayati | [SDhPS, 7 280.1]
na khalu punarbhikṣavo yūyaṃ kṛtakṛtyāḥ kṛtakaraṇīyāḥ | [SDhPS, 7 280.2]
api tu khalu punarbhikṣavo yuṣmākamabhyāsaḥ | [SDhPS, 7 281.1]
itastathāgatajñānaṃ vyavalokayadhvaṃ bhikṣavo vyavacārayadhvam | [SDhPS, 7 282.1]
yad yuṣmākaṃ nirvāṇaṃ naiva nirvāṇam api tu khalu punar upāyakauśalyametad bhikṣavastathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāṃ yat trīṇi yānāni saṃprakāśayantīti | [SDhPS, 7 283.1]
atha khalu bhagavānimamevārthaṃ bhūyasyā mātrayopadarśayamānastasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 7 284.1]
{SDhPS, 8}
atha khalvāyuṣmān pūrṇo maitrāyaṇīputro bhagavato 'ntikādidamevaṃrūpamupāyakauśalyajñānadarśanaṃ saṃdhābhāṣitanirdeśaṃ śrutvā eṣāṃ ca mahāśrāvakāṇāṃ vyākaraṇaṃ śrutvā imāṃ ca pūrvayogapratisaṃyuktāṃ kathāṃ śrutvā imāṃ ca bhagavato vṛṣabhatāṃ śrutvā āścaryaprāpto 'bhūdadbhutaprāpto 'bhūnnirāmiṣeṇa ca cittena prītiprāmodyena sphuṭo 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 8 1.1]
mahatā ca prītiprāmodyena mahatā ca dharmagauraveṇa utthāyāsanād bhagavataścaraṇayoḥ praṇipatya evaṃ cittamutpāditavān | [SDhPS, 8 2.1]
āścaryaṃ bhagavan āścaryaṃ sugata | [SDhPS, 8 2.2]
paramaduṣkaraṃ tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ kurvanti ya imaṃ nānādhātukaṃ lokamanuvartayante bahubhiścopāyakauśalyajñānanidarśanaiḥ sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśayanti tasmiṃstasmiṃśca sattvān vilagnānupāyakauśalyena pramocayanti | [SDhPS, 8 3.1]
kimatra bhagavan asmābhiḥ śakyaṃ kartum | [SDhPS, 8 4.1]
tathāgata evāsmākaṃ jānīte āśayaṃ pūrvayogacaryāṃ ca | [SDhPS, 8 4.2]
sa bhagavataḥ pādau śirasābhivandya ekānte sthito 'bhūd bhagavantameva namaskurvan animiṣābhyāṃ ca netrābhyāṃ samprekṣamāṇaḥ | [SDhPS, 8 5.1]
atha khalu bhagavānāyuṣmantaḥ pūrṇasya maitrāyaṇīputrasya cittāśayamavalokya sarvāvantaṃ bhikṣusaṃghamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 8 6.1]
paśyatha bhikṣavo yūyamimaṃ śrāvakaṃ pūrṇaṃ maitrāyaṇīputraṃ yo mayāsya bhikṣusaṃghasya dharmakathikānāmagryo nirdiṣṭo bahubhiśca bhūtairguṇairabhiṣṭuto bahubhiśca prakārairasmin mama śāsane saddharmaparigrahāyābhiyuktaḥ | [SDhPS, 8 6.2]
catasṛṇāṃ parṣadāṃ saṃharṣakaḥ samādāpakaḥ samuttejakaḥ saṃpraharṣako 'klānto dharmadeśanayālamasya dharmasyākhyātālamanugrahītā sabrahmacāriṇām | [SDhPS, 8 7.1]
muktvā bhikṣavastathāgataṃ nānyaḥ śaktaḥ pūrṇaṃ maitrāyaṇīputramarthato vā vyañjanato vā paryādātum | [SDhPS, 8 8.1]
tatkiṃ manyadhve bhikṣavo mamaivāyaṃ saddharmaparigrāhaka iti | [SDhPS, 8 9.1]
na khalu punarbhikṣavo yuṣmābhirevaṃ draṣṭavyam | [SDhPS, 8 9.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 8 10.1]
abhijānāmyahaṃ bhikṣavo 'tīte 'dhvani navanavatīnāṃ buddhakoṭīnāṃ yatra anenaiva teṣāṃ buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ śāsane saddharmaḥ parigṛhītaḥ | [SDhPS, 8 10.2]
tadyathāpi nāma mama etarhi sarvatra cāgryo dharmakathikānāmabhūt sarvatra ca śūnyatāgatiṃ gato 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 8 11.1]
sarvatra ca pratisaṃvidāṃ lābhī abhūt sarvatra ca bodhisattvābhijñāsu gatiṃ gato 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 8 12.1]
suviniścitadharmadeśako nirvicikitsadharmadeśakaḥ pariśuddhadharmadeśakaścābhūt | [SDhPS, 8 13.1]
teṣāṃ ca buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ śāsane yāvadāyuṣpramāṇaṃ brahmacaryaṃ caritavān | [SDhPS, 8 14.1]
sarvatra ca śrāvaka iti saṃjñāyate sma | [SDhPS, 8 15.1]
sa khalvanenopāyena aprameyāṇāmasaṃkhyeyānāṃ sattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇāmarthamakārṣīd aprameyānasaṃkhyeyāṃśca sattvān paripācitavān anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 8 16.1]
sarvatra ca buddhakṛtyena sattvānāṃ pratyupasthito 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 8 17.1]
sarvatra cātmano buddhakṣetraṃ pariśodhayati sma | [SDhPS, 8 18.1]
sattvānāṃ ca paripākāyābhiyukto 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 8 19.1]
eṣāmapi bhikṣavo vipaśyipramukhānāṃ saptānāṃ tathāgatānāṃ yeṣāmahaṃ saptama eṣa evāgryo dharmakathikānāmabhūt | [SDhPS, 8 20.1]
yadapi tadbhikṣavo bhaviṣyatyanāgate 'dhvani asmin bhadrakalpe caturbhirbuddhairūnaṃ buddhasahasraṃ teṣāmapi śāsane eṣa eva pūrṇo maitrāyaṇīputro 'gryo dharmakathikānāṃ bhaviṣyati saddharmaparigrāhakaśca bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 8 21.1]
evamanāgate 'dhvani aprameyāṇāmasaṃkhyeyānāṃ buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ saddharmamādhārayiṣyaty aprameyāṇāmasaṃkhyeyānāṃ sattvānāmarthaṃ kariṣyaty aprameyānasaṃkhyeyāṃśca sattvān paripācayiṣyatyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 8 22.1]
satatasamitaṃ cābhiyukto bhaviṣyatyātmano buddhakṣetrapariśuddhaye sattvaparipācanāya | [SDhPS, 8 23.1]
sa imāmevaṃrūpāṃ bodhisattvacaryāṃ paripūrya aprameyairasaṃkhyeyaiḥ kalpairanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbhotsyate | [SDhPS, 8 24.1]
dharmaprabhāso nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loke bhaviṣyati vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān | [SDhPS, 8 25.1]
asminneva buddhakṣetra utpatsyate | [SDhPS, 8 26.1]
tena khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ samayena gaṅgānadīvālukopamās trisāhasramahāsāhasralokadhātava ekaṃ buddhakṣetraṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 8 27.1]
samaṃ pāṇitalajātaṃ saptaratnamayamapagataparvataṃ saptaratnamayaiḥ kūṭāgāraiḥ paripūrṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 8 28.1]
devavimānāni cākāśasthitāni bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 8 29.1]
devā api manuṣyān drakṣyanti manuṣyā api devān drakṣyanti | [SDhPS, 8 30.1]
tena khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ samayena idaṃ buddhakṣetramapagatapāpaṃ bhaviṣyati apagatamātṛgrāmaṃ ca | [SDhPS, 8 31.1]
sarve ca te sattvā aupapādukā bhaviṣyanti brahmacāriṇo manomayairātmabhāvaiḥ svayaṃprabhā ṛddhimanto vaihāyasaṃgamā vīryavantaḥ smṛtimantaḥ prajñāvantaḥ suvarṇavarṇaiḥ samucchrayair dvātriṃśadbhir mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtavigrahāḥ | [SDhPS, 8 32.1]
tena khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ samayena tasmin buddhakṣetre teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ dvāvāhārau bhaviṣyataḥ | [SDhPS, 8 33.1]
katamau dvau | [SDhPS, 8 34.1]
yaduta dharmaprītyāhāro dhyānaprītyāhāraśca | [SDhPS, 8 34.2]
aprameyāṇi cāsaṃkhyeyāni bodhisattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi bhaviṣyanti sarveṣāṃ ca mahābhijñāprāptānāṃ pratisaṃvidgatiṃgatānāṃ sattvāvavādakuśalānām | [SDhPS, 8 35.1]
gaṇanāsamatikrāntāścāsya śrāvakā bhaviṣyanti maharddhikā mahānubhāvā aṣṭavimokṣadhyāyinaḥ | [SDhPS, 8 36.1]
evamaparimitaguṇasamanvāgataṃ tad buddhakṣetraṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 8 37.1]
ratnāvabhāsaśca nāma sa kalpo bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 8 38.1]
suviśuddhā ca nāma sā lokadhāturbhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 8 39.1]
aprameyānasaṃkhyeyāṃścāsya kalpānāyuṣpramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 8 40.1]
parinirvṛtasya ca tasya bhagavato dharmaprabhāsasya tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasya saddharmaścirasthāyī bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 8 41.1]
ratnamayaiśca stūpaiḥ sā lokadhātuḥ sphuṭā bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 8 42.1]
evamacintyaguṇasamanvāgataṃ bhikṣavastasya bhagavatastadbuddhakṣetraṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 8 43.1]
idamavocadbhagavān | [SDhPS, 8 44.1]
idaṃ vaditvā sugato hyathāparametaduvāca śāstā | [SDhPS, 8 45.1]
atha khalu teṣāṃ dvādaśānāṃ vaśībhūtaśatānāmetadabhavat | [SDhPS, 8 66.1]
āścaryaprāptāḥ smādbhutaprāptāḥ sma | [SDhPS, 8 66.2]
saced asmākamapi bhagavān yatheme 'nye mahāśrāvakā vyākṛtā evamasmākamapi tathāgataḥ pṛthak pṛthag vyākuryāt | [SDhPS, 8 67.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃsteṣāṃ mahāśrāvakāṇāṃ cetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya āyuṣmantaṃ mahākāśyapamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 8 68.1]
imāni kāśyapa dvādaśa vaśībhūtaśatāni yeṣāmahametarhi saṃmukhībhūtaḥ | [SDhPS, 8 68.2]
sarvāṇyetānyahaṃ kāśyapa dvādaśa vaśībhūtaśatānyanantaraṃ vyākaromi | [SDhPS, 8 69.1]
tatra kāśyapa kauṇḍinyo bhikṣurmahāśrāvako dvāṣaṣṭīnāṃ buddhakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇāṃ pareṇa parataraṃ samantaprabhāso nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loke bhaviṣyati vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān | [SDhPS, 8 70.1]
tatra kāśyapa anenaikena nāmadheyena pañca tathāgataśatāni bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 8 71.1]
ataḥ pañca mahāśrāvakaśatāni sarvāṇyanantaramanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbhotsyante | [SDhPS, 8 72.1]
sarvāṇyeva samantaprabhāsanāmadheyāni bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 8 73.1]
tadyathā gayākāśyapo nadīkāśyapaḥ urubilvakāśyapaḥ kālaḥ kālodāyī aniruddho revataḥ kapphiṇo bakkulaścundaḥ svāgataḥ ityevaṃpramukhāni pañca vaśībhūtaśatāni | [SDhPS, 8 74.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 8 75.1]
atha khalu tāni pañcārhacchatāni bhagavataḥ saṃmukhamātmano vyākaraṇāni śrutvā tuṣṭā udagrā āttamanasaḥ pramuditāḥ prītisaumanasyajātā yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [SDhPS, 8 89.1]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādayoḥ śirobhirnipatya evamāhuḥ | [SDhPS, 8 90.1]
atyayaṃ vayaṃ bhagavan deśayāmo yairasmābhir bhagavannevaṃ satatasamitaṃ cittaṃ paribhāvitam | [SDhPS, 8 90.2]
idamasmākaṃ parinirvāṇam | [SDhPS, 8 90.3]
parinirvṛtā vayamiti | [SDhPS, 8 91.1]
yathāpīdaṃ bhagavan avyaktā akuśalā avidhijñāḥ | [SDhPS, 8 92.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 8 93.1]
yairnāma asmābhirbhagavaṃstathāgatajñāne 'bhisaṃboddhavye evaṃrūpeṇa parīttena jñānena paritoṣaṃ gatāḥ sma | [SDhPS, 8 93.2]
tadyathāpi nāma bhagavan kasyacideva puruṣasya kaṃcideva mitragṛhaṃ praviṣṭasya mattasya vā suptasya vā sa mitro 'narghamaṇiratnaṃ vastrānte badhnīyāt | [SDhPS, 8 94.1]
asyedaṃ maṇiratnaṃ bhavatviti | [SDhPS, 8 94.2]
atha khalu bhagavan sa puruṣa utthāyāsanāt prakrāmet | [SDhPS, 8 95.1]
so 'nyaṃ janapadapradeśaṃ prapadyeta | [SDhPS, 8 96.1]
sa tatra kṛcchraprāpto bhavet | [SDhPS, 8 97.1]
āhāracīvaraparyeṣṭihetoḥ kṛcchramāpadyeta | [SDhPS, 8 98.1]
mahatā ca vyāyāmena kathaṃcit kaṃcidāhāraṃ pratilabheta | [SDhPS, 8 99.1]
tena ca saṃtuṣṭo bhavedāttamanaskaḥ pramuditaḥ | [SDhPS, 8 100.1]
atha khalu bhagavaṃstasya puruṣasya sa purāṇamitraḥ puruṣo yena tasya tadanargheyaṃ maṇiratnaṃ vastrānte baddhaṃ sa taṃ punareva paśyet | [SDhPS, 8 101.1]
tamevaṃ vadet | [SDhPS, 8 102.1]
kiṃ tvaṃ bhoḥ puruṣa kṛcchramāpadyase āhāracīvaraparyeṣṭihetor yadā yāvad bhoḥ puruṣa mayā tava sukhavihārārthaṃ sarvakāmanivartakamanargheyaṃ maṇiratnaṃ vastrānte upanibaddham | [SDhPS, 8 102.2]
niryātitaṃ te bhoḥ puruṣa mamaitanmaṇiratnam | [SDhPS, 8 103.1]
tadevamupanibaddhameva bhoḥ puruṣa vastrānte maṇiratnam | [SDhPS, 8 104.1]
na ca nāma tvaṃ bhoḥ puruṣa pratyavekṣase | [SDhPS, 8 105.1]
kiṃ mama baddhaṃ yena vā baddhaṃ ko hetuḥ kiṃnidānaṃ vā baddhametat | [SDhPS, 8 105.2]
bālajātīyastvaṃ bhoḥ puruṣa yastvaṃ kṛcchreṇa āhāracīvaraṃ paryeṣamāṇastuṣṭimāpadyase | [SDhPS, 8 105.3]
gaccha tvaṃ bhoḥ puruṣa etanmaṇiratnaṃ grahāya mahānagaraṃ gatvā parivartayasva | [SDhPS, 8 106.1]
tena ca dhanena sarvāṇi dhanakaraṇīyāni kuruṣveti | [SDhPS, 8 107.1]
evameva bhagavan asmākamapi tathāgatena pūrvameva bodhisattvacaryāṃ caratā sarvajñatācittānyutpāditānyabhūvan | [SDhPS, 8 108.1]
tāni ca vayaṃ bhagavan na jānīmo na budhyāmahe | [SDhPS, 8 109.1]
te vayaṃ bhagavan arhadbhūmau nirvṛtāḥ sma iti saṃjānīmaḥ | [SDhPS, 8 110.1]
vayaṃ kṛcchraṃ jīvāmo yadvayaṃ bhagavan evaṃ parīttena jñānena paritoṣam āpadyāmaḥ | [SDhPS, 8 111.1]
sarvajñajñānapraṇidhānena sadā avinaṣṭena | [SDhPS, 8 112.1]
te vayaṃ bhagavaṃstathāgatena saṃbodhyamānāḥ | [SDhPS, 8 113.1]
mā yūyaṃ bhikṣava etannirvāṇaṃ manyadhvam | [SDhPS, 8 113.2]
saṃvidyante bhikṣavo yuṣmākaṃ saṃtāne kuśalamūlāni yāni mayā pūrvaṃ paripācitāni | [SDhPS, 8 114.1]
etarhi ca mamaivedamupāyakauśalyaṃ dharmadeśanābhilāpena yad yūyametarhi nirvāṇamiti manyadhve | [SDhPS, 8 115.1]
evaṃ ca vayaṃ bhagavatā saṃbodhayitvā adyānuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau vyākṛtāḥ | [SDhPS, 8 116.1]
atha khalu tāni pañca vaśībhūtaśatānyājñātakauṇḍinyapramukhāni tasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣanta | [SDhPS, 8 117.1]
{SDhPS, 9}
atha khalvāyuṣmānānandastasyāṃ velāyāmevaṃ cintayāmāsa | [SDhPS, 9 1.1]
apyeva nāma vayamevaṃrūpaṃ vyākaraṇaṃ pratilabhemahi | [SDhPS, 9 1.2]
evaṃ ca cintayitvā anuvicintya prārthayitvā utthāyāsanād bhagavataḥ pādayornipatya āyuṣmāṃśca rāhulo 'pyevaṃ cintayitvā anuvicintya prārthayitvā bhagavataḥ pādayornipatya evaṃ vācamabhāṣata | [SDhPS, 9 2.1]
asmākamapi tāvad bhagavan avasaro bhavatu | [SDhPS, 9 2.2]
asmākamapi tāvat sugata avasaro bhavatu | [SDhPS, 9 3.1]
asmākaṃ hi bhagavān pitā janako layanaṃ trāṇaṃ ca | [SDhPS, 9 4.1]
vayaṃ hi bhagavan sadevamānuṣāsure loke 'tīva citrīkṛtāḥ | [SDhPS, 9 5.1]
bhagavataścaite putrā bhagavataścopasthāyakāḥ bhagavataśca dharmakośaṃ dhārayantīti | [SDhPS, 9 5.2]
tannāma bhagavan kṣiprameva pratirūpaṃ bhaved yad bhagavānasmākaṃ vyākuryādanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 9 6.1]
anye ca dve bhikṣusahasre sātireke śaikṣāśaikṣāṇāṃ śrāvakāṇāmutthāyāsanebhya ekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā añjaliṃ pragṛhya bhagavato 'bhimukhaṃ bhagavantamullokayamāne tasthatur etāmeva cintāmanuvicintayamāne yaduta idameva buddhajñānam | [SDhPS, 9 7.1]
apyeva nāma vayamapi vyākaraṇaṃ pratilabhemahi anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhāviti | [SDhPS, 9 7.2]
atha khalu bhagavānāyuṣmantamānandamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 9 8.1]
bhaviṣyasi tvamānanda anāgate 'dhvani sāgaravaradharabuddhivikrīḍitābhijño nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān | [SDhPS, 9 8.2]
dvāṣaṣṭīnāṃ buddhakoṭīnāṃ satkāraṃ kṛtvā gurukāraṃ mānanāṃ pūjanāṃ ca kṛtvā teṣāṃ buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ saddharmaṃ dhārayitvā śāsanaparigrahaṃ ca kṛtvā anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbhotsyasi | [SDhPS, 9 9.1]
sa tvamānanda anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhiṃ saṃbuddhaḥ samāno viṃśatigaṅgānadīvālukāsamāni bodhisattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi paripācayiṣyasyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 9 10.1]
samṛddhaṃ ca te buddhakṣetraṃ bhaviṣyati vaiḍūryamayaṃ ca | [SDhPS, 9 11.1]
anavanāmitavaijayantī ca nāma sā lokadhāturbhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 9 12.1]
manojñaśabdābhigarjitaśca nāma sa kalpo bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 9 13.1]
aparimitāṃśca kalpāṃstasya bhagavataḥ sāgaravaradharabuddhivikrīḍitābhijñasya tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasya āyuṣpramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati yeṣāṃ kalpānāṃ na śakyaṃ gaṇanayā paryanto 'dhigantum | [SDhPS, 9 14.1]
tāvadasaṃkhyeyāni tāni kalpakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi tasya bhagavata āyuṣpramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 9 15.1]
yāvacca ānanda tasya bhagavataḥ sāgaravaradharabuddhivikrīḍitābhijñasya tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasyāyuṣpramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati taddviguṇaṃ parinirvṛtasya saddharmaḥ sthāsyati | [SDhPS, 9 16.1]
yāvāṃstasya bhagavataḥ saddharmaḥ sthāsyati taddviguṇaḥ saddharmapratirūpakaṃ sthāsyati | [SDhPS, 9 17.1]
tasya khalu punarānanda sāgaravaradharabuddhivikrīḍitābhijñasya tathāgatasya daśasu dikṣu bahūni gaṅgānadīvālukāsamāni buddhakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi varṇaṃ bhāṣiṣyanti | [SDhPS, 9 18.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 9 19.1]
atha khalu tasyāṃ parṣadi navayānasamprasthitānāmaṣṭānāṃ bodhisattvasahasrāṇāmetadabhavat | [SDhPS, 9 25.1]
na bodhisattvānāmapi tāvadasmābhirevamudāraṃ vyākaraṇaṃ śrutapūrvaṃ kaḥ punarvādaḥ śrāvakāṇām | [SDhPS, 9 25.2]
kaḥ khalvatra heturbhaviṣyati kaḥ pratyaya iti | [SDhPS, 9 25.3]
atha khalu bhagavāṃsteṣāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ cetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya tān bodhisattvānāmantrayāmāsa | [SDhPS, 9 25.4]
samamasmābhiḥ kulaputrā ekakṣaṇe ekamuhūrte mayā ca ānandena ca anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau cittamutpāditaṃ dharmagaganābhyudgatarājasya tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasya saṃmukham | [SDhPS, 9 25.5]
tatraiṣa kulaputrā bāhuśrutye ca satatasamitamabhiyukto 'bhūd ahaṃ ca vīryārambhe 'bhiyuktaḥ | [SDhPS, 9 26.1]
tena mayā kṣiprataramanuttarā samyaksaṃbodhirabhisaṃbuddhā | [SDhPS, 9 27.1]
ayaṃ punarānandabhadro buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ saddharmakośadhara eva bhavati sma | [SDhPS, 9 28.1]
yaduta bodhisattvānāṃ pariniṣpattihetoḥ praṇidhānametatkulaputrā asya kulaputrasyeti | [SDhPS, 9 28.2]
atha khalvāyuṣmānānando bhagavato 'ntikādātmano vyākaraṇaṃ śrutvā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhāv ātmanaśca buddhakṣetraguṇavyūhān śrutvā pūrvapraṇidhānacaryāṃ ca śrutvā tuṣṭa udagra āttamanaskaḥ pramuditaḥ prītisaumanasyajāto 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 9 29.1]
tasmiṃśca samaye bahūnāṃ buddhakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇāṃ saddharmamanusmarati smātmanaśca pūrvapraṇidhānam | [SDhPS, 9 30.1]
atha khalvāyuṣmānānandastasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 9 31.1]
atha khalu bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ rāhulabhadramāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 9 34.1]
bhaviṣyasi tvaṃ rāhulabhadra anāgate 'dhvani saptaratnapadmavikrāntagāmī nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān daśalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāṃstathāgatānarhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhān satkṛtya gurukṛtya mānayitvā pūjayitvā arcayitvā | [SDhPS, 9 34.2]
sadā teṣāṃ buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ jyeṣṭhaputro bhaviṣyasi tadyathāpi nāma mamaitarhi | [SDhPS, 9 35.1]
tasya khalu punā rāhulabhadra bhagavataḥ saptaratnapadmavikrāntagāminastathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasya evaṃrūpamevāyuṣpramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyaty evaṃrūpaiva sarvākāraguṇasaṃpad bhaviṣyati tadyathāpi nāma tasya bhagavataḥ sāgaravaradharabuddhivikrīḍitābhijñasya tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasya sarvākāraguṇopetā buddhakṣetraguṇavyūhā bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 9 36.1]
tasyāpi rāhula sāgaravaradharabuddhivikrīḍitābhijñasya tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasya tvameva jyeṣṭhaputro bhaviṣyasi | [SDhPS, 9 37.1]
tataḥ paścāt pareṇānuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbhotsyasīti | [SDhPS, 9 38.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 9 39.1]
adrākṣītkhalu punarbhagavāṃste dve śrāvakasahasre śaikṣāśaikṣāṇāṃ śrāvakāṇāṃ bhagavantamavalokayamāne abhimukhaṃ prasannacitte mṛducitte mārdavacitte | [SDhPS, 9 44.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyām āyuṣmantamānandamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 9 45.1]
paśyasi tvamānanda ete dve śrāvakasahasre śaikṣāśaikṣāṇāṃ śrāvakāṇām | [SDhPS, 9 45.2]
āha | [SDhPS, 9 45.3]
paśyāmi bhagavan paśyāmi sugata | [SDhPS, 9 45.4]
bhagavānāha | [SDhPS, 9 46.1]
sarva evaite ānanda dve bhikṣusahasre samaṃ bodhisattvacaryāṃ samudānayiṣyanti pañcāśallokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāṃśca buddhān bhagavataḥ satkṛtya gurukṛtya mānayitvā pūjayitvā arcayitvā apacāyitvā saddharmaṃ ca dhārayitvā paścime samucchraye ekakṣaṇenaikamuhūrtenaikalavenaikasaṃnipātena daśasu dikṣvanyonyāsu lokadhātuṣu sveṣu sveṣu buddhakṣetreṣvanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbhotsyante | [SDhPS, 9 46.2]
ratnaketurājā nāma tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhā bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 9 47.1]
paripūrṇaṃ caiṣāṃ kalpamāyuṣpramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 9 48.1]
samāścaiṣāṃ buddhakṣetraguṇavyūhā bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 9 49.1]
samaḥ śrāvakagaṇo bodhisattvagaṇaśca bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 9 50.1]
samaṃ caiṣāṃ parinirvāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 9 51.1]
samaścaiṣāṃ saddharmaḥ sthāsyati | [SDhPS, 9 52.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 9 53.1]
atha khalu te śaikṣāśaikṣāḥ śrāvakā bhagavato 'ntikāt saṃmukhaṃ svāni svāni vyākaraṇāni śrutvā tuṣṭā udagrā āttamanaskāḥ pramuditāḥ prītisaumanasyajātā bhagavantaṃ gāthābhyāmadhyabhāṣanta | [SDhPS, 9 59.1]
tṛptāḥ sma lokapradyota śrutvā vyākaraṇaṃ idam | [SDhPS, 9 60.1]
amṛtena yathā siktāḥ sukhitāḥ sama tathāgata | [SDhPS, 9 60.2]
nāsmākaṃ kāṅkṣā vimatirna bheṣyāma narottamāḥ | [SDhPS, 9 61.1]
adyāsmābhiḥ sukhaṃ prāptaṃ śrutvā vyākaraṇaṃ idam | [SDhPS, 9 61.2]
{SDhPS, 10}
atha khalu bhagavan bhaiṣajyarājaṃ bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvamārabhya tānyaśītiṃ bodhisattvasahasrāṇyāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 10 1.1]
paśyasi tvaṃ bhaiṣajyarāja asyāṃ parṣadi bahudevanāgayakṣagandharvāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragamanuṣyāmanuṣyān bhikṣubhikṣuṇyupāsakopāsikāḥ śrāvakayānīyān pratyekabuddhayānīyān bodhisattvayānīyāṃśca yairayaṃ dharmaparyāyastathāgatasya saṃmukhaṃ śrutaḥ | [SDhPS, 10 1.2]
āha | [SDhPS, 10 1.3]
paśyāmi bhagavan paśyāmi sugata | [SDhPS, 10 1.4]
bhagavānāha | [SDhPS, 10 2.1]
sarve khalvete bhaiṣajyarāja bodhisattvā mahāsattvā yairasyāṃ parṣadi antaśaḥ ekāpi gāthā śrutaikapadamapi śrutaṃ yairvā punarantaśa ekacittotpādenāpy anumoditamidaṃ sūtram | [SDhPS, 10 2.2]
sarvā etā ahaṃ bhaiṣajyarāja catasraḥ parṣado vyākaromyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 10 3.1]
ye 'pi kecid bhaiṣajyarāja tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śroṣyanty antaśa ekagāthāmapi śrutvāntaśa ekenāpi cittotpādena abhyanumodayiṣyanti tānapyahaṃ bhaiṣajyarāja kulaputrān vā kuladuhitṝr vā vyākaromyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 10 4.1]
paripūrṇabuddhakoṭīnayutaśatasahasraparyupāsitāvinaste bhaiṣajyarāja kulaputrā vā kuladuhitaro vā bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 10 5.1]
buddhakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrakṛtapraṇidhānās te bhaiṣajyarāja kulaputrā vā kuladuhitaro vā bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 10 6.1]
sattvānāmanukampārthamasmin jambudvīpe manuṣyeṣu pratyājātā veditavyā ya ito dharmaparyāyādantaśa ekagāthāmapi dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti prakāśayiṣyanti saṃgrāhayiṣyanti likhiṣyanti likhitvā cānusmariṣyanti kālena ca kālaṃ vyavalokayiṣyanti | [SDhPS, 10 7.1]
tasmiṃśca pustake tathāgatagauravamutpādayiṣyanti śāstṛgauraveṇa satkariṣyanti gurukariṣyanti mānayiṣyanti pūjayiṣyanti | [SDhPS, 10 8.1]
taṃ ca pustakaṃ puṣpadhūpagandhamālyavilepanacūrṇacīvaracchatradhvajapatākāvādyādibhir namaskārāñjalikarmabhiśca pūjayiṣyanti | [SDhPS, 10 9.1]
ye kecid bhaiṣajyarāja kulaputrā vā kuladuhitaro vā ito dharmaparyāyādantaśa ekagāthāmapi dhārayiṣyanti anumodayiṣyanti vā sarvāṃstānahaṃ bhaiṣajyarāja vyākaromyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 10 10.1]
tatra bhaiṣajyarāja yaḥ kaścidanyataraḥ puruṣo vā strī vā evaṃ vadet | [SDhPS, 10 11.1]
kīdṛśāḥ khalvapi te sattvā bhaviṣyantyanāgate 'dhvani tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhā iti | [SDhPS, 10 11.2]
tasya bhaiṣajyarāja puruṣasya vā striyā vā sa kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā darśayitavyo ya ito dharmaparyāyādantaśaścatuṣpādikāmapi gāthāṃ dhārayitā śrāvayitā vā deśayitā vā sagauravo veha dharmaparyāye | [SDhPS, 10 11.3]
ayaṃ sa kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā yo hyanāgate 'dhvani tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 10 12.1]
evaṃ paśya | [SDhPS, 10 13.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 10 14.1]
sa hi bhaiṣajyarāja kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā tathāgato veditavyaḥ sadevakena lokena | [SDhPS, 10 14.2]
tasya ca tathāgatasyaivaṃ satkāraḥ kartavyo yaḥ khalvasmāddharmaparyāyādantaśa ekagāthāmapi dhārayet | [SDhPS, 10 15.1]
kaḥ punarvādo ya imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ sakalasamāptam udgṛhṇīyād dhārayedvā vācayedvā paryavāpnuyādvā prakāśayedvā likhedvā likhāpayedvā likhitvā cānusmaret | [SDhPS, 10 15.2]
tatra ca pustake satkāraṃ kuryāt gurukāraṃ kuryāt mānanāṃ pūjanāmarcanāmapacāyanāṃ puṣpadhūpagandhamālyavilepanacūrṇacīvaracchatradhvajapatākāvādyāñjalinamaskāraiḥ praṇāmaiḥ | [SDhPS, 10 16.1]
pariniṣpannaḥ sa bhaiṣajyarāja kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau veditavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 10 17.1]
tathāgatadarśī ca veditavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 10 18.1]
lokasya hitānukampakaḥ praṇidhānavaśenopapanno 'smin jambudvīpe manuṣyeṣu asya dharmaparyāyasya saṃprakāśanatāyai | [SDhPS, 10 19.1]
yaḥ svayamudāraṃ dharmābhisaṃskāramudārāṃ ca buddhakṣetropapattiṃ sthāpayitvā asya dharmaparyāyasya saṃprakāśanahetormayi parinirvṛte sattvānāṃ hitārthamanukampārthaṃ ca ihopapanno veditavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 10 20.1]
tathāgatadūtaḥ sa bhaiṣajyarāja kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā veditavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 10 21.1]
tathāgatakṛtyakarastathāgatasaṃpreṣitaḥ sa bhaiṣajyarāja kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā saṃjñātavyo ya imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya saṃprakāśayed antaśo rahasi cauryeṇāpi kasyacidekasattvasyāpi saṃprakāśayedācakṣīta vā | [SDhPS, 10 22.1]
yaḥ khalu punarbhaiṣajyarāja kaścideva sattvo duṣṭacittaḥ pāpacitto raudracittastathāgatasya saṃmukhaṃ kalpamavarṇaṃ bhāṣed yaśca teṣāṃ tathārūpāṇāṃ dharmabhāṇakānāmasya sūtrāntasya dhārakāṇāṃ gṛhasthānāṃ vā pravrajitānāṃ vā ekāmapi vācamapriyāṃ saṃśrāvayed bhūtāṃ vā abhūtāṃ vedam āgāḍhataraṃ pāpakaṃ karmeti vadāmi | [SDhPS, 10 23.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 10 24.1]
tathāgatābharaṇapratimaṇḍitaḥ sa bhaiṣajyarāja kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā veditavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 10 24.2]
tathāgataṃ sa bhaiṣajyarāja aṃsena pariharati ya imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ likhitvā pustakagataṃ kṛtvā aṃsena pariharati | [SDhPS, 10 25.1]
sa yena yenaiva prakrāmet tena tenaiva sattvair añjalīkaraṇīyaḥ satkartavyo gurukartavyo mānayitavyaḥ pūjayitavyo 'rcayitavyo 'pacāyitavyo divyamānuṣyakaiḥ puṣpadhūpagandhamālyavilepanacūrṇacīvaracchatradhvajapatākāvādyakhādyabhojyānnapānayānair agraprāptaiśca divyai ratnarāśibhiḥ | [SDhPS, 10 26.1]
sa dharmabhāṇakaḥ satkartavyo gurukartavyo mānayitavyaḥ pūjayitavyo divyāśca ratnarāśayastasya dharmabhāṇakasyopanāmayitavyāḥ | [SDhPS, 10 27.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 10 28.1]
apyeva nāma ekavāramapi imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ saṃśrāvayed yaṃ śrutvā aprameyā asaṃkhyeyāḥ sattvāḥ kṣipramanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau pariniṣpadyeyuḥ | [SDhPS, 10 28.2]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 10 29.1]
buddhatve sthātukāmena svayaṃbhūjñānamicchatā | [SDhPS, 10 30.1]
satkartavyāśca te sattvā ye dhārenti imaṃ nayam | [SDhPS, 10 30.2]
ārocayāmi te bhaiṣajyarāja prativedayāmi te | [SDhPS, 10 45.1]
bahavo hi mayā bhaiṣajyarāja dharmaparyāyā bhāṣitā bhāṣāmi bhāṣiṣye ca | [SDhPS, 10 46.1]
sarveṣāṃ ca teṣāṃ bhaiṣajyarāja dharmaparyāyāṇāmayameva dharmaparyāyaḥ sarvalokavipratyanīkaḥ sarvalokāśraddadhanīyaḥ | [SDhPS, 10 47.1]
tathāgatasyāpyetad bhaiṣajyarāja ādhyātmikadharmarahasyaṃ tathāgatabalasaṃrakṣitam apratibhinnapūrvam anācakṣitapūrvam anākhyātam idaṃ sthānam | [SDhPS, 10 48.1]
bahujanapratikṣipto 'yaṃ bhaiṣajyarāja dharmaparyāyastiṣṭhato 'pi tathāgatasya kaḥ punarvādaḥ parinirvṛtasya | [SDhPS, 10 49.1]
api tu khalu punarbhaiṣajyarāja tathāgatacīvaracchannāste kulaputrā vā kuladuhitaro vā veditavyāḥ | [SDhPS, 10 50.1]
anyalokadhātusthitaiśca tathāgatairavalokitāśca adhiṣṭhitāśca | [SDhPS, 10 51.1]
pratyātmikaṃ ca teṣāṃ śraddhābalaṃ bhaviṣyati kuśalamūlabalaṃ ca praṇidhānabalaṃ ca | [SDhPS, 10 52.1]
tathāgatavihāraikasthānanivāsinaśca te bhaiṣajyarāja kulaputrā vā kuladuhitaro vā bhaviṣyanti tathāgatapāṇiparimārjitamūrdhānaśca te bhaviṣyanti ya imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya śraddadhiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti likhiṣyanti satkariṣyanti gurukariṣyanti pareṣāṃ ca saṃśrāvayiṣyanti | [SDhPS, 10 53.1]
yasmin khalu punarbhaiṣajyarāja pṛthivīpradeśe 'yaṃ dharmaparyāyo bhāṣyeta vā deśyeta vā likhyeta vā svādhyāyeta vā saṃgāyeta vā tasmin bhaiṣajyarāja pṛthivīpradeśe tathāgatacaityaṃ kārayitavyaṃ mahantaṃ ratnamayamuccaṃ pragṛhītam | [SDhPS, 10 54.1]
na ca tasminnavaśyaṃ tathāgataśarīrāṇi pratiṣṭhāpayitavyāni | [SDhPS, 10 55.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 10 56.1]
ekaghanameva tasmiṃstathāgataśarīramupanikṣiptaṃ bhavati yasmin pṛthivīpradeśe 'yaṃ dharmaparyāyo bhāṣyeta vā deśyeta vā paṭhyeta vā saṃgāyeta vā likhyeta vā likhito vā pustakagatastiṣṭhet | [SDhPS, 10 56.2]
tasmiṃśca stūpe satkāro gurukāro mānanā pūjanā arcanā karaṇīyā sarvapuṣpadhūpagandhamālyavilepanacūrṇacīvaracchatradhvajapatākāvaijayantībhiḥ | [SDhPS, 10 57.1]
sarvagītavādyanṛtyatūryatālāvacarasaṃgītisaṃpravāditaiḥ pūjā karaṇīyā | [SDhPS, 10 58.1]
ye ca khalu punarbhaiṣajyarāja sattvāstaṃ tathāgatacaityaṃ labheran vandanāya pūjanāya darśanāya vā sarve te bhaiṣajyarāja abhyāsannībhūtā veditavyā anuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodheḥ | [SDhPS, 10 59.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 10 60.1]
bahavo bhaiṣajyarāja gṛhasthāḥ pravrajitāśca bodhisattvacaryāṃ caranti na ca punarimaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ labhante darśanāya vā śravaṇāya vā likhanāya vā pūjanāya vā | [SDhPS, 10 60.2]
na tāvatte bhaiṣajyarāja bodhisattvacaryāyāṃ kuśalā bhavanti yāvannemaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śṛṇvanti | [SDhPS, 10 61.1]
ye tvimaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śṛṇvanti śrutvā cādhimucyanti avataranti vijānanti parigṛhṇanti tasmin samaye te āsannasthāyino bhaviṣyantyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhāvabhyāśībhūtāḥ | [SDhPS, 10 62.1]
tadyathāpi nāma bhaiṣajyarāja kaścideva puruṣo bhavedudakārthī udakagaveṣī | [SDhPS, 10 63.1]
sa udakārtham ujjaṅgale pṛthivīpradeśe udapānaṃ khānayet | [SDhPS, 10 64.1]
sa yāvat paśyecchuṣkaṃ pāṇḍaraṃ pāṃsuṃ nirvāhyamānaṃ tāvajjānīyād dūra itastāvad udakamiti | [SDhPS, 10 65.1]
atha pareṇa samayena sa puruṣa ārdrapāṃsum udakasaṃmiśraṃ kardamapaṅkabhūtam udakabindubhiḥ sravadbhirnirvāhyamānaṃ paśyet tāṃśca puruṣānudapānakhānakān kardamapaṅkadigdhāṅgān atha khalu punarbhaiṣajyarāja sa puruṣastatpūrvanimittaṃ dṛṣṭvā niṣkāṅkṣo bhavennirvicikitsaḥ | [SDhPS, 10 66.1]
āsannamidaṃ khalūdakamiti | [SDhPS, 10 66.2]
evameva bhaiṣajyarāja dūre te bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhavantyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau yāvannemaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śṛṇvanti nodgṛhṇanti nāvataranti nāvagāhante na cintayanti | [SDhPS, 10 67.1]
yadā khalu punarbhaiṣajyarāja bodhisattvā mahāsattvā imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śṛṇvanti udgṛhṇanti dhārayanti vācayanti avataranti svādhyāyanti cintayanti bhāvayanti tadā te 'bhyāśībhūtā bhaviṣyantyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 10 68.1]
sattvānāmito bhaiṣajyarāja dharmaparyāyādanuttarā samyaksaṃbodhirājāyate | [SDhPS, 10 69.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 10 70.1]
paramasaṃdhābhāṣitavivaraṇo hyayaṃ dharmaparyāyastathāgatair arhadbhiḥ samyaksaṃbuddhaiḥ | [SDhPS, 10 70.2]
dharmanigūḍhasthānam ākhyātaṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāṃ pariniṣpattihetoḥ | [SDhPS, 10 71.1]
yaḥ kaścid bhaiṣajyarāja bodhisattvo 'sya dharmaparyāyasyottraset saṃtraset saṃtrāsamāpadyen navayānasamprasthitaḥ sa bhaiṣajyarāja bodhisattvo mahāsattvo veditavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 10 72.1]
sacet punaḥ śrāvakayānīyo 'sya dharmaparyāyasyottraset saṃtraset saṃtrāsamāpadyetādhimānikaḥ sa bhaiṣajyarāja śrāvakayānikaḥ pudgalo veditavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 10 73.1]
yaḥ kaścid bhaiṣajyarāja bodhisattvo mahāsattvastathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya paścime kāle paścime samaye imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ catasṛṇāṃ parṣadāṃ saṃprakāśayet tena bhaiṣajyarāja bodhisattvena mahāsattvena tathāgatalayanaṃ praviśya tathāgatacīvaraṃ prāvṛtya tathāgatasyāsane niṣadya ayaṃ dharmaparyāyaścatasṛṇāṃ parṣadāṃ saṃprakāśayitavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 10 74.1]
katamacca bhaiṣajyarāja tathāgatalayanam | [SDhPS, 10 75.1]
sarvasattvamaitrīvihāraḥ khalu punarbhaiṣajyarāja tathāgatalayanam | [SDhPS, 10 75.2]
tatra tena kulaputreṇa praveṣṭavyam | [SDhPS, 10 76.1]
katamacca bhaiṣajyarāja tathāgatacīvaram | [SDhPS, 10 77.1]
mahākṣāntisauratyaṃ khalu punarbhaiṣajyarāja tathāgatacīvaram | [SDhPS, 10 77.2]
tattena kulaputreṇa vā kuladuhitrā vā prāvaritavyam | [SDhPS, 10 78.1]
katamacca bhaiṣajyarāja tathāgatasya dharmāsanam | [SDhPS, 10 79.1]
sarvadharmaśūnyatāpraveśaḥ khalu punarbhaiṣajyarāja tathāgatasya dharmāsanam | [SDhPS, 10 79.2]
tatra tena kulaputreṇa niṣattavyaṃ niṣadya cāyaṃ dharmaparyāyaścatasṛṇāṃ parṣadāṃ saṃprakāśayitavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 10 80.1]
anavalīnacittena bodhisattvena purastādbodhisattvagaṇasya bodhisattvayānasamprasthitānāṃ catasṛṇāṃ parṣadāṃ saṃprakāśayitavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 10 81.1]
anyalokadhātusthitaścāhaṃ bhaiṣajyarāja tasya kulaputrasya nirmitaiḥ parṣadaḥ samāvartayiṣyāmi | [SDhPS, 10 82.1]
nirmitāṃśca bhikṣubhikṣuṇyupāsakopāsikāḥ saṃpreṣayiṣyāmi dharmaśravaṇāya | [SDhPS, 10 83.1]
te tasya dharmabhāṇakasya bhāṣitaṃ na pratibādhiṣyanti na pratikṣepsyanti | [SDhPS, 10 84.1]
sacetkhalu punararaṇyagato bhaviṣyati tatrāpyahamasya bahudevanāgayakṣagandharvāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragān saṃpreṣayiṣyāmi dharmaśravaṇāya | [SDhPS, 10 85.1]
anyalokadhātusthitaścāhaṃ bhaiṣajyarāja tasya kulaputrasya mukhamupadarśayiṣyāmi | [SDhPS, 10 86.1]
yāni ca asya asmāddharmaparyāyāt padavyañjanāni paribhraṣṭāni bhaviṣyanti tāni tasya svādhyāyataḥ pratyuccārayiṣyāmi | [SDhPS, 10 87.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 10 88.1]
{SDhPS, 11}
atha khalu bhagavataḥ purastāttataḥ pṛthivīpradeśāt parṣanmadhyāt saptaratnamayaḥ stūpo 'bhyudgataḥ pañcayojanaśatānyuccaistvena tadanurūpeṇa ca pariṇāhena | [SDhPS, 11 1.1]
abhyudgamya vaihāyasamantarīkṣe samavātiṣṭhaccitro darśanīyaḥ pañcabhiḥ puṣpagrahaṇīyavedikāsahasraiḥ svabhyalaṃkṛto bahutoraṇasahasraiḥ pratimaṇḍitaḥ patākāvaijayantīsahasrābhiḥ pralambito ratnadāmasahasrābhiḥ pralambitaḥ paṭṭaghaṇṭāsahasraiḥ pralambitaḥ tamālapatracandanagandhaṃ pramuñcamānaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 2.1]
tena ca gandhena sarvāvatīyaṃ lokadhātuḥ saṃmūrchitābhūt | [SDhPS, 11 3.1]
chatrāvalī cāsya yāvaccāturmahārājakāyikadevabhavanāni samucchritābhūt saptaratnamayī tadyathā suvarṇasya rūpyasya vaiḍūryasya musāragalvasyāśmagarbhasya lohitamukteḥ karketanasya | [SDhPS, 11 4]
tasmiṃśca stūpe trāyastriṃśatkāyikā devaputrā divyair māndāravamahāmāndāravaiḥ puṣpaistaṃ ratnastūpamavakiranti adhyavakiranti abhiprakiranti | [SDhPS, 11 5.1]
tasmācca ratnastūpādevaṃrūpaḥ śabdo niścarati sma | [SDhPS, 11 6.1]
sādhu sādhu bhagavan śākyamune | [SDhPS, 11 6.2]
subhāṣitaste 'yaṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīko dharmaparyāyaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 7.1]
evametat bhagavan evametat sugata | [SDhPS, 11 8.1]
atha khalu tāścatasraḥ parṣadastaṃ mahāntaṃ ratnastūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā vaihāyasamantarīkṣe sthitaṃ saṃjātaharṣāḥ prītiprāmodyaprasādaprāptāḥ tasyāṃ velāyāmutthāya āsanebhyo 'ñjaliṃ pragṛhyāvasthitāḥ | [SDhPS, 11 9.1]
atha khalu tasyāṃ velāyāṃ mahāpratibhāno nāma bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sadevamānuṣāsuraṃ lokaṃ kautūhalaprāptaṃ viditvā bhagavantametadavocat | [SDhPS, 11 10.1]
ko bhagavan hetuḥ kaḥ pratyayo 'syaivaṃrūpasya mahāratnastūpasya loke prādurbhāvāya | [SDhPS, 11 10.2]
ko vā bhagavan asmānmahāratnastūpādevaṃrūpaṃ śabdaṃ niścārayati | [SDhPS, 11 10.3]
evamukte bhagavān mahāpratibhānaṃ bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvametadavocat | [SDhPS, 11 10.4]
asmin mahāpratibhāna mahāratnastūpe tathāgatasyātmabhāvastiṣṭhati ekaghanaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 10.5]
tasyaiṣa stūpaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 11.1]
sa eṣa śabdaṃ niścārayati | [SDhPS, 11 12.1]
asti mahāpratibhānādhastāyāṃ diśi asaṃkhyeyāni lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇyatikramya ratnaviśuddhā nāma lokadhātuḥ | [SDhPS, 11 13.1]
tasyāṃ prabhūtaratno nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 11 14.1]
tasyaitadbhagavataḥ pūrvapraṇidhānamabhūt | [SDhPS, 11 15.1]
ahaṃ khalu pūrvaṃ bodhisattvacaryāṃ caramāṇo na tāvanniryāto 'nuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau yāvanmayāyaṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīko dharmaparyāyo bodhisattvāvavādo na śruto 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 11 15.2]
yadā tu mayā ayaṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīko dharmaparyāyaḥ śrutas tadā paścādahaṃ pariniṣpanno 'bhūvamanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 11 16.1]
tena khalu punarmahāpratibhāna bhagavatā prabhūtaratnena tathāgatenārhatā samyaksaṃbuddhena parinirvāṇakālasamaye sadevakasya lokasya samārakasya sabrahmakasya saśramaṇabrāhmaṇikāyāḥ prajāyāḥ purastādevamārocitam | [SDhPS, 11 17.1]
