mama khalu bhikṣavaḥ parinirvṛtasya asya tathāgatātmabhāvavigrahasya eko mahāratnastūpaḥ kartavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 17.2]
śeṣāḥ punaḥ stūpā mamoddiśya kartavyāḥ | [SDhPS, 11 18.1]
tasya khalu punarmahāpratibhāna bhagavataḥ prabhūtaratnasya tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasyaitadadhiṣṭhānamabhūt | [SDhPS, 11 19.1]
ayaṃ mama stūpo daśasu dikṣu sarvalokadhātuṣu yeṣu buddhakṣetreṣvayaṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīko dharmaparyāyaḥ saṃprakāśyeta teṣu teṣvayaṃ mamātmabhāvavigrahastūpaḥ samabhyudgacchet | [SDhPS, 11 19.2]
taistairbuddhairbhagavadbhirasmin saddharmapuṇḍarīke dharmaparyāye bhāṣyamāṇe parṣanmaṇḍalasyopari vaihāyasaṃ tiṣṭhet | [SDhPS, 11 20.1]
teṣāṃ ca buddhānāṃ bhagavatāmimaṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ bhāṣamāṇānāmayaṃ mamātmabhāvavigrahastūpaḥ sādhukāraṃ dadyāt | [SDhPS, 11 21.1]
tadayaṃ mahāpratibhāna tasya bhagavataḥ prabhūtaratnasya tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasya śarīrastūpaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 22.1]
asyāṃ sahāyāṃ lokadhātau asmin saddharmapuṇḍarīke dharmaparyāye mayā bhāṣyamāṇe 'smāt parṣanmaṇḍalamadhyādabhyudgamya uparyantarīkṣe vaihāyasaṃ sthitvā sādhukāraṃ dadāti sma | [SDhPS, 11 23.1]
atha khalu mahāpratibhāno bodhisattvo mahāsattvo bhagavantametadavocat | [SDhPS, 11 24.1]
paśyāma vayaṃ bhagavan etaṃ tathāgatavigrahaṃ bhagavato 'nubhāvena | [SDhPS, 11 24.2]
evamukte bhagavān mahāpratibhānaṃ bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvametadavocat | [SDhPS, 11 25.1]
tasya khalu punarmahāpratibhāna bhagavataḥ prabhūtaratnasya tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasya praṇidhānaṃ gurukamabhūt | [SDhPS, 11 25.2]
etadasya praṇidhānam | [SDhPS, 11 26.1]
yadā khalvanyeṣu buddhakṣetreṣu buddhā bhagavanta imaṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ bhāṣeyus tadāyaṃ mamātmabhāvavigrahastūpo 'sya saddharmapuṇḍarīkasya dharmaparyāyasya śravaṇāya gacchet tathāgatānāmantikam | [SDhPS, 11 26.2]
yadā punaste buddhā bhagavanto mamātmabhāvavigraham udghāṭya darśayitukāmā bhaveyuścatasṛṇāṃ parṣadām atha taistathāgatairdaśasu dikṣvanyonyeṣu buddhakṣetreṣu ya ātmabhāvanirmitāstathāgatavigrahā anyānyanāmadheyās teṣu teṣu buddhakṣetreṣu sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśayanti tān sarvān saṃnipātya tairātmabhāvanirmitaistathāgatavigrahaiḥ sārdhaṃ paścādayaṃ mamātmabhāvavigrahastūpaḥ samudghāṭya upadarśayitavyaścatasṛṇāṃ parṣadām | [SDhPS, 11 27.1]
tanmayāpi mahāpratibhāna bahavastathāgatavigrahā nirmitā ye daśasu dikṣvanyonyeṣu buddhakṣetreṣu lokadhātusahasreṣu sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśayanti | [SDhPS, 11 28.1]
te sarve khalvihānayitavyā bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 11 29.1]
atha khalu mahāpratibhāno bodhisattvo mahāsattvo bhagavantametadavocat | [SDhPS, 11 30.1]
tānapi tāvad bhagavaṃstathāgatātmabhāvāṃstathāgatanirmitān sarvān vandāmahai | [SDhPS, 11 30.2]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmūrṇākośādraśmiṃ prāmuñcad yayā raśmyā samanantarapramuktayā pūrvasyāṃ diśi pañcāśatsu gaṅgānadīvālukāsameṣu lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu ye buddhā bhagavanto viharanti sma te sarve saṃdṛśyante sma | [SDhPS, 11 31.1]
tāni ca buddhakṣetrāṇi sphaṭikamayāni saṃdṛśyante sma ratnavṛkṣaiśca citrāṇi saṃdṛśyante sma dūṣyapaṭṭadāmasamalaṃkṛtāni bahubodhisattvaśatasahasraparipūrṇāni vitānavitatāni saptaratnahemajālapraticchannāni | [SDhPS, 11 32.1]
teṣu teṣu buddhā bhagavanto madhureṇa valgunā svareṇa sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśayamānāḥ saṃdṛśyante sma | [SDhPS, 11 33.1]
bodhisattvaśatasahasraiśca paripūrṇāni tāni buddhakṣetrāṇi saṃdṛśyante sma | [SDhPS, 11 34.1]
evaṃ pūrvadakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi | [SDhPS, 11 35.1]
evaṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi | [SDhPS, 11 36.1]
evaṃ dakṣiṇapaścimāyāṃ diśi | [SDhPS, 11 37.1]
evaṃ paścimāyāṃ diśi | [SDhPS, 11 38.1]
evaṃ paścimottarāyāṃ diśi | [SDhPS, 11 39.1]
evamuttarāyāṃ diśi | [SDhPS, 11 40.1]
evamuttarapūrvasyāṃ diśi | [SDhPS, 11 41.1]
evamadhastāyāṃ diśi | [SDhPS, 11 42.1]
evamūrdhvāyāṃ diśi | [SDhPS, 11 43.1]
evaṃ samantāddaśasu dikṣu ekaikasyāṃ diśi bahūni gaṅgānadīvālukopamāni buddhakṣetrakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi bahuṣu gaṅgānadīvālukopameṣu lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu ye buddhā bhagavantastiṣṭhanti te sarve saṃdṛśyante sma | [SDhPS, 11 44.1]
atha khalu te daśasu dikṣu tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ svān svān bodhisattvagaṇānāmantrayanti sma | [SDhPS, 11 45.1]
gantavyaṃ khalu punaḥ kulaputrā bhaviṣyati asmābhiḥ sahāṃ lokadhātuṃ bhagavataḥ śākyamunestathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasyāntikaṃ prabhūtaratnasya tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasya śarīrastūpavandanāya | [SDhPS, 11 45.2]
atha khalu te buddhā bhagavantaḥ svaiḥ svairupasthāyakaiḥ sārdhamātmadvitīyā ātmatṛtīyā imāṃ sahāṃ lokadhātumāgacchanti sma | [SDhPS, 11 46.1]
iti hi tasmin samaye iyaṃ sarvāvatī lokadhātū ratnavṛkṣapratimaṇḍitābhūd vaiḍūryamayī saptaratnahemajālasaṃchannā mahāratnagandhadhūpanadhūpitā māndāravamahāmāndāravapuṣpasaṃstīrṇā kiṅkiṇījālālaṃkṛtā suvarṇasūtrāṣṭāpadanibaddhā apagatagrāmanagaranigamajanapadarāṣṭrarājadhānī apagatakālaparvatā apagatamucilindamahāmucilindaparvatā apagatacakravālamahācakravālaparvatā apagatasumeruparvatā apagatatadanyamahāparvatā apagatamahāsamudrā apagatanadīmahānadīparisaṃsthitābhūd apagatadevamanuṣyāsurakāyā apagatanirayatiryagyoniyamalokā | [SDhPS, 11 47.1]
iti hi tasmin samaye ye 'syāṃ sahāyāṃ lokadhātau ṣaḍgatyupapannāḥ sattvās te sarve 'nyeṣu lokadhātuṣūpanikṣiptā abhūvan sthāpayitvā ye tasyāṃ parṣadi saṃnipatitā abhūvan | [SDhPS, 11 48.1]
atha khalu te buddhā bhagavanta upasthāyakadvitīyā upasthāyakatṛtīyā imāṃ sahāṃ lokadhātumāgacchanti sma | [SDhPS, 11 49.1]
āgatāgatāśca te tathāgatā ratnavṛkṣamūle siṃhāsanamupaniśritya viharanti sma | [SDhPS, 11 50.1]
ekaikaśca ratnavṛkṣaḥ pañcayojanaśatānyuccaistvenābhūt anupūrvaśākhāpatrapalāśapariṇāhaḥ puṣpaphalapratimaṇḍitaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 51.1]
ekaikasmiṃśca ratnavṛkṣamūle siṃhāsanaṃ prajñaptamabhūt pañcayojanaśatānyuccaistvena mahāratnapratimaṇḍitam | [SDhPS, 11 52.1]
tasminnekaikastathāgataḥ paryaṅkaṃ baddhvā niṣaṇṇo 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 11 53.1]
anena paryāyeṇa sarvasyāṃ trisāhasramahāsāhasrāyāṃ lokadhātau sarvaratnavṛkṣamūleṣu tathāgatāḥ paryaṅkaṃ baddhvā niṣaṇṇā abhūvan | [SDhPS, 11 54.1]
tena khalu punaḥ samayena iyaṃ trisāhasramahāsāhasrī lokadhātustathāgataparipūrṇābhūt | [SDhPS, 11 55.1]
na tāvad bhagavataḥ śākyamunestathāgatasyātmabhāvanirmitā ekasmādapi digbhāgāt sarva āgatā abhūvan | [SDhPS, 11 56.1]
atha khalu punarbhagavān śākyamunistathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhasteṣāṃ tathāgatavigrahāṇām āgatāgatānām avakāśaṃ nirmimīte sma | [SDhPS, 11 57.1]
samantādaṣṭabhyo digbhyo viṃśatibuddhakṣetrakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi sarvāṇi vaiḍūryamayāni saptaratnahemajālasaṃchannāni kiṅkiṇījālālaṃkṛtāni māndāravamahāmāndāravapuṣpasaṃstīrṇāni divyavitānavitatāni divyapuṣpadāmābhipralambitāni divyagandhadhūpanadhūpitāni | [SDhPS, 11 58.1]
sarvāṇi ca tāni viṃśatibuddhakṣetrakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇy apagatagrāmanagaranigamajanapadarāṣṭrarājadhānīni apagatakālaparvatāni apagatamucilindamahāmucilindaparvatāni apagatacakravālamahācakravālaparvatāni apagatasumeruparvatāni apagatatadanyamahāparvatāni apagatamahāsamudrāṇi apagatanadīmahānadīni parisaṃsthāpayati apagatadevamanuṣyāsurakāyāni apagatanirayatiryagyoniyamalokāni | [SDhPS, 11 59.1]
tāni ca sarvāṇi bahubuddhakṣetrāṇi ekameva buddhakṣetramekameva pṛthivīpradeśaṃ parisaṃsthāpayāmāsa samaṃ ramaṇīyaṃ saptaratnamayaiśca vṛkṣaiścitritam | [SDhPS, 11 60.1]
teṣāṃ ca ratnavṛkṣāṇāṃ pañcayojanaśatānyārohapariṇāho 'nupūrvaśākhāpatrapuṣpaphalopetaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 61.1]
sarvasmiṃśca ratnavṛkṣamūle pañcayojanaśatānyārohapariṇāhaṃ divyaratnamayaṃ vicitraṃ darśanīyaṃ siṃhāsanaṃ prajñaptamabhūt | [SDhPS, 11 62.1]
teṣu ratnavṛkṣamūleṣv āgatāgatāstathāgatāḥ siṃhāsaneṣu paryaṅkaṃ baddhvā niṣīdante sma | [SDhPS, 11 63.1]
anena paryāyeṇa punaraparāṇi viṃśatilokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇy ekaikasyāṃ diśi śākyamunistathāgataḥ pariśodhayati sma teṣāṃ tathāgatānām āgatānām avakāśārtham | [SDhPS, 11 64.1]
tānyapi viṃśatilokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇy ekaikasyāṃ diśi apagatagrāmanagaranigamajanapadarāṣṭrarājadhānīni apagatakālaparvatāni apagatamucilindamahāmucilindaparvatāni apagatacakravālamahācakravālaparvatāni apagatasumeruparvatāni apagatatadanyamahāparvatāni apagatamahāsamudrāṇi apagatanadīmahānadīni parisaṃsthāpayati apagatadevamanuṣyāsurakāyāni apagatanirayatiryagyoniyamalokāni | [SDhPS, 11 65.1]
te ca sarvasattvā anyeṣu lokadhātuṣūpanikṣiptāḥ | [SDhPS, 11 66.1]
tānyapi buddhakṣetrāṇi vaiḍūryamayāni saptaratnahemajālapraticchannāni kiṅkiṇījālālaṃkṛtāni māndāravamahāmāndāravapuṣpasaṃstīrṇāni divyavitānavitatāni divyapuṣpadāmābhipralambitāni divyagandhadhūpanadhūpitāni ratnavṛkṣopaśobhitāni | [SDhPS, 11 67.1]
sarve ca te ratnavṛkṣāḥ pañcayojanaśatapramāṇāḥ | [SDhPS, 11 68.1]
pañcayojanapramāṇāni ca siṃhāsanānyabhinirmitāni | [SDhPS, 11 69.1]
tataste tathāgatā niṣīdante sma pṛthak pṛthak siṃhāsaneṣu ratnavṛkṣamūleṣu paryaṅkaṃ baddhvā | [SDhPS, 11 70.1]
tena khalu punaḥ samayena bhagavatā śākyamuninā ye nirmitāstathāgatāḥ pūrvasyāṃ diśi sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśayanti sma gaṅgānadīvālukopameṣu buddhakṣetrakoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu te sarve samāgatā daśabhyo digbhyaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 71.1]
te cāgatā aṣṭāsu dikṣu niṣaṇṇā abhūvan | [SDhPS, 11 72.1]
tena khalu punaḥ samayenaikaikasyāṃ diśi triṃśallokadhātukoṭīśatasahasrāṇyaṣṭabhyo digbhyaḥ samantāttaistathāgatairākrāntā abhūvan | [SDhPS, 11 73.1]
atha khalu te tathāgatāḥ sveṣu sveṣu siṃhāsaneṣūpaviṣṭāḥ svān svānupasthāyakān saṃpreṣayanti sma bhagavataḥ śākyamunerantikam | [SDhPS, 11 74.1]
ratnapuṣpapuṭān dattvā evaṃ vadanti sma | [SDhPS, 11 75.1]
gacchata yūyaṃ gṛdhrakūṭaṃ parvatam | [SDhPS, 11 75.2]
gatvā ca punastasmiṃstaṃ bhagavantaṃ śākyamuniṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ vanditvā asmadvacanād alpābādhatāṃ mandaglānatāṃ ca balaṃ ca sparśavihāratāṃ ca paripṛcchadhvaṃ sārdhaṃ bodhisattvagaṇena śrāvakagaṇena | [SDhPS, 11 76.1]
anena ca ratnarāśinā abhyavakiradhvam evaṃ ca vadadhvam | [SDhPS, 11 77.1]
dadāti khalu punarbhagavāṃstathāgataśchandamasya mahāratnastūpasya samudghāṭane | [SDhPS, 11 77.2]
evaṃ te tathāgatāḥ sarve svān svānupasthāyakān saṃpreṣayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 11 78.1]
atha khalu bhagavān śākyamunistathāgatastasyāṃ velāyāṃ svānnirmitānaśeṣataḥ samāgatān viditvā pṛthakpṛthak siṃhāsaneṣu niṣaṇṇāṃśca viditvā tāṃścopasthāyakāṃsteṣāṃ tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāmāgatān viditvā chandaṃ ca taistathāgatairarhadbhiḥ samyaksaṃbuddhairārocitaṃ viditvā tasyāṃ velāyāṃ svakāddharmāsanādutthāya vaihāyasamantarīkṣe 'tiṣṭhat | [SDhPS, 11 79.1]
tāśca sarvāścatasraḥ pariṣadaḥ utthāyāsanebhyo 'ñjalīḥ parigṛhya bhagavato mukham ullokayantyastasthuḥ | [SDhPS, 11 80.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstaṃ mahāntaṃ ratnastūpaṃ vaihāyasaṃ sthitaṃ dakṣiṇayā hastāṅgulyā madhye samudghāṭayati sma | [SDhPS, 11 81.1]
samudghāṭya ca dve bhittī pravisārayati sma | [SDhPS, 11 82.1]
tadyathāpi nāma mahānagaradvāreṣu mahākapāṭasaṃpuṭāvargalavimuktau pravisāryete evameva bhagavāṃstaṃ mahāntaṃ ratnastūpaṃ vaihāyasaṃ sthitaṃ dakṣiṇayā hastāṅgulyā madhye samudghāṭya apāvṛṇoti sma | [SDhPS, 11 83.1]
samanantaravivṛtasya khalu punastasya mahāratnastūpasyātha khalu bhagavān prabhūtaratnastathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ siṃhāsanopaviṣṭaḥ paryaṅkaṃ baddhvā pariśuṣkagātraḥ saṃghaṭitakāyo yathā samādhisamāpannastathā saṃdṛśyate sma | [SDhPS, 11 84.1]
evaṃ ca vācamabhāṣata | [SDhPS, 11 85.1]
sādhu sādhu bhagavan śākyamune | [SDhPS, 11 85.2]
subhāṣitaste 'yaṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīko dharmaparyāyaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 86.1]
sādhu khalu punastvaṃ bhagavan śākyamune yastvamimaṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ parṣanmadhye bhāṣase | [SDhPS, 11 87.1]
asyaivāhaṃ bhagavan saddharmapuṇḍarīkasya dharmaparyāyasya śravaṇāyehāgataḥ | [SDhPS, 11 88.1]
atha khalu tāścatasraḥ parṣadastaṃ bhagavantaṃ prabhūtaratnaṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ bahukalpakoṭīnayutaśatasahasraparinirvṛtaṃ tathā bhāṣamāṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā āścaryaprāptā adbhutaprāptā abhūvan | [SDhPS, 11 89.1]
tasyāṃ velāyāṃ taṃ bhagavantaṃ prabhūtaratnaṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ taṃ ca bhagavantaṃ śākyamuniṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ divyamānuṣyakai ratnarāśibhirabhyavakiranti sma | [SDhPS, 11 90.1]
atha khalu bhagavān prabhūtaratnastathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho bhagavataḥ śākyamunestathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasya tasminneva siṃhāsane 'rdhāsanamadāsīt tasyaiva mahāratnastūpābhyantara evaṃ ca vadati | [SDhPS, 11 91.1]
ihaiva bhagavān śākyamunistathāgato niṣīdatu | [SDhPS, 11 91.2]
atha khalu bhagavān śākyamunistathāgatastasminnardhāsane niṣasāda tenaiva tathāgatena sārdham | [SDhPS, 11 92.1]
ubhau ca tau tathāgatau tasya mahāratnastūpasya madhye siṃhāsanopaviṣṭau vaihāyasamantarīkṣasthau saṃdṛśyete | [SDhPS, 11 93.1]
atha khalu tāsāṃ catasṛṇāṃ parṣadāmetadabhavat | [SDhPS, 11 94.1]
dūrasthā vayamābhyāṃ tathāgatābhyām | [SDhPS, 11 94.2]
yannūnaṃ vayamapi tathāgatānubhāvena vaihāyasamabhyudgacchema iti | [SDhPS, 11 95.1]
atha khalu bhagavān śākyamunistathāgatastāsāṃ catasṛṇāṃ parṣadāṃ cetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya tasyāṃ velāyāmṛddhibalena tāścatasraḥ parṣado vaihāyasamuparyantarīkṣe pratiṣṭhāpayati sma | [SDhPS, 11 96.1]
atha khalu bhagavān śākyamunistathāgatastasyāṃ velāyāṃ tāścatasraḥ parṣada āmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 11 97.1]
ko bhikṣavo yuṣmākamutsahate tasyāṃ sahāyāṃ lokadhātau imaṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ saṃprakāśayitum | [SDhPS, 11 97.2]
ayaṃ sa kālo 'yaṃ sa samayaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 97.3]
saṃmukhībhūtastathāgataḥ | [SDhPS, 11 98.1]
parinirvāyitukāmo bhikṣavastathāgata imaṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ dharmaparyāyamupanikṣipya | [SDhPS, 11 99.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 11 100.1]
atha khalu bhagavān kṛtsnaṃ bodhisattvagaṇaṃ sasurāsuraṃ ca lokamāmantryaitadavocat | [SDhPS, 11 142.1]
bhūtapūrvaṃ bhikṣavo 'tīte 'dhvani ahamaprameyāsaṃkhyeyān kalpān saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ sūtraṃ paryeṣitavān akhinno 'viśrāntaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 142.2]
pūrvaṃ ca ahamanekān kalpānanekāni kalpaśatasahasrāṇi rājābhūvamanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau kṛtapraṇidhānaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 143.1]
na ca me cittavyāvṛttirabhūt | [SDhPS, 11 144.1]
ṣaṇṇāṃ ca pāramitānāṃ paripūryā udyukto 'bhūvamaprameyadānapradaḥ suvarṇamaṇimuktāvaidūryaśaṅkhaśilāpravālajātarūparajatāśmagarbhamusāragalvalohitamuktāgrāmanagaranigamajanapadarāṣṭrarājadhānībhāryāputraduhitṛdāsīdāsakarmakarapauruṣeyahastyaśvarathaṃ yāvadātmaśarīraparityāgī karacaraṇaśirottamāṅgapratyaṅgajīvitadātā | [SDhPS, 11 145.1]
na ca me kadācidāgrahacittamutpannam | [SDhPS, 11 146.1]
tena ca samayena ayaṃ loko dīrghāyur abhūt | [SDhPS, 11 147.1]
anekavarṣaśatasahasrajīvitena ca ahaṃ kālena dharmārthaṃ rājyaṃ kāritavān na viṣayārtham | [SDhPS, 11 148.1]
so 'haṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ kumāraṃ rājye 'bhiṣicya caturdiśaṃ jyeṣṭhadharmagaveṣaṇāya udyukto 'bhūvam | [SDhPS, 11 149.1]
evaṃ ghaṇṭayā ghoṣāpayitavān | [SDhPS, 11 150.1]
yo me jyeṣṭhaṃ dharmamanupradāsyaty arthaṃ cākhyāsyati tasyāhaṃ dāso bhūyāsam | [SDhPS, 11 150.2]
tena ca kālena ṛṣirabhūt | [SDhPS, 11 151.1]
sa māmetadavocat | [SDhPS, 11 152.1]
asti mahārāja saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ nāma sūtraṃ jyeṣṭhadharmanirdeśakam | [SDhPS, 11 152.2]
tadyadi dāsyamabhyupagacchasi tataste 'haṃ taṃ dharmaṃ śrāvayiṣyāmi | [SDhPS, 11 153.1]
so 'haṃ śrutvā tasyarṣervacanaṃ hṛṣṭastuṣṭa udagra āttamanāḥ prītisaumanasyajāto yena sa ṛṣistenopeyivān | [SDhPS, 11 154.1]
upetyāvocat | [SDhPS, 11 155.1]
yatte dāsena karma karaṇīyaṃ tatkaromi | [SDhPS, 11 155.2]
so 'haṃ tasyarṣerdāsabhāvamabhyupetya tṛṇakāṣṭhapānīyakandamūlaphalādīni preṣyakarmāṇi kṛtavān yāvad dvārādhyakṣo 'pyahamāsam | [SDhPS, 11 156.1]
divasaṃ caivaṃvidhaṃ karma kṛtvā rātrau śayānasya mañcake pādān dhārayāmi | [SDhPS, 11 157.1]
na ca me kāyaklamo na cetasi klamo 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 11 158.1]
evaṃ ca me kurvataḥ paripūrṇaṃ varṣāsahasraṃ gatam | [SDhPS, 11 159.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmetamevārthaṃ paridyotayannimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 11 160.1]
tatkiṃ manyadhve bhikṣavo 'nyaḥ sa tena kālena tena samayena rājābhūt | [SDhPS, 11 166.1]
na khalu punarevaṃ draṣṭavyam | [SDhPS, 11 166.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 11 167.1]
ahaṃ sa tena kālena tena samayena rājābhūvam | [SDhPS, 11 167.2]
syātkhalu punarbhikṣavo 'nyaḥ sa tena kālena tena samayenarṣirabhūt | [SDhPS, 11 168.1]
na khalu punarevaṃ draṣṭavyam | [SDhPS, 11 168.2]
ayameva sa tena kālena tena samayena devadatto bhikṣurṛṣirabhūt | [SDhPS, 11 169.1]
devadatto hi bhikṣavo mama kalyāṇamitram | [SDhPS, 11 170.1]
devadattameva cāgamya mayā ṣaṭ pāramitāḥ paripūritā mahāmaitrī mahākaruṇā mahāmuditā mahopekṣā | [SDhPS, 11 171.1]
dvātriṃśanmahāpuruṣalakṣaṇāni aśītyanuvyañjanāni suvarṇavarṇacchavitā daśa balāni catvāri vaiśāradyāni catvāri saṃgrahavastūni aṣṭādaśāveṇikabuddhadharmā maharddhibalatā daśadiksattvanistāraṇatā sarvam etad devadattam āgamya | [SDhPS, 11 172.1]
ārocayāmi vo bhikṣavaḥ prativedayāmi | [SDhPS, 11 173.1]
eṣa devadatto bhikṣuranāgate 'dhvani aprameyaiḥ kalpairasaṃkhyeyairdevarājo nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho bhaviṣyati vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca bhagavān devasopānāyāṃ lokadhātau | [SDhPS, 11 173.2]
devarājasya khalu punarbhikṣavastathāgatasya viṃśatyantarakalpānāyuṣpramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 11 174.1]
vistareṇa ca dharmaṃ deśayiṣyati | [SDhPS, 11 175.1]
gaṅgānadīvālukāsamāśca sattvāḥ sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkariṣyanti | [SDhPS, 11 176.1]
aneke ca sattvāḥ pratyekabodhau cittamutpādayiṣyanti | [SDhPS, 11 177.1]
gaṅgānadīvālukāsamāśca sattvā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau cittamutpādayiṣyanty avaivartikakṣāntipratilabdhāśca bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 11 178.1]
devarājasya khalu punarbhikṣavastathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya viṃśatyantarakalpān saddharmaḥ sthāsyati | [SDhPS, 11 179.1]
na ca śarīraṃ dhātubhedena bhetsyate | [SDhPS, 11 180.1]
ekaghanaṃ cāsya śarīraṃ bhaviṣyati saptaratnastūpaṃ praviṣṭam | [SDhPS, 11 181.1]
sa ca stūpaḥ ṣaṣṭiyojanaśatānyuccaistvena bhaviṣyati catvāriṃśadyojanānyāyāmena | [SDhPS, 11 182.1]
sarve ca tatra devamanuṣyāḥ pūjāṃ kariṣyanti puṣpadhūpagandhamālyavilepanacūrṇacīvaracchatradhvajapatākābhir gāthābhiḥ | [SDhPS, 11 183.1]
tena cābhiṣṭoṣyanti | [SDhPS, 11 184.1]
ye ca taṃ stūpaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kariṣyanti praṇāmaṃ vā teṣāṃ kecid agraphalamarhattvaṃ sākṣātkariṣyanti kecit pratyekabodhimanuprāpsyante acintyāścāprameyā devamanuṣyā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau cittānyutpādya avinivartanīyā bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 11 185.1]
atha khalu bhagavān punareva bhikṣusaṃghamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 11 186.1]
yaḥ kaścit bhikṣavo 'nāgate 'dhvani kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā imaṃ saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ sūtraparivartaṃ śroṣyati śrutvā ca na kāṅkṣiṣyati na vicikitsiṣyati viśuddhacittaścādhimokṣyate tena tisṛṇāṃ durgatīnāṃ dvāraṃ pithitaṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 11 186.2]
narakatiryagyoniyamalokopapattiṣu na patiṣyati | [SDhPS, 11 186.3]
daśadigbuddhakṣetropapannaścedameva sūtraṃ janmani janmani śroṣyati | [SDhPS, 11 187.1]
devamanuṣyalokopapannasya cāsya viśiṣṭasthānaprāptirbhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 11 188.1]
yasmiṃśca buddhakṣetra upapatsyate tasminnaupapāduke saptaratnamaye padme upapatsyate tathāgatasya saṃmukham | [SDhPS, 11 189.1]
atha khalu tasyāṃ velāyāmadhastāddiśaḥ prabhūtaratnasya tathāgatasya buddhakṣetrādāgataḥ prajñākūṭo nāma bodhisattvaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 190.1]
sa taṃ prabhūtaratnaṃ tathāgatametadavocat | [SDhPS, 11 191.1]
gacchāmo bhagavan svakaṃ buddhakṣetram | [SDhPS, 11 191.2]
atha khalu bhagavān śākyamunistathāgataḥ prajñākūṭaṃ bodhisattvametadavocat | [SDhPS, 11 192.1]
muhūrtaṃ tāvat kulaputra āgamayasva yāvanmadīyena bodhisattvena mañjuśriyā kumārabhūtena sārdhaṃ kaṃcideva dharmaviniścayaṃ kṛtvā paścāt svakaṃ buddhakṣetraṃ gamiṣyasi | [SDhPS, 11 192.2]
atha khalu tasyāṃ velāyāṃ mañjuśrīḥ kumārabhūtaḥ sahasrapatre padme śakaṭacakrapramāṇamātre niṣaṇṇo 'nekabodhisattvaparivṛtaḥ puraskṛtaḥ samudramadhyāt sāgaranāgarājabhavanādabhyudgamya upari vaihāyasaṃ khagapathena gṛdhrakūṭe parvate bhagavato 'ntikamupasaṃkrāntaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 193.1]
atha mañjuśrīḥ kumārabhūtaḥ padmādavatīrya bhagavataḥ śākyamuneḥ prabhūtaratnasya ca tathāgatasya pādau śirasābhivanditvā yena prajñākūṭo bodhisattvastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 194.1]
upasaṃkramya prajñākūṭena bodhisattvena sārdhaṃ saṃmukhaṃ saṃmodanīṃ saṃrañjanīṃ vividhāṃ kathāmupasaṃgṛhya ekānte nyaṣīdat | [SDhPS, 11 195.1]
atha khalu prajñākūṭo bodhisattvo mañjuśriyaṃ kumārabhūtametadavocat | [SDhPS, 11 196.1]
samudramadhyagatena tvayā mañjuśrīḥ kiyān sattvadhāturvinītaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 196.2]
mañjuśrīrāha | [SDhPS, 11 196.3]
anekānyaprameyāṇyasaṃkhyeyāni sattvāni vinītāni | [SDhPS, 11 196.4]
tāvadaprameyāṇyasaṃkhyeyāni yāvadvācā na śakyaṃ vijñāpayituṃ cittena vā cintayitum | [SDhPS, 11 197.1]
muhūrtaṃ tāvat kulaputra āgamayasva yāvat pūrvanimittaṃ drakṣyasi | [SDhPS, 11 198.1]
samanantarabhāṣitā ceyaṃ mañjuśriyā kumārabhūtena vāk tasyāṃ velāyāmanekāni padmasahasrāṇi samudramadhyādabhyudgatāni upari vaihāyasam | [SDhPS, 11 199.1]
teṣu ca padmeṣvanekāni bodhisattvasahasrāṇi saṃniṣaṇṇāni | [SDhPS, 11 200.1]
atha te bodhisattvāstenaiva khagapathena yena gṛdhrakūṭaḥ parvatastenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [SDhPS, 11 201.1]
upasaṃkramya tataścopari vaihāyasaṃ sthitāḥ saṃdṛśyante sma | [SDhPS, 11 202.1]
sarve ca te mañjuśriyā kumārabhūtena vinītā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 11 203.1]
tatra ye bodhisattvā mahāyānasamprasthitāḥ pūrvamabhūvaṃs te mahāyānaguṇān ṣaṭ pāramitāḥ saṃvarṇayanti | [SDhPS, 11 204.1]
ye śrāvakapūrvā bodhisattvāste śrāvakayānameva saṃvarṇayanti | [SDhPS, 11 205.1]
sarve ca te sarvadharmān śūnyāniti saṃjānanti sma mahāyānaguṇāṃśca | [SDhPS, 11 206.1]
atha khalu mañjuśrīḥ kumārabhūtaḥ prajñākūṭaṃ bodhisattvametadavocat | [SDhPS, 11 207.1]
sarvo 'yaṃ kulaputra mayā samudramadhyagatena sattvavinayaḥ kṛtaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 207.2]
sa cāyaṃ saṃdṛśyate | [SDhPS, 11 208.1]
atha khalu prajñākūṭo bodhisattvo mañjuśriyaṃ kumārabhūtaṃ gāthābhigītena paripṛcchati | [SDhPS, 11 209.1]
mahābhadra prajñayā sūranāman asaṃkhyeyā ye vinītāstvayādya | [SDhPS, 11 210.1]
sattvā amī kasya cāyaṃ prabhāvas tadbrūhi pṛṣṭo naradeva tvametat | [SDhPS, 11 210.2]
kaṃ vā dharmaṃ deśitavānasi tvaṃ kiṃ vā sūtraṃ bodhimārgopadeśam | [SDhPS, 11 211.1]
yacchrutvāmī bodhaye jātacittāḥ sarvajñatve niścitaṃ labdhagādhāḥ | [SDhPS, 11 211.2]
mañjuśrīrāha | [SDhPS, 11 212.1]
samudramadhye saddharmapuṇḍarīkaṃ sūtraṃ bhāṣitavān na cānyat | [SDhPS, 11 212.2]
prajñākūṭa āha | [SDhPS, 11 213.1]
idaṃ sūtraṃ gambhīraṃ sūkṣmaṃ durdṛśaṃ na cānena sūtreṇa kiṃcidanyat sūtraṃ samamasti | [SDhPS, 11 213.2]
asti kaścit sattvo ya idaṃ sūtraratnaṃ satkuryādavaboddhumanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃboddhum | [SDhPS, 11 214.1]
mañjuśrīrāha | [SDhPS, 11 214.2]
asti kulaputra sāgarasya nāgarājño duhitā aṣṭavarṣā jātyā mahāprajñā tīkṣṇendriyā jñānapūrvaṃgamena kāyavāṅmanaskarmaṇā samanvāgatā sarvatathāgatabhāṣitavyañjanārthodgrahaṇe dhāraṇīpratilabdhā sarvadharmasattvasamādhānasamādhisahasraikakṣaṇapratilābhinī | [SDhPS, 11 214.3]
bodhicittāvinivartinī vistīrṇapraṇidhānā sarvasattveṣvātmapremānugatā guṇotpādane ca samarthā | [SDhPS, 11 215.1]
na ca tebhyaḥ parihīyate | [SDhPS, 11 216.1]
smitamukhī paramayā śubhavarṇapuṣkalatayā samanvāgatā maitracittā karuṇāṃ ca vācaṃ bhāṣate | [SDhPS, 11 217.1]
sā samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃboddhuṃ samarthā | [SDhPS, 11 218.1]
prajñākūṭo bodhisattva āha | [SDhPS, 11 219.1]
dṛṣṭo mayā bhagavān śākyamunistathāgato bodhāya ghaṭamāno bodhisattvabhūto 'nekāni puṇyāni kṛtavān | [SDhPS, 11 219.2]
anekāni ca kalpasahasrāṇi na kadācid vīryaṃ sraṃsitavān | [SDhPS, 11 220.1]
trisāhasramahāsāhasrāyāṃ lokadhātau nāsti kaścidantaśaḥ sarṣapamātro 'pi pṛthivīpradeśaḥ yatrānena śarīraṃ na nikṣiptaṃ sattvahitahetoḥ | [SDhPS, 11 221.1]
paścād bodhimabhisaṃbuddhaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 222.1]
ka evaṃ śraddadhyād yadanayā śakyaṃ muhūrtena anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃboddhum | [SDhPS, 11 223.1]
atha khalu tasyāṃ velāyāṃ sāgaranāgarājaduhitā agrataḥ sthitā saṃdṛśyate sma | [SDhPS, 11 223.2]
sā bhagavataḥ pādau śirasābhivandya ekānte 'sthāt | [SDhPS, 11 224.1]
tasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 11 224.2]
puṇyaṃ puṇyaṃ gabhīraṃ ca diśaḥ sphurati sarvaśaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 225.1]
sūkṣmaṃ śarīraṃ dvātriṃśallakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam | [SDhPS, 11 225.2]
anuvyañjanayuktaṃ ca sarvasattvanamaskṛtam | [SDhPS, 11 226.1]
sarvasattvābhigamyaṃ ca antarāpaṇavadyathā | [SDhPS, 11 226.2]
yathecchayā me saṃbodhiḥ sākṣī me 'tra tathāgataḥ | [SDhPS, 11 227.1]
vistīrṇaṃ deśayiṣyāmi dharmaṃ duḥkhapramocanam | [SDhPS, 11 227.2]
atha khalu tasyāṃ velāyāmāyuṣmān śāriputrastāṃ sāgaranāgarājaduhitaram etadavocat | [SDhPS, 11 228.1]
kevalaṃ kulaputri bodhāya cittamutpannam | [SDhPS, 11 228.2]
avivartyāprameyaprajñā cāsi | [SDhPS, 11 229.1]
samyaksaṃbuddhatvaṃ tu durlabham | [SDhPS, 11 230.1]
asti kulaputri strī na ca vīryaṃ sraṃsayaty anekāni ca kalpaśatānyanekāni ca kalpasahasrāṇi puṇyāni karoti ṣaṭ pāramitāḥ paripūrayati na cādyāpi buddhatvaṃ prāpnoti | [SDhPS, 11 231.1]
kiṃ kāraṇam | [SDhPS, 11 232.1]
pañca sthānāni strī adyāpi na prāpnoti | [SDhPS, 11 232.2]
katamāni pañca | [SDhPS, 11 233.1]
prathamaṃ brahmasthānaṃ dvitīyaṃ śakrasthānaṃ tṛtīyaṃ mahārājasthānaṃ caturthaṃ cakravartisthānaṃ pañcamam avaivartikabodhisattvasthānam | [SDhPS, 11 233.2]
atha khalu tasyāṃ velāyāṃ sāgaranāgarājaduhitureko maṇirasti yaḥ kṛtsnāṃ mahāsāhasrāṃ lokadhātuṃ mūlyaṃ kṣamate | [SDhPS, 11 234.1]
sa ca maṇistayā sāgaranāgarājaduhitrā bhagavate dattaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 235.1]
sa bhagavatā ca anukampāmupādāya pratigṛhītaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 236.1]
atha sāgaranāgarājaduhitā prajñākūṭaṃ bodhisattvaṃ sthaviraṃ ca śāriputrametadavocat | [SDhPS, 11 237.1]
yo 'yaṃ maṇirmayā bhagavato dattaḥ sa ca bhagavatā śīghraṃ pratigṛhīto veti | [SDhPS, 11 237.2]
sthavira āha | [SDhPS, 11 237.3]
tvayā ca śīghraṃ datto bhagavatā ca śīghraṃ pratigṛhītaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 237.4]
sāgaranāgarājaduhitā āha | [SDhPS, 11 238.1]
yadyahaṃ bhadanta śāriputra maharddhikī syāṃ śīghrataraṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhyeyam | [SDhPS, 11 238.2]
na cāsya maṇeḥ pratigrāhakaḥ syāt | [SDhPS, 11 239.1]
atha tasyāṃ velāyāṃ sāgaranāgarājaduhitā sarvalokapratyakṣaṃ sthavirasya ca śāriputrasya pratyakṣaṃ tat strīndriyamantarhitaṃ puruṣendriyaṃ ca prādurbhūtaṃ bodhisattvabhūtaṃ cātmānaṃ saṃdarśayati | [SDhPS, 11 240.1]
tasyāṃ velāyāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ diśaṃ prakrāntaḥ | [SDhPS, 11 241.1]
atha dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi vimalā nāma lokadhātuḥ | [SDhPS, 11 242.1]
tatra saptaratnamaye bodhivṛkṣamūle niṣaṇṇamabhisaṃbuddhamātmānaṃ saṃdarśayati sma dvātriṃśallakṣaṇadharaṃ sarvānuvyañjanarūpaṃ prabhayā ca daśadiśaṃ sphuritvā dharmadeśanāṃ kurvāṇam | [SDhPS, 11 243.1]
ye ca sahāyāṃ lokadhātau sattvās te sarve taṃ tathāgataṃ paśyanti sma sarvaiśca devanāgayakṣagandharvāsuragaruḍakinnaramanuṣyāmanuṣyair namasyamānaṃ dharmadeśanāṃ ca kurvantam | [SDhPS, 11 244.1]
ye ca sattvāstasya tathāgatasya dharmadeśanāṃ śṛṇvanti sarve te 'vinivartanīyā bhavantyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 11 245.1]
sā ca vimalā lokadhātur iyaṃ ca sahā lokadhātuḥ ṣaḍvikāraṃ prākampat | [SDhPS, 11 246.1]
bhagavataśca śākyamuneḥ parṣanmaṇḍalānāṃ trayāṇāṃ prāṇisahasrāṇāmanutpattikadharmakṣāntipratilābho 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 11 247.1]
trayāṇāṃ ca prāṇiśatasahasrāṇāmanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau vyākaraṇapratilābho 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 11 248.1]
atha prajñākūṭo bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sthaviraśca śāriputrastūṣṇīmabhūtām | [SDhPS, 11 249.1]
{SDhPS, 12}
atha khalu bhaiṣajyarājo bodhisattvo mahāsattvo mahāpratibhānaśca bodhisattvo mahāsattvo viṃśatibodhisattvaśatasahasraparivāro bhagavataḥ saṃmukhamimāṃ vācamabhāṣetām | [SDhPS, 12 1.1]
alpotsuko bhagavān bhavatvasminnarthe | [SDhPS, 12 1.2]
vayamimaṃ bhagavan dharmaparyāyaṃ tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya sattvānāṃ deśayiṣyāmaḥ saṃprakāśayiṣyāmaḥ | [SDhPS, 12 2.1]
kiṃcāpi bhagavan śaṭhakāḥ sattvāstasmin kāle bhaviṣyanti parīttakuśalamūlā adhimānikā lābhasatkārasaṃniśritā akuśalamūlapratipannā durdamā adhimuktivirahitā anadhimuktibahulā api tu khalu punarvayaṃ bhagavan kṣāntibalamupadarśayitvā tasmin kāle idaṃ sūtramuddekṣyāmo dhārayiṣyāmo deśayiṣyāmo likhiṣyāmaḥ satkariṣyāmo gurukariṣyāmo mānayiṣyāmaḥ pūjayiṣyāmaḥ | [SDhPS, 12 3.1]
kāyajīvitaṃ ca vayaṃ bhagavan utsṛjya idaṃ sūtraṃ prakāśayiṣyāmaḥ | [SDhPS, 12 4.1]
alpotsuko bhagavān bhavatviti | [SDhPS, 12 5.1]
atha khalu tasyāṃ parṣadi śaikṣāśaikṣāṇāṃ bhikṣūṇāṃ pañcamātrāṇi bhikṣuśatāni bhagavantametadūcuḥ | [SDhPS, 12 6.1]
vayamapi bhagavan utsahāmahe imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ saṃprakāśayitum api tu khalu punarbhagavan anyāsu lokadhātuṣviti | [SDhPS, 12 6.2]
atha khalu yāvantaste bhagavataḥ śrāvakāḥ śaikṣāśaikṣā bhagavatā vyākṛtā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhāvaṣṭau bhikṣusahasrāṇi sarvāṇi tāni yena bhagavāṃstenāñjaliṃ praṇamayya bhagavantametadūcuḥ | [SDhPS, 12 7.1]
alpotsuko bhagavān bhavatu | [SDhPS, 12 7.2]
vayamapīmaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ saṃprakāśayiṣyāmastathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya paścime kāle paścime samaye api tvanyāsu lokadhātuṣu | [SDhPS, 12 8.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 12 9.1]
asyāṃ bhagavan sahāyāṃ lokadhātau adhimānikāḥ sattvā alpakuśalamūlā nityaṃ vyāpannacittāḥ śaṭhā vaṅkajātīyāḥ | [SDhPS, 12 9.2]
atha khalu mahāprajāpatī gautamī bhagavato mātṛbhaginī ṣaḍbhir bhikṣuṇīsahasraiḥ sārdhaṃ śaikṣāśaikṣābhir bhikṣuṇībhiḥ utthāyāsanād yena bhagavāṃs tenāñjaliṃ praṇamayya bhagavantamullokayantī sthitābhūt | [SDhPS, 12 10.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāṃ mahāprajāpatīṃ gautamīmāmantrayāmāsa | [SDhPS, 12 11.1]
kiṃ tvaṃ gautami durmanasvinī sthitā tathāgataṃ vyavalokayasi | [SDhPS, 12 11.2]
nāhaṃ parikīrtitā vyākṛtā ca anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 12 11.3]
api tu khalu punargautami sarvaparṣadvyākaraṇena vyākṛtāsi | [SDhPS, 12 12.1]
api tu khalu punastvaṃ gautami ita upādāya aṣṭātriṃśatāṃ buddhakoṭīniyutaśatasahasrāṇāmantike satkāraṃ gurukāraṃ mānanāṃ pūjanām arcanām apacāyanāṃ kṛtvā bodhisattvo mahāsattvo dharmabhāṇako bhaviṣyasi | [SDhPS, 12 13.1]
imānyapi ṣaḍ bhikṣuṇīsahasrāṇi śaikṣāśaikṣāṇāṃ bhikṣuṇīnāṃ tvayaiva sārdhaṃ teṣāṃ tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāmantike bodhisattvā dharmabhāṇakā bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 12 14.1]
tataḥ pareṇa paratareṇa bodhisattvacaryāṃ paripūrya sarvasattvapriyadarśano nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loke bhaviṣyasi vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān | [SDhPS, 12 15.1]
sa ca gautami sarvasattvapriyadarśanastathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhastāni ṣaḍ bodhisattvasahasrāṇi paraṃparāvyākaraṇena vyākariṣyatyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 12 16.1]
atha khalu rāhulamāturyaśodharāyā bhikṣuṇyā etadabhavat | [SDhPS, 12 17.1]
na me bhagavatā nāmadheyaṃ parikīrtitam | [SDhPS, 12 17.2]
atha khalu bhagavān yaśodharāyā bhikṣuṇyāścetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya yaśodharāṃ bhikṣuṇīmetadavocat | [SDhPS, 12 18.1]
ārocayāmi te yaśodhare prativedayāmi te | [SDhPS, 12 18.2]
tvamapi daśānāṃ buddhakoṭīsahasrāṇāmantike satkāraṃ gurukāraṃ mānanāṃ pūjanām arcanāmapacāyanāṃ kṛtvā bodhisattvo dharmabhāṇako bhaviṣyasi | [SDhPS, 12 19.1]
bodhisattvacaryāṃ ca anupūrveṇa paripūrya raśmiśatasahasraparipūrṇadhvajo nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho loke bhaviṣyasi vidhācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavid anuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān bhadrāyāṃ lokadhātau | [SDhPS, 12 20.1]
aparimitaṃ ca tasya bhagavato raśmiśatasahasraparipūrṇadhvajasya tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasyāyuṣpramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | [SDhPS, 12 21.1]
atha khalu mahāprajāpatī gautamī bhikṣuṇī ṣaḍbhikṣuṇīsahasraparivārā yaśodharā ca bhikṣuṇī caturbhikṣuṇīsahasraparivārā bhagavato 'ntikāt svakaṃ vyākaraṇaṃ śrutvā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau āścaryaprāptā adbhutaprāptāśca tasyāṃ velāyāmimāṃ gāthāmabhāṣanta | [SDhPS, 12 22.1]
bhagavan vinetāsi vināyako 'si śāstāsi lokasya sadevakasya | [SDhPS, 12 23.1]
āśvāsadātā naradevapūjito vayaṃ pi saṃtoṣita adya nātha | [SDhPS, 12 23.2]
atha khalu tā bhikṣuṇyaḥ imāṃ gāthāṃ bhāṣitvā bhagavantametadūcuḥ | [SDhPS, 12 24.1]
vayamapi bhagavan samutsahāmahe imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ saṃprakāśayituṃ paścime kāle paścime samaye 'pi tvanyāsu lokadhātuṣviti | [SDhPS, 12 24.2]
atha khalu bhagavān yena tāny aśītibodhisattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi dhāraṇīpratilabdhānāṃ bodhisattvānām avaivartikadharmacakrapravartakānāṃ tenāvalokayāmāsa | [SDhPS, 12 25.1]
atha khalu te bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ samanantarāvalokitā bhagavatā utthāyāsanebhyo yena bhagavāṃs tenāñjaliṃ praṇāmyaivaṃ cintayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 12 26.1]
asmākaṃ bhagavān adhyeṣati asya dharmaparyāyasya saṃprakāśanatāyai | [SDhPS, 12 26.2]
te khalvevam anuvicintya samprakampitāḥ parasparamūcuḥ | [SDhPS, 12 27.1]
kathaṃ vayaṃ kulaputrāḥ kariṣyāmo yad bhagavānadhyeṣati asya dharmaparyāyasyānāgate 'dhvani saṃprakāśanatāyai | [SDhPS, 12 27.2]
atha khalu te kulaputrā bhagavato gauraveṇa ātmanaśca pūrvacaryāpraṇidhānena bhagavato 'bhimukhaṃ siṃhanādaṃ nadante sma | [SDhPS, 12 27.3]
vayaṃ bhagavan anāgate 'dhvani imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ tathāgate parinirvṛte daśasu dikṣu gatvā sarvasattvāṃllekhayiṣyāmaḥ pāṭhayiṣyāmaś cintāpayiṣyāmaḥ prakāśayiṣyāmo bhagavata evānubhāvena | [SDhPS, 12 27.4]
bhagavāṃśca asmākamanyalokadhātusthito rakṣāvaraṇaguptiṃ kariṣyati | [SDhPS, 12 28.1]
atha khalu te bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ samasaṃgītyā bhagavantamābhirgāthābhiradhyabhāṣanta | [SDhPS, 12 29.1]
alpotsukastvaṃ bhagavan bhavasva vayaṃ tadā te parinirvṛtasya | [SDhPS, 12 30.1]
svaṃ paścime kāli subhairavasmin prakāśayiṣyāmida sūtramuttamam | [SDhPS, 12 30.2]
{SDhPS, 13}
atha khalu mañjuśrīḥ kumārabhūto bhagavantametadavocata | [SDhPS, 13 1.1]
duṣkaraṃ bhagavan paramaduṣkaram ebhir bodhisattvairmahāsattvair utsoḍhaṃ bhagavato gauraveṇa | [SDhPS, 13 1.2]
kathaṃ bhagavan ebhirbodhisattvairmahāsattvairayaṃ dharmaparyāyaḥ paścime kāle paścime samaye saṃprakāśayitavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 13 2.1]
evamukte bhagavān mañjuśriyaṃ kumārabhūtametadavocat | [SDhPS, 13 2.2]
caturṣu mañjuśrīrdharmeṣu pratiṣṭhitena bodhisattvena mahāsattvena ayaṃ dharmaparyāyaḥ paścime kāle paścime samaye saṃprakāśayitavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 13 2.3]
katameṣu caturṣu | [SDhPS, 13 3.1]
iha mañjuśrīrbodhisattvena mahāsattvena ācāragocarapratiṣṭhitena ayaṃ dharmaparyāyaḥ paścime kāle paścime samaye saṃprakāśayitavyaḥ | [SDhPS, 13 3.2]
kathaṃ ca mañjuśrīrbodhisattvo mahāsattva ācāragocarapratiṣṭhito bhavati | [SDhPS, 13 4.1]
yadā ca mañjuśrīrbodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ kṣānto bhavati dānto dāntabhūmimanuprāpto 'nutrastāsaṃtrastamanā anabhyasūyako yadā ca mañjuśrīrbodhisattvo mahāsattvo na kasmiṃściddharme carati yathābhūtaṃ ca dharmāṇāṃ svalakṣaṇaṃ vyavalokayati | [SDhPS, 13 4.2]
yā khalveṣu dharmeṣv avicāraṇā avikalpanāyam ucyate mañjuśrīrbodhisattvasya mahāsattvasyācāraḥ | [SDhPS, 13 5.1]
katamaśca mañjuśrīrbodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya gocaraḥ | [SDhPS, 13 6.1]
yadā ca mañjuśrīrbodhisattvo mahāsattvo na rājānaṃ saṃsevate na rājaputrān na rājamahāmātrān na rājapuruṣān saṃsevate na bhajate na paryupāste nopasaṃkrāmati nānyatīrthyāṃś carakaparivrājakājīvakanirgranthān na kāvyaśāstraprasṛtān sattvān saṃsevate na bhajate na paryupāste na ca lokāyatamantradhārakān na lokāyatikān sevate na bhajate na paryupāste na ca taiḥ sārdhaṃ saṃstavaṃ karoti | [SDhPS, 13 6.2]
na caṇḍālān na mauṣṭikān na saukarikān na kaukkuṭikān na mṛgalubdhakān na māṃsikān na naṭanṛttakān na jhallān na mallān | [SDhPS, 13 7.1]
anyāni pareṣāṃ ratikrīḍāsthānāni tāni nopasaṃkrāmati | [SDhPS, 13 8.1]
na ca taiḥ sārdhaṃ saṃstavaṃ karoti | [SDhPS, 13 9.1]
anyatropasaṃkrāntānāṃ kālena kālaṃ dharmaṃ bhāṣate taṃ cāniśrito bhāṣate | [SDhPS, 13 10.1]
śrāvakayānīyāṃśca bhikṣubhikṣuṇyupāsakopāsikā na sevate na bhajate na paryupāste na ca taiḥ sārdhaṃ saṃstavaṃ karoti | [SDhPS, 13 11.1]
na ca taiḥ saha samavadhānagocaro bhavati caṃkrame vā vihāre vā | [SDhPS, 13 12.1]
anyatropasaṃkrāntānāṃ caiṣāṃ kālena kālaṃ dharmaṃ bhāṣate taṃ cāniśrito bhāṣate | [SDhPS, 13 13.1]
ayaṃ mañjuśrīrbodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya gocaraḥ | [SDhPS, 13 14.1]
punaraparaṃ mañjuśrīrbodhisattvo mahāsattvo na mātṛgrāmasya anyatarānyataramanunayanimittamudgṛhya abhīkṣṇaṃ dharmaṃ deśayati na ca mātṛgrāmasya abhīkṣṇaṃ darśanakāmo bhavati | [SDhPS, 13 15.1]
na ca kulānyupasaṃkramati na ca dārikāṃ vā kanyāṃ vā vadhukāṃ vā abhīkṣṇamābhāṣitavyāṃ manyate na pratisaṃmodayati | [SDhPS, 13 16.1]
na ca paṇḍakasya dharmaṃ deśayati na ca tena sārdhaṃ saṃstavaṃ karoti na ca pratisaṃmodayati | [SDhPS, 13 17.1]
na caikākī bhikṣārthamantargṛhaṃ praviśaty anyatra tathāgatānusmṛtiṃ bhāvayamānaḥ | [SDhPS, 13 18.1]
sacetpunarmātṛgrāmasya dharmaṃ deśayati sa nāntaśo dharmasaṃrāgeṇāpi dharmaṃ deśayati kaḥ punar vādaḥ strīsaṃrāgeṇa | [SDhPS, 13 19.1]
nāntaśo dantāvalīmapyupadarśayati kaḥ punar vāda audārikamukhavikāram | [SDhPS, 13 20.1]
na ca śrāmaṇeraṃ na ca śrāmaṇerīṃ na bhikṣuṃ na bhikṣuṇīṃ na kumārakaṃ na kumārikāṃ sātīyati na ca taiḥ sārdhaṃ saṃstavaṃ karoti na ca saṃlāpaṃ karoti | [SDhPS, 13 21.1]
sa ca pratisaṃlayanaguruko bhavaty abhīkṣṇaṃ ca pratisaṃlayanaṃ sevate | [SDhPS, 13 22.1]
ayamucyate mañjuśrīr bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya prathamo gocaraḥ | [SDhPS, 13 23.1]
punaraparaṃ mañjuśrīr bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sarvadharmān śūnyān vyavalokayati yathāvat pratiṣṭhitān dharmān aviparītasthāyino yathābhūtasthitān acalān akampyān avivartyān aparivartān sadā yathābhūtasthitān ākāśasvabhāvān niruktivyavahāravivarjitān ajātān abhūtān anasambhūtān asaṃskṛtān asaṃtānān asattābhilāpapravyāhṛtān asaṅgasthānasthitān saṃjñāviparyāsaprādurbhūtān | [SDhPS, 13 24.1]
evaṃ hi mañjuśrīrbodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'bhīkṣṇaṃ sarvadharmān vyavalokayan viharaty anena vihāreṇa viharan bodhisattvo mahāsattvo gocare sthito bhavati | [SDhPS, 13 25.1]
ayaṃ mañjuśrīrbodhisattvasya dvitīyo gocaraḥ | [SDhPS, 13 26.1]
atha khalu bhagavānetamevārthaṃ bhūyasyā mātrayā saṃdarśayamānastasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 13 27.1]
punaraparaṃ mañjuśrīr bodhisattvo mahāsattvastathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya paścime kāle paścime samaye saddharmavipralope vartamāne imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ saṃprakāśayitukāmaḥ sukhasthito bhavati | [SDhPS, 13 53.1]
sa sukhasthitaśca dharmaṃ bhāṣate kāyagataṃ vā pustakagataṃ vā | [SDhPS, 13 54.1]
pareṣāṃ ca deśayamāno nādhimātramupālambhajātīyo bhavati na cānyān dharmabhāṇakān bhikṣūn parivadati na cāvarṇaṃ bhāṣate na cāvarṇaṃ niścārayati na cānyeṣāṃ śrāvakayānīyānāṃ bhikṣūṇāṃ nāma gṛhītvāvarṇaṃ bhāṣate na cāvarṇaṃ cārayati na ca teṣāmantike pratyarthikasaṃjñī bhavati | [SDhPS, 13 55.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 13 56.1]
yathāpīdaṃ sukhasthānasthitatvāt | [SDhPS, 13 56.2]
sa āgatāgatānāṃ dhārmaśrāvaṇikānām anuparigrāhikayā anabhyasūyayā dharmaṃ deśayati | [SDhPS, 13 57.1]
avivadamāno na ca praśnaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ śrāvakayānena visarjayati | [SDhPS, 13 58.1]
api tu khalu punastathā visarjayati yathā buddhajñānam abhisaṃbudhyate | [SDhPS, 13 59.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 13 60.1]
punaraparaṃ mañjuśrīrbodhisattvo mahāsattvastathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya saddharmakṣayāntakāle vartamāne idaṃ sūtraṃ dhārayamāṇo bodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'nīrṣuko bhavatyaśaṭho 'māyāvī na cānyeṣāṃ bodhisattvayānīyānāṃ pudgalānāmavarṇaṃ bhāṣate nāpavadati nāvasādayati | [SDhPS, 13 74.1]
na cānyeṣāṃ bhikṣubhikṣuṇyupāsakopāsikānāṃ śrāvakayānīyānāṃ vā pratyekabuddhayānīyānāṃ vā bodhisattvayānīyānāṃ vā kaukṛtyamupasaṃharati | [SDhPS, 13 75.1]
dūre yūyaṃ kulaputrā anuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodher na tasyāṃ yūyaṃ saṃdṛśyadhve | [SDhPS, 13 75.2]
atyantapramādavihāriṇo yūyam | [SDhPS, 13 76.1]
na yūyaṃ pratibalāstaṃ jñānamabhisaṃboddhum | [SDhPS, 13 77.1]
ityevaṃ na kasyacid bodhisattvayānīyasya kaukṛtyamupasaṃharati | [SDhPS, 13 78.1]
na ca dharmavivādābhirato bhavati na ca dharmavivādaṃ karoti sarvasattvānāṃ cāntike maitrībalaṃ na vijahāti | [SDhPS, 13 79.1]
sarvatathāgatānāṃ cāntike pitṛsaṃjñāmutpādayati sarvabodhisattvānāṃ cāntike śāstṛsaṃjñāmutpādayati | [SDhPS, 13 80.1]
ye ca daśasu dikṣu loke bodhisattvā mahāsattvās tān abhīkṣṇamadhyāśayena gauraveṇa ca namaskurute | [SDhPS, 13 81.1]
dharmaṃ ca deśayamāno 'nūnamanadhikaṃ dharmaṃ deśayati samena dharmapremṇā na ca kasyacidantaśo dharmapremṇāpyadhikataramanugrahaṃ karotīmaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ saṃprakāśayamānaḥ | [SDhPS, 13 82.1]
anena mañjuśrīstṛtīyena dharmeṇa samanvāgato bodhisattvo mahāsattvastathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya saddharmaparikṣayāntakāle vartamāne imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ saṃprakāśayamānaḥ sukhasparśaṃ viharaty aviheṭhitaś cemaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ saṃprakāśayati | [SDhPS, 13 83.1]
bhavanti cāsya dharmasaṃgītyāṃ sahāyakāḥ | [SDhPS, 13 84.1]
utpatsyante cāsya dhārmaśrāvaṇikā ye 'syemaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śroṣyanti śraddhāsyanti pattīyiṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti likhiṣyanti likhāpayiṣyanti pustakagataṃ ca kṛtvā satkariṣyanti gurukariṣyanti mānayiṣyanti pūjayiṣyanti | [SDhPS, 13 85.1]
idamavocad bhagavān | [SDhPS, 13 86.1]
punaraparaṃ mañjuśrīrbodhisattvo mahāsattvastathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya saddharmapratikṣayāntakāle vartamāne imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ dhārayitukāmastena bhikṣuṇā gṛhasthapravrajitānāmantikād dūreṇa dūraṃ vihartavyaṃ maitrīvihāreṇa ca vihartavyam | [SDhPS, 13 94.1]
ye ca sattvā bodhāya samprasthitā bhavanti teṣāṃ sarveṣāmantike spṛhotpādayitavyā | [SDhPS, 13 95.1]
evaṃ cānena cittamutpādayitavyam | [SDhPS, 13 96.1]
mahāduṣprajñajātīyā bateme sattvā ye tathāgatasyopāyakauśalyaṃ saṃdhābhāṣitaṃ na śṛṇvanti na jānanti na budhyante na pṛcchanti na śraddadhanti nādhimucyante | [SDhPS, 13 97.1]
kiṃcāpyete sattvā imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ nāvataranti na budhyante api tu khalu punarahametāmanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhya yo yasmin sthito bhaviṣyati taṃ tasminneva ṛddhibalenāvarjayiṣyāmi pattīyāpayiṣyāmi avatārayiṣyāmi paripācayiṣyāmi | [SDhPS, 13 98.1]
anenāpi mañjuśrīścaturthena dharmeṇa samanvāgato bodhisattvo mahāsattvastathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ saṃprakāśayamāno 'vyābādho bhavati satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito bhikṣubhikṣuṇyupāsakopāsikānāṃ rājñā rājaputrāṇāṃ rājāmātyānāṃ rājamahāmātrāṇāṃ naigamajānapadānāṃ brāhmaṇagṛhapatīnām | [SDhPS, 13 99.1]
antarīkṣāvacarāścāsya devatāḥ śrāddhāḥ pṛṣṭhato 'nubaddhā bhaviṣyanti dharmaśravaṇāya | [SDhPS, 13 100.1]
devaputrāścāsya sadānubaddhā bhaviṣyantyārakṣāyai grāmagatasya vā vihāragatasya vā | [SDhPS, 13 101.1]
upasaṃkramiṣyanti rātriṃdivaṃ dharmaṃ paripṛcchakāḥ | [SDhPS, 13 102.1]
tasya ca vyākaraṇena tuṣṭā udagrā āttamanaskā bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 13 103.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 13 104.1]
sarvabuddhādhiṣṭhito 'yaṃ mañjuśrīrdharmaparyāyaḥ | [SDhPS, 13 104.2]
atītānāgatapratyutpannair mañjuśrīs tathāgatair arhadbhiḥ samyaksaṃbuddhairayaṃ dharmaparyāyo nityādhiṣṭhitaḥ | [SDhPS, 13 105.1]
durlabho 'sya mañjuśrīrdharmaparyāyasya bahuṣu lokadhātuṣu śabdo vā ghoṣo vā nāmaśravo vā | [SDhPS, 13 106.1]
tadyathāpi nāma mañjuśrī rājā bhavati balacakravartī balena taṃ svakaṃ rājyaṃ nirjināti | [SDhPS, 13 107.1]
tato 'sya pratyarthikāḥ pratyamitrāḥ pratirājānastena sārdhaṃ vigrahamāpannā bhavanti | [SDhPS, 13 108.1]
atha tasya rājño balacakravartino vividhā yodhā bhavanti | [SDhPS, 13 109.1]
te taiḥ śatrubhiḥ sārdhaṃ yudhyante | [SDhPS, 13 110.1]
atha sa rājā tān yodhān yudhyamānān dṛṣṭvā teṣāṃ yodhānāṃ prīto bhavatyāttamanaskaḥ | [SDhPS, 13 111.1]
sa prīta āttamanāḥ samānasteṣāṃ yodhānāṃ vividhāni dānāni dadāti | [SDhPS, 13 112.1]
tadyathā grāmaṃ vā grāmakṣetrāṇi vā dadāti nagaraṃ nagarakṣetrāṇi vā dadāti vastrāṇi dadāti veṣṭanāni hastābharaṇāni pādābharaṇāni kaṇṭhābharaṇāni karṇābharaṇāni sauvarṇasūtrāṇi hārārdhahārāṇi hiraṇyasuvarṇamaṇimuktāvaiḍūryaśaṅkhaśilāpravālānyapi dadāti hastyaśvarathapattidāsīdāsānapi dadāti yānāni śibikāśca dadāti | [SDhPS, 13 113.1]
na punaḥ kasyaciccūḍāmaṇiṃ dadāti | [SDhPS, 13 114.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 13 115.1]
eka eva hi sa cūḍāmaṇī rājño mūrdhasthāyī | [SDhPS, 13 115.2]
yadā punar mañjuśrī rājā tamapi cūḍāmaṇiṃ dadāt tadā sa sarvo rājñaś caturaṅgabalakāya āścaryaprāpto bhavatyadbhutaprāptaḥ | [SDhPS, 13 116.1]
evameva mañjuśrīstathāgato 'pyarhan samyaksaṃbuddho dharmasvāmī dharmarājā svena bāhubalanirjitena puṇyabalanirjitena traidhātuke dharmeṇa dharmarājyaṃ kārayati | [SDhPS, 13 117.1]
tasya māraḥ pāpīyāṃstraidhātukamākrāmati | [SDhPS, 13 118.1]
atha khalu tathāgatasyāpi āryā yodhā māreṇa sārdhaṃ yudhyante | [SDhPS, 13 119.1]
atha khalu mañjuśrīstathāgato 'pyarhan samyaksaṃbuddho dharmasvāmī dharmarājā teṣāmāryāṇāṃ yodhānāṃ yudhyatāṃ dṛṣṭvā vividhāni sūtraśatasahasrāṇi bhāṣate sma catasṛṇāṃ parṣadāṃ saṃharṣaṇārtham | [SDhPS, 13 120.1]
nirvāṇanagaraṃ caiṣāṃ mahādharmanagaraṃ dadāti | [SDhPS, 13 121.1]
nirvṛtyā cainān pralobhayati sma | [SDhPS, 13 122.1]
na punarimamevaṃrūpaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ bhāṣate sma | [SDhPS, 13 123.1]
tatra mañjuśrīryathā sa rājā balacakravartī teṣāṃ yodhānāṃ yudhyatāṃ mahatā puruṣakāreṇa vismāpitaḥ samānaḥ paścāttaṃ sarvasvabhūtaṃ paścimaṃ cūḍāmaṇiṃ dadāti sarvalokāśraddheyaṃ vismayabhūtam | [SDhPS, 13 124.1]
yathā mañjuśrīstasya rājñaḥ sa cūḍāmaṇiścirarakṣito mūrdhasthāyy evameva mañjuśrīstathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhastraidhātuke dharmarājo dharmeṇa rājyaṃ kārayamāṇo yasmin samaye paśyati śrāvakāṃśca bodhisattvāṃśca skandhamāreṇa vā kleśamāreṇa vā sārdhaṃ yudhyamānāṃs taiśca sārdhaṃ yudhyamānairyadā rāgadveṣamohakṣayaḥ sarvatraidhātukān niḥsaraṇaṃ sarvamāranirghātanaṃ mahāpuruṣakāraḥ kṛto bhavati tadā tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho 'pyārāgitaḥ samānas teṣām āryāṇāṃ yodhānām imam evaṃrūpaṃ sarvalokavipratyanīkaṃ sarvalokāśraddheyam abhāṣitapūrvam anirdiṣṭapūrvaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ bhāṣate sma | [SDhPS, 13 125.1]
sarveṣāṃ sarvajñatāhārakaṃ mahācūḍāmaṇiprakhyaṃ tathāgataḥ śrāvakebhyo 'nuprayacchati sma | [SDhPS, 13 126.1]
eṣā hi mañjuśrīstathāgatānāṃ paramā dharmadeśanāyaṃ paścimas tathāgatānāṃ dharmaparyāyaḥ | [SDhPS, 13 127.1]
sarveṣāṃ dharmaparyāyāṇām ayaṃ dharmaparyāyaḥ sarvagambhīraḥ sarvalokavipratyanīko yo 'yaṃ mañjuśrīs tathāgatenādya tenaiva rājñā balacakravartinā ciraparirakṣitaścūḍāmaṇir avamucya yodhebhyo dattaḥ | [SDhPS, 13 128.1]
evameva mañjuśrīs tathāgato 'pīmaṃ dharmaguhyaṃ cirānurakṣitaṃ sarvadharmaparyāyāṇāṃ mūrdhasthāyi tathāgatavijñeyam | [SDhPS, 13 129.1]
tadidaṃ tathāgatenādya saṃprakāśitamiti | [SDhPS, 13 130.1]
atha khalu bhagavānetam evārthaṃ bhūyasyā mātrayā saṃdarśayamānastasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 13 131.1]
{SDhPS, 14}
atha khalu anyalokadhātvāgatānāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāmaṣṭau gaṅgānadīvālukāsamā bodhisattvā mahāsattvāstasmin samaye tataḥ parṣanmaṇḍalādabhyutthitā abhūvan | [SDhPS, 14 1.1]
te 'ñjaliṃ pragṛhya bhagavato 'bhimukhā bhagavantaṃ namasyamānā bhagavantametadūcuḥ | [SDhPS, 14 2.1]
saced bhagavānasmākamanujānīyād vayamapi bhagavan imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya tasyāṃ sahāyāṃ lokadhātau saṃprakāśayema vācayema lekhayema pūjayemāsmiṃśca dharmaparyāye yogam āpadyemahi | [SDhPS, 14 2.2]
tatsādhu bhagavānasmākamapīmaṃ dharmaparyāyamanujānātu | [SDhPS, 14 3.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstān bodhisattvānetadavocat | [SDhPS, 14 4.1]
alaṃ kulaputrāḥ | [SDhPS, 14 4.2]
kiṃ yuṣmākamanena kṛtyena | [SDhPS, 14 5.1]
santi kulaputrā iha mamaivāsyāṃ sahāyāṃ lokadhātau ṣaṣṭigaṅgānadīvālukāsamāni bodhisattvasahasrāṇi ekasya bodhisattvasya parivāraḥ | [SDhPS, 14 5.2]
evaṃrūpāṇāṃ ca bodhisattvānāṃ ṣaṣṭyeva gaṅgānadīvālukāsamāni bodhisattvasahasrāṇi yeṣāmekaikasya bodhisattvasya iyāneva parivāraḥ ye mama parinirvṛtasya paścime kāle paścime samaye imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti saṃprakāśayiṣyanti | [SDhPS, 14 6.1]
samanantarabhāṣitā ceyaṃ bhagavatā vāg atheyaṃ sahā lokadhātuḥ samantāt sphuṭitā visphuṭitā abhūt | [SDhPS, 14 7.1]
tebhyaśca sphoṭāntarebhyo bahūni bodhisattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇyuttiṣṭhante sma suvarṇavarṇaiḥ kāyair dvātriṃśadbhirmahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samanvāgatā ye 'syāṃ mahāpṛthivyāmadha ākāśadhātau viharanti sma | [SDhPS, 14 8.1]
imāmeva sahāṃ lokadhātuṃ niśritya te khalvimam evaṃrūpaṃ bhagavataḥ śabdaṃ śrutvā pṛthivyā adhaḥ samutthitā yeṣāmekaiko bodhisattvaḥ ṣaṣṭigaṅgānadīvālukopamabodhisattvaparivāro gaṇī mahāgaṇī gaṇācāryaḥ | [SDhPS, 14 9.1]
tādṛśānāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāṃ gaṇīnāṃ mahāgaṇīnāṃ gaṇācāryāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭigaṅgānadīvālukopamāni bodhisattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi ye itaḥ sahāyā lokadhātor dharaṇīvivarebhyaḥ samunmajjante sma | [SDhPS, 14 10.1]
kaḥ punar vādaḥ pañcāśadgaṅgānadīvālukopamabodhisattvaparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.1]
kaḥ punar vādaś catvāriṃśadgaṅgānadīvālukopamabodhisattvaparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.2]
kaḥ punar vādas triṃśadgaṅgānadīvālukopamabodhisattvaparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.3]
kaḥ punar vādo viṃśatibodhisattvaparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.4]
kaḥ punar vādo daśagaṅgānadīvālukopamabodhisattvaparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.5]
kaḥ punar vādaḥ pañcacatustridvigaṅgānadīvālukopamabodhisattvaparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.6]
kaḥ punar vāda ekagaṅgānadīvālukopamabodhisattvaparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.7]
kaḥ punar vādo 'rdhagaṅgānadīvālukopamabodhisattvaparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.8]
kaḥ punar vādaś caturbhāgaṣaḍbhāgāṣṭabhāgadaśabhāgaviṃśatibhāgatriṃśadbhāgacatvāriṃśadbhāgapañcāśadbhāgaśatabhāgasahasrabhāgaśatasahasrabhāgakoṭībhāgakoṭīśatabhāgakoṭīsahasrabhāgakoṭīśatasahasrabhāgakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrabhāgagaṅgānadīvālukopamabodhisattvaparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.9]
kaḥ punar vādo bahubodhisattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasraparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.10]
kaḥ punar vādaḥ koṭīparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.11]
kaḥ punar vādaḥ śatasahasraparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.12]
kaḥ punar vādaḥ sahasraparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.13]
kaḥ punar vādaḥ pañcaśataparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.14]
kaḥ punar vādaś catuḥśatatriśatadviśataparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.15]
kaḥ punar vādaḥ ekaśataparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.16]
kaḥ punar vādaḥ pañcāśadbodhisattvaparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 11.17]
peyālam | [SDhPS, 14 11.18]
kaḥ punar vādaś catvāriṃśatriṃśadviṃśatidaśapañcacatustridvibodhisattvaparivārāṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 12.1]
kaḥ punar vāda ātmadvitīyānāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 12.2]
kaḥ punar vādo 'parivārāṇām ekavihāriṇāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [SDhPS, 14 12.3]
na teṣāṃ saṃkhyā vā gaṇanā vā upamā vā upaniṣadvā upalabhyate ya iha sahāyāṃ lokadhātau dharaṇīvivarebhyo bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ samunmajjante sma | [SDhPS, 14 12.4]
te ca unmajjyonmajjya yena sa mahāratnastūpo vaihāyasamantarīkṣe sthito yasmin sa bhagavān prabhūtaratnastathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ parinirvṛto bhagavatā śākyamuninā tathāgatenārhatā samyaksaṃbuddhena sārdhaṃ siṃhāsane niṣaṇṇas tenopasaṃkrāmanti sma | [SDhPS, 14 13.1]
upasaṃkramya ca ubhayayos tathāgatayorarhatoḥ samyaksaṃbuddhayoḥ pādau śirobhirvanditvā sarvāṃśca tān bhagavataḥ śākyamunestathāgatasyātmīyān nirmitāṃstathāgatavigrahān ye te samantato daśasu dikṣvanyonyāsu lokadhātuṣu saṃnipatitā nānāratnavṛkṣamūleṣu siṃhāsanopaviṣṭās tān sarvān abhivandya namaskṛtya ca anekaśatasahasrakṛtvastāṃstathāgatānarhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhān pradakṣiṇīkṛtya nānāprakārair bodhisattvastavair abhiṣṭutya ekānte tasthuḥ | [SDhPS, 14 14.1]
añjaliṃ pragṛhya bhagavantaṃ śākyamuniṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ ca prabhūtaratnaṃ tathāgatam arhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddham abhisaṃmukhaṃ namaskurvanti sma | [SDhPS, 14 15.1]
tena khalu punaḥ samayena teṣāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāṃ pṛthivīvivarebhya unmajjatāṃ tathāgatāṃśca vandamānānāṃ nānāprakārair bodhisattvastavair abhiṣṭuvatāṃ paripūrṇāḥ pañcāśadantarakalpā gacchanti sma | [SDhPS, 14 16.1]
tāṃśca pañcāśadantarakalpān sa bhagavān śākyamunistathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhas tūṣṇīmabhūt | [SDhPS, 14 17.1]
tāścatasraḥ parṣadastāneva pañcāśadantarakalpāṃs tūṣṇīṃbhāvenāvasthitā abhūvan | [SDhPS, 14 18.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstathārūpam ṛddhyabhisaṃskāramakarod yathārūpeṇarddhyabhisaṃskāreṇābhisaṃskṛtena tāś catasraḥ parṣadastamevaikaṃ paścādbhaktaṃ saṃjānante sma | [SDhPS, 14 19.1]
imāṃ ca sahāṃ lokadhātuṃ śatasahasrākāśaparigṛhītāṃ bodhisattvaparipūrṇāmadrākṣuḥ | [SDhPS, 14 20.1]
tasya khalu punarmahato bodhisattvagaṇasya mahato bodhisattvarāśeścatvāro bodhisattvā mahāsattvā ye pramukhā abhūvaṃs tadyathā viśiṣṭacāritraśca nāma bodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'nantacāritraśca nāma bodhisattvo mahāsattvo viśuddhacāritraśca nāma bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ supratiṣṭhitacāritraśca nāma bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ | [SDhPS, 14 21.1]
ime catvāro bodhisattvā mahāsattvāstasya mahato bodhisattvagaṇasya mahato bodhisattvarāśeḥ pramukhā abhūvan | [SDhPS, 14 22.1]
atha khalu catvāro bodhisattvā mahāsattvāstasya mahato bodhisattvagaṇasya mahato bodhisattvarāśeragrataḥ sthitvā bhagavato 'bhimukhamañjaliṃ pragṛhya bhagavantametadūcuḥ | [SDhPS, 14 22.2]
kaccid bhagavato 'lpābādhatā mandaglānatā sukhasaṃsparśavihāratā ca | [SDhPS, 14 22.3]
kaccid bhagavan sattvāḥ svākārāḥ suvijñāpakāḥ suvineyāḥ suviśodhakāḥ | [SDhPS, 14 22.4]
mā haiva bhagavataḥ khedamutpādayanti | [SDhPS, 14 22.5]
atha khalu te catvāro bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhagavantam ābhyāṃ gāthābhyāmadhyabhāṣanta | [SDhPS, 14 23.1]
kaccit sukhaṃ viharasi lokanātha prabhaṃkara | [SDhPS, 14 24.1]
ābādhavipramukto 'si sparśaḥ kāye tavānagha | [SDhPS, 14 24.2]
svākārāścaiva te sattvāḥ suvineyāḥ suśodhakāḥ | [SDhPS, 14 25.1]
mā haiva khedaṃ janayanti lokanāthasya bhāṣataḥ | [SDhPS, 14 25.2]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasya mahato bodhisattvagaṇasya mahato bodhisattvarāśeḥ pramukhāṃścaturo bodhisattvān mahāsattvānetadavocat | [SDhPS, 14 26.1]
evametat kulaputrā evametat | [SDhPS, 14 26.2]
sukhasaṃsparśavihāro 'smi alpābādho mandaglānaḥ | [SDhPS, 14 27.1]
svākārāśca mamaiva te sattvāḥ suvijñāpakāḥ suvineyāḥ suviśodhakāḥ | [SDhPS, 14 28.1]
na ca me khedaṃ janayanti viśodhyamānāḥ | [SDhPS, 14 29.1]
tat kasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 14 30.1]
mamaiva hyete kulaputrāḥ sattvāḥ paurvakeṣu samyaksaṃbuddheṣu kṛtaparikarmāṇaḥ | [SDhPS, 14 30.2]
darśanādeva hi kulaputrāḥ śravaṇācca mamādhimucyante buddhajñānam avataranti avagāhante | [SDhPS, 14 31.1]
yatra ye 'pi śrāvakabhūmau vā pratyekabuddhabhūmau vā kṛtaparicaryā abhuvaṃs te 'pi mayaiva etarhi buddhadharmajñānamavatāritāḥ saṃśrāvitāśca paramārtham | [SDhPS, 14 32.1]
atha khalu te bodhisattvā mahāsattvāstasyāṃ velāyāmime gāthe abhāṣanta | [SDhPS, 14 33.1]
sādhu sādhu mahāvīra anumodāmahe vayam | [SDhPS, 14 34.1]
svākārā yena te sattvāḥ suvineyāḥ suśodhakāḥ | [SDhPS, 14 34.2]
ye cedaṃ jñānagambhīraṃ śṛṇvanti tava nāyaka | [SDhPS, 14 35.1]
śrutvā ca adhimucyante uttaranti ca nāyaka | [SDhPS, 14 35.2]
evamukte bhagavāṃstasya mahato bodhisattvagaṇasya mahato bodhisattvarāśeḥ pramukhebhyaścaturbhyo bodhisattvebhyo mahāsattvebhyaḥ sādhukāramadāt | [SDhPS, 14 36.1]
sādhu sādhu kulaputrā ye yūyaṃ tathāgatamabhinandatha iti | [SDhPS, 14 36.2]
tena khalu punaḥ samayena maitreyasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya anyeṣāṃ cāṣṭānāṃ gaṅgānadīvālukopamānāṃ bodhisattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇām etadabhavat | [SDhPS, 14 37.1]
adṛṣṭapūrvo 'yamasmābhirmahābodhisattvagaṇo mahābodhisattvarāśiḥ | [SDhPS, 14 37.2]
aśrutapūrvaśca yo 'yaṃ pṛthivīvivarebhyaḥ samunmajjya bhagavataḥ purataḥ sthitvā bhagavantaṃ satkurvanti gurukurvanti mānayanti pūjayanti bhagavantaṃ ca pratisaṃmodante | [SDhPS, 14 38.1]
kutaḥ khalvime bodhisattvā mahāsattvā āgatā iti | [SDhPS, 14 39.1]
atha khalu maitreyo bodhisattvo mahāsattva ātmanā vicikitsāṃ kathaṃkathāṃ viditvā teṣāṃ gaṅgānadīvālukopamānāṃ bodhisattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇāṃ cetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkam ājñāya tasyāṃ velāyāmañjaliṃ pragṛhya bhagavantaṃ gāthābhigītenaitamevārthaṃ paripṛcchanti sma | [SDhPS, 14 40.1]
tena khalu punaḥ samayena ye te tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhā anyebhyo lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasrebhyo 'bhyāgatā bhagavataḥ śākyamunestathāgatasya nirmitā ye 'nyeṣu lokadhātuṣu sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśayanti sma ye bhagavataḥ śākyamunestathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasya samantādaṣṭabhyo digbhyo ratnavṛkṣamūleṣu mahāratnasiṃhāsaneṣūpaviṣṭāḥ paryaṅkabaddhās teṣāṃ tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāṃ ye svakasvakā upasthāyakās te 'pi taṃ mahāntaṃ bodhisattvagaṇaṃ bodhisattvarāśiṃ dṛṣṭvā samantāt pṛthivīvivarebhya unmajjantamākāśadhātupratiṣṭhitaṃ te 'pyāścaryaprāptāstān svān svāṃstathāgatānetadūcuḥ | [SDhPS, 14 69.1]
kuto bhagavan iyanto bodhisattvā mahāsattvā āgacchantyaprameyā asaṃkhyeyāḥ | [SDhPS, 14 69.2]
evamuktāste tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāstān svān svānupasthāyakānetadūcuḥ | [SDhPS, 14 69.3]
āgamayadhvaṃ yūyaṃ kulaputrā muhūrtam | [SDhPS, 14 69.4]
eṣa maitreyo nāma bodhisattvo mahāsattvo bhagavataḥ śākyamuneranantaraṃ vyākṛto 'nuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau sa etaṃ bhagavantaṃ śākyamuniṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddham etam arthaṃ paripṛcchati | [SDhPS, 14 70.1]
eṣa ca bhagavān śākyamunistathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho vyākariṣyati | [SDhPS, 14 71.1]
tato yūyaṃ śroṣyatheti | [SDhPS, 14 72.1]
atha khalu bhagavān maitreyaṃ bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 14 73.1]
sādhu sādhu ajita | [SDhPS, 14 73.2]
udārametadajita sthānaṃ yattvaṃ māṃ paripṛcchasi | [SDhPS, 14 74.1]
atha khalu bhagavān sarvāvantaṃ bodhisattvagaṇamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 14 75.1]
tena hi kulaputrāḥ sarva eva prayatā bhavadhvam | [SDhPS, 14 75.2]
susaṃnaddhā dṛḍhasthāmāśca bhavadhvaṃ sarvaścāyaṃ bodhisattvagaṇaḥ | [SDhPS, 14 76.1]
tathāgatajñānadarśanaṃ kulaputrāstathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ sāṃprataṃ saṃprakāśayati tathāgatavṛṣabhitaṃ tathāgatakarma tathāgatavikrīḍitaṃ tathāgatavijṛmbhitaṃ tathāgataparākramamiti | [SDhPS, 14 77.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 14 78.1]
atha khalu bhagavānimā gāthā bhāṣitvā tasyāṃ velāyāṃ maitreyaṃ bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 14 83.1]
ārocayāmi te ajita prativedayāmi | [SDhPS, 14 83.2]
ya ime ajita bodhisattvā aprameyā asaṃkhyeyā acintyā atulyā agaṇanīyā ye yuṣmābhir adṛṣṭapūrvā ya etarhi pṛthivīvivarebhyo niṣkrāntā mayaite ajita sarve bodhisattvā mahāsattvā asyāṃ sahāyāṃ lokadhātāvanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhya samādāpitāḥ samuttejitāḥ saṃpraharṣitā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau pariṇāmitāḥ | [SDhPS, 14 84.1]
mayā caite kulaputrā asmin bodhisattvadharme paripācitāḥ pratiṣṭhāpitā niveśitāḥ parisaṃsthāpitā avatāritāḥ paribodhitāḥ pariśodhitāḥ | [SDhPS, 14 85.1]
ete ca ajita bodhisattvā mahāsattvā asyāṃ sahāyāṃ lokadhātau adhastādākāśadhātuparigrahe prativasanti | [SDhPS, 14 86.1]
svādhyāyoddeśacintāyoniśomanasikārapravṛttā ete kulaputrā asaṃgaṇikārāmā asaṃsargābhiratā anikṣiptadhurā ārabdhavīryāḥ | [SDhPS, 14 87.1]
ete ajita kulaputrā vivekārāmā vivekābhiratāḥ | [SDhPS, 14 88.1]
naite kulaputrā devamanuṣyānupaniśrāya viharanty asaṃsargacaryābhiratāḥ | [SDhPS, 14 89.1]
ete kulaputrā dharmārāmābhiratā buddhajñāne 'bhiyuktāḥ | [SDhPS, 14 90.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 14 91.1]
atha khalu maitreyo bodhisattvo mahāsattvastāni ca saṃbahulāni bodhisattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇy āścaryaprāptānyabhūvan adbhutaprāptāni vismayaprāptāni | [SDhPS, 14 99.1]
kathaṃ nāma bhagavatā anena kṣaṇavihāreṇa alpena kālāntareṇa amī etāvanto bodhisattvā mahāsattvā asaṃkhyeyāḥ samādāpitāḥ paripācitāśca anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 14 99.2]
atha khalu maitreyo bodhisattvo mahāsattvo bhagavantametadavocat | [SDhPS, 14 100.1]
kathamidānīṃ bhagavaṃstathāgatena kumārabhūtena kapilavastunaḥ śākyanagarān niṣkasya gayānagarānnātidūre bodhimaṇḍavarāgragatena anuttarā samyaksaṃbodhirabhisaṃbuddhā | [SDhPS, 14 100.2]
tasyādya bhagavan kālasya sātiriṃkāṇi catvāriṃśadvarṣāṇi | [SDhPS, 14 100.3]
tatkathaṃ bhagavaṃstathāgatena iyatā kālāntareṇedamaparimitaṃ tathāgatakṛtyaṃ kṛtaṃ tathāgatena tathāgatavṛṣabhitā tathāgataparākramaḥ kṛto yo 'yaṃ bodhisattvagaṇo bodhisattvarāśiriyatā bhagavan kālāntareṇa anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau samādāpitaḥ paripācitaśca | [SDhPS, 14 101.1]
asya bhagavan bodhisattvagaṇasya bodhisattvarāśergaṇyamānasya kalpakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrair apy anto nopalabhyate | [SDhPS, 14 101.2]
evamaprameyā bhagavan ime bodhisattvā mahāsattvā evam asaṃkhyeyāś ciracaritabrahmacaryā bahubuddhaśatasahasrāvaropitakuśalamūlā bahukalpaśatasahasrapariniṣpannāḥ | [SDhPS, 14 102.1]
tadyathāpi nāma bhagavan kaścideva puruṣo navo daharaḥ śiśuḥ kṛṣṇakeśaḥ prathamena vayasā samanvāgataḥ pañcaviṃśativarṣo jātyā bhavet | [SDhPS, 14 103.1]
sa varṣaśatikān putrānādarśayed evaṃ ca vadet | [SDhPS, 14 104.1]
ete kulaputrā mama putrā iti | [SDhPS, 14 104.2]
te ca varṣaśatikāḥ puruṣā evaṃ ca vadeyuḥ | [SDhPS, 14 105.1]
eṣo 'smākaṃ pitā janaka iti | [SDhPS, 14 105.2]
tasya ca puruṣasya bhagavaṃstadvacanamaśraddheyaṃ bhavellokasya duḥśraddheyam | [SDhPS, 14 106.1]
evameva bhagavānacirābhisaṃbuddho 'nuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhim ime ca bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bahvaprameyā bahukalpakoṭīnayutaśatasahasracīrṇacaritabrahmacaryā dīrgharātraṃ hi kṛtaniścayā buddhajñāne samādhimukhaśatasahasrasamāpadyanavyutthānakuśalāḥ mahābhijñāparikarmaniryātāḥ mahābhijñākṛtaparikarmāṇaḥ paṇḍitā buddhabhūmau saṃgītakuśalāstathāgatadharmāṇām āścaryādbhutā lokasya mahāvīryabalasthāmaprāptāḥ | [SDhPS, 14 107.1]
tāṃśca bhagavānevaṃ vadati | [SDhPS, 14 107.2]
mayaite ādita eva samādāpitāḥ samuttejitāḥ paripācitāḥ pariṇāmitāśca asyāṃ bodhisattvabhūmāviti | [SDhPS, 14 107.3]
anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddhena mayaiṣa sarvavīryaparākramaḥ kṛta iti | [SDhPS, 14 108.1]
kiṃcāpi vayaṃ bhagavaṃstathāgatasya vacanaṃ śraddhayāgamiṣyāmaḥ | [SDhPS, 14 109.1]
ananyathāvādī tathāgata iti | [SDhPS, 14 109.2]
tathāgata evaitamarthaṃ jānīyāt | [SDhPS, 14 110.1]
navayānasamprasthitāḥ khalu punarbhagavan bodhisattvā mahāsattvā vicikitsāmāpadyante | [SDhPS, 14 111.1]
atra sthāne parinirvṛte tathāgate imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śrutvā na pattīyiṣyanti na śraddhāsyanti nādhimokṣyanti | [SDhPS, 14 112.1]
tataste bhagavan dharmavyasanasaṃvartanīyena karmābhisaṃskāreṇa samanvāgatā bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 14 113.1]
tatsādhu bhagavan etamevārthaṃ deśaya yadvayaṃ niḥsaṃśayā asmin dharme bhavemānāgate 'dhvani bodhisattvayānīyāḥ kulaputrā vā kuladuhitaro vā śrutvā na vicikitsām āpadyeranniti | [SDhPS, 14 114.1]
atha khalu maitreyo bodhisattvo mahāsattvastasyāṃ velāyāṃ bhagavantam ābhir gāthābhir adhyabhāṣata | [SDhPS, 14 115.1]
{SDhPS, 15}
atha khalu bhagavān sarvāvantaṃ bodhisattvagaṇamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 15 1.1]
avakalpayadhvaṃ me kulaputrā abhiśraddadhadhvaṃ tathāgatasya bhūtāṃ vācaṃ vyāharataḥ | [SDhPS, 15 1.2]
dvitīyakamapi bhagavāṃstān bodhisattvānāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 15 2.1]
avakalpayadhvaṃ me kulaputrā abhiśraddadhadhvaṃ tathāgatasya bhūtāṃ vācaṃ vyāharataḥ | [SDhPS, 15 2.2]
tṛtīyakamapi bhagavāṃstān bodhisattvānāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 15 3.1]
avakalpayadhvaṃ me kulaputrā abhiśraddadhadhvaṃ tathāgatasya bhūtāṃ vācaṃ vyāharataḥ | [SDhPS, 15 3.2]
atha khalu sa sarvāvān bodhisattvagaṇo maitreyaṃ bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvamagrataḥ sthāpayitvā añjaliṃ pragṛhya bhagavantametadavocat | [SDhPS, 15 4.1]
bhāṣatu bhagavānetamevārthaṃ bhāṣatu sugataḥ | [SDhPS, 15 4.2]
vayaṃ tathāgatasya bhāṣitamabhiśraddhāsyāmaḥ | [SDhPS, 15 5.1]
dvitīyakamapi sa sarvāvān bodhisattvagaṇo bhagavantametadavocat | [SDhPS, 15 6.1]
bhāṣatu bhagavānetamevārthaṃ bhāṣatu sugataḥ | [SDhPS, 15 6.2]
vayaṃ tathāgatasya bhāṣitamabhiśraddhāsyāmaḥ | [SDhPS, 15 7.1]
tṛtīyakamapi sa sarvāvān bodhisattvagaṇo bhagavantametadavocat | [SDhPS, 15 8.1]
bhāṣatu bhagavānetamevārthaṃ bhāṣatu sugataḥ | [SDhPS, 15 8.2]
vayaṃ tathāgatasya bhāṣitamabhiśraddhāsyāma iti | [SDhPS, 15 9.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃsteṣāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ yāvattṛtīyakamapyadhyeṣaṇāṃ viditvā tān bodhisattvānāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 15 10.1]
tena hi kulaputrāḥ śṛṇudhvamidamevaṃrūpaṃ mamādhiṣṭhānabalādhānaṃ yadayaṃ kulaputrāḥ sadevamānuṣāsuro loka evaṃ saṃjānīte | [SDhPS, 15 10.2]
sāṃprataṃ bhagavatā śākyamuninā tathāgatena śākyakulādabhiniṣkramya gayāhvaye mahānagare bodhimaṇḍavarāgragatena anuttarā samyaksaṃbodhirabhisaṃbuddheti | [SDhPS, 15 10.3]
naivaṃ draṣṭavyam | [SDhPS, 15 11.1]
api tu khalu punaḥ kulaputrāḥ bahūni mama kalpakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇy anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddhasya | [SDhPS, 15 12.1]
tadyathāpi nāma kulaputrāḥ pañcāśatsu lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu ye pṛthivīdhātuparamāṇavo 'tha khalu kaścideva puruṣa utpadyate | [SDhPS, 15 13.1]
sa ekaṃ paramāṇurajaṃ gṛhītvā pūrvasyāṃ diśi pañcāśallokadhātvasaṃkhyeyaśatasahasrāṇyatikramya tadekaṃ paramāṇurajaḥ samupanikṣipet | [SDhPS, 15 14.1]
anena paryāyeṇa kalpakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi sa puruṣaḥ sarvāṃstāṃllokadhātūn vyapagatapṛthivīdhātūn kuryāt sarvāṇi ca tāni pṛthivīdhātuparamāṇurajāṃsi anena paryāyeṇa anena ca lakṣanikṣepeṇa pūrvasyāṃ diśyupanikṣipet | [SDhPS, 15 15.1]
tatkiṃ manyadhve kulaputrāḥ śakyaṃ te lokadhātavaḥ kenaciccintayituṃ vā gaṇayituṃ vā tulayituṃ vā upalakṣayituṃ vā | [SDhPS, 15 16.1]
evamukte maitreyo bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sa ca sarvāvān bodhisattvagaṇo bodhisattvarāśirbhagavantametadavocat | [SDhPS, 15 16.2]
asaṃkhyeyāste bhagavaṃllokadhātavo 'gaṇanīyāś cittabhūmisamatikrāntāḥ | [SDhPS, 15 16.3]
sarvaśrāvakapratyekabuddhairapi bhagavan āryeṇa jñānena na śakyaṃ cintayituṃ vā gaṇayituṃ vā tulayituṃ vā upalakṣayituṃ vā | [SDhPS, 15 17.1]
asmākamapi tāvad bhagavan avaivartyabhūmisthitānāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām asmin sthāne cittagocaro na pravartate | [SDhPS, 15 18.1]
tāvadaprameyā bhagavaṃste lokadhātavo bhaveyuriti | [SDhPS, 15 19.1]
evamukte bhagavāṃstān bodhisattvān mahāsattvānetadavocat | [SDhPS, 15 20.1]
ārocayāmi vaḥ kulaputrāḥ prativedayāmi vaḥ | [SDhPS, 15 20.2]
yāvantaḥ kulaputrāste lokadhātavo yeṣu tena puruṣeṇa tāni paramāṇurajāṃsyupanikṣiptāni yeṣu ca nopanikṣiptāni sarveṣu teṣu kulaputra lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu na tāvanti paramāṇurajāṃsi saṃvidyante yāvanti mama kalpakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇyanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhim abhisaṃbuddhasya | [SDhPS, 15 21.1]
yataḥprabhṛtyahaṃ kulaputrā asyāṃ sahāyāṃ lokadhātau sattvānāṃ dharmaṃ deśayāmy anyeṣu ca lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu ye ca mayā kulaputrā atrāntarā tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ parikīrtitā dīpaṃkaratathāgataprabhṛtayas teṣāṃ ca tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāṃ parinirvāṇāni mayaiva tāni kulaputrā upāyakauśalyadharmadeśanābhinirhāranirmitāni | [SDhPS, 15 22.1]
api tu khalu punaḥ kulaputrās tathāgata āgatāgatānāṃ sattvānām indriyavīryavaimātratāṃ vyavalokya tasmiṃstasminnātmano nāma vyāharati | [SDhPS, 15 23.1]
tasmiṃstasmiṃścātmanaḥ parinirvāṇaṃ vyāharati tathā tathā ca sattvān paritoṣayati nānāvidhairdharmaparyāyaiḥ | [SDhPS, 15 24.1]
tatra kulaputrāstathāgato nānādhimuktānāṃ sattvānāmalpakuśalamūlānāṃ bahūpakleśānāmevaṃ vadati | [SDhPS, 15 25.1]
daharo 'hamasmi bhikṣavo jātyābhiniṣkrāntaḥ | [SDhPS, 15 25.2]
acirābhisaṃbuddho 'smi bhikṣavo 'nuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhim | [SDhPS, 15 26.1]
yatkhalu punaḥ kulaputrās tathāgata evaṃ cirābhisaṃbuddha evaṃ vyāharati | [SDhPS, 15 27.1]
acirābhisaṃbuddho 'hamasmīti nānyatra sattvānāṃ paripācanārtham | [SDhPS, 15 27.2]
avatāraṇārthamete dharmaparyāyā bhāṣitāḥ | [SDhPS, 15 28.1]
sarve ca te kulaputrā dharmaparyāyāstathāgatena sattvānāṃ vinayārthāya bhāṣitāḥ | [SDhPS, 15 29.1]
yāṃ ca kulaputrāstathāgataḥ sattvānāṃ vinayārthavācaṃ bhāṣate ātmopadarśanena vā paropadarśanena vātmārambaṇena vā parārambaṇena vā yatkiṃcittathāgato vyāharati sarve te dharmaparyāyāḥ satyāstathāgatena bhāṣitāḥ | [SDhPS, 15 29.2]
nāstyatra tathāgatasya mṛṣāvādaḥ | [SDhPS, 15 30.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 15 31.1]
dṛṣṭaṃ hi tathāgatena traidhātukaṃ yathābhūtam | [SDhPS, 15 31.2]
na jāyate na mriyate na cyavate nopapadyate na saṃsarati na parinirvāti na bhūtaṃ nābhūtaṃ na santaṃ nāsantaṃ na tathā nānyathā na vitathā nāvitathā | [SDhPS, 15 32.1]
na tathā traidhātukaṃ tathāgatena dṛṣṭaṃ yathā bālapṛthagjanāḥ paśyanti | [SDhPS, 15 33.1]
pratyakṣadharmā tathāgataḥ khalvasmin sthāne 'saṃpramoṣadharmā | [SDhPS, 15 34.1]
tatra tathāgato yāṃ kāṃcidvācaṃ vyāharati sarvaṃ tatsatyaṃ na mṛṣā nānyathā | [SDhPS, 15 35.1]
api tu khalu punaḥ sattvānāṃ nānācaritānāṃ nānābhiprāyāṇāṃ saṃjñāvikalpacaritānāṃ kuśalamūlasaṃjananārthaṃ vividhān dharmaparyāyān vividhairārambaṇairvyāharati | [SDhPS, 15 36.1]
yaddhi kulaputrāstathāgatena kartavyaṃ tat tathāgataḥ karoti | [SDhPS, 15 37.1]
tāvaccirābhisaṃbuddho 'parimitāyuṣpramāṇastathāgataḥ sadā sthitaḥ | [SDhPS, 15 38.1]
aparinirvṛtas tathāgataḥ parinirvāṇam ādarśayati vaineyavaśena | [SDhPS, 15 39.1]
na ca tāvanme kulaputrā adyāpi paurvikī bodhisattvacaryā pariniṣpāditā | [SDhPS, 15 40.1]
āyuṣpramāṇam apy aparipūrṇam | [SDhPS, 15 41.1]
api tu khalu punaḥ kulaputrā adyāpi taddviguṇena me kalpakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi bhaviṣyanti āyuṣpramāṇasyāparipūrṇatvāt | [SDhPS, 15 42.1]
idānīṃ khalu punarahaṃ kulaputrā aparinirvāyamāṇa eva parinirvāṇamārocayāmi | [SDhPS, 15 43.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 15 44.1]
sattvānahaṃ kulaputrā anena paryāyeṇa paripācayāmi | [SDhPS, 15 44.2]
mā haiva me 'ticiraṃ tiṣṭhato 'bhīkṣṇadarśanena akṛtakuśalamūlāḥ sattvāḥ puṇyavirahitā daridrabhūtāḥ kāmalolupā andhā dṛṣṭijālasaṃchannās tiṣṭhati tathāgata iti viditvā kilīkṛtasaṃjñā bhaveyur na ca tathāgate durlabhasaṃjñām utpādayeyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 44.3]
āsannā vayaṃ tathāgatasyeti | [SDhPS, 15 44.4]
vīryaṃ nārabheyustraidhātukānniḥsaraṇārthaṃ na ca tathāgate durlabhasaṃjñām utpādayeyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 45.1]
tataḥ kulaputrāḥ tathāgataḥ upāyakauśalyena teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ durlabhaprādurbhāvo bhikṣavastathāgata iti vācaṃ vyāharati sma | [SDhPS, 15 46.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 15 47.1]
tathā hi teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ bahubhiḥ kalpakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrairapi tathāgatadarśanaṃ bhavati vā na vā | [SDhPS, 15 47.2]
tataḥ khalvahaṃ kulaputrāstadārambaṇaṃ kṛtvaivaṃ vadāmi | [SDhPS, 15 48.1]
durlabhaprādurbhāvā hi bhikṣavastathāgatā iti | [SDhPS, 15 48.2]
te bhūyasyā mātrayā durlabhaprādurbhāvāṃstathāgatān viditvā āścaryasaṃjñāmutpādayiṣyanti śokasaṃjñāmutpādayiṣyanti | [SDhPS, 15 49.1]
apaśyantaśca tathāgatānarhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhān tṛṣitā bhaviṣyanti tathāgatadarśanāya | [SDhPS, 15 50.1]
teṣāṃ tāni tathāgatārambaṇamanaskārakuśalamūlāni dīrgharātramarthāya hitāya sukhāya ca bhaviṣyanti | [SDhPS, 15 51.1]
etamarthaṃ viditvā tathāgato 'parinirvāyanneva parinirvāṇam ārocayati sattvānāṃ vaineyavaśam upādāya | [SDhPS, 15 52.1]
tathāgatasyaiṣa kulaputrā dharmaparyāyo yadevaṃ vyāharati | [SDhPS, 15 53.1]
nāstyatra tathāgatasya mṛṣāvādaḥ | [SDhPS, 15 54.1]
tadyathāpi nāma kulaputrāḥ kaścideva vaidyapuruṣo bhavet paṇḍito vyakto medhāvī sukuśalaḥ sarvavyādhipraśamanāya | [SDhPS, 15 55.1]
tasya ca puruṣasya bahavaḥ putrā bhaveyurdaśa vā viṃśatirvā triṃśadvā catvāriṃśadvā pañcāśadvā śataṃ vā | [SDhPS, 15 56.1]
sa ca vaidyaḥ pravāsagato bhavet te cāsya sarve putrā garapīḍā vā viṣapīḍā vā bhaveyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 57.1]
tena gareṇa vā viṣeṇa vā duḥkhābhir vedanābhirabhitūrṇā bhaveyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 58.1]
te tena gareṇa vā viṣeṇa vā dahyamānāḥ pṛthivyāṃ prapateyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 59.1]
atha sa teṣāṃ vaidyaḥ pitā pravāsādāgacchet | [SDhPS, 15 60.1]
te cāsya putrāstena gareṇa vā viṣeṇa vā duḥkhābhirvedanābhirārtāḥ | [SDhPS, 15 61.1]
kecidviparītasaṃjñino bhaveyuḥ kecidaviparītasaṃjñino bhaveyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 62.1]
sarve ca te tenaiva duḥkhenārtāstaṃ pitaraṃ dṛṣṭvābhinandeyur evaṃ cainaṃ vadeyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 63.1]
diṣṭyāsi tāta kṣemasvastibhyāmāgataḥ | [SDhPS, 15 63.2]
tadasmākam asmād ātmoparodhād garādvā viṣādvā parimocayasva | [SDhPS, 15 64.1]
dadasva nastāta jīvitamiti | [SDhPS, 15 65.1]
atha khalu sa vaidyastān putrān duḥkhārtān dṛṣṭvā vedanābhibhūtān dahyataḥ pṛthivyāṃ pariveṣṭamānāṃs tato mahābhaiṣajyaṃ samudānayitvā varṇasampannaṃ gandhasampannaṃ rasasampannaṃ ca śilāyāṃ piṣṭvā teṣāṃ putrāṇāṃ pānāya dadyād evaṃ cainān vadet | [SDhPS, 15 66.1]
pibatha putrā idaṃ mahābhaiṣajyaṃ varṇasampannaṃ gandhasampannaṃ rasasampannam | [SDhPS, 15 66.2]
idaṃ yūyaṃ putrā mahābhaiṣajyaṃ pītvā kṣipramevāsmād garādvā viṣādvā parimokṣyadhve svasthā bhaviṣyatha arogāśca | [SDhPS, 15 67.1]
tatra ye tasya vaidyasya putrā aviparītasaṃjñinas te bhaiṣajyasya varṇaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā gandhaṃ cāghrāya rasaṃ cāsvādya kṣipramevābhyavahareyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 68.1]
te cābhyavaharantas tasmād ābādhāt sarveṇa sarvaṃ vimuktā bhaveyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 69.1]
ye punastasya putrā viparītasaṃjñinas te taṃ pitaramabhinandeyur enaṃ caivaṃ vadeyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 70.1]
diṣṭyāsi tāta kṣemasvastibhyāmāgato yastvamasmākaṃ cikitsaka iti | [SDhPS, 15 70.2]
te caivaṃ vācaṃ bhāṣeran tacca bhaiṣajyamupanāmitaṃ na pibeyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 71.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ | [SDhPS, 15 72.1]
tathā hi teṣāṃ tayā viparītasaṃjñayā tad bhaiṣajyamupanāmitaṃ varṇenāpi na rocate gandhenāpi rasenāpi na rocate | [SDhPS, 15 72.2]
atha khalu sa vaidyapuruṣa evaṃ cintayet | [SDhPS, 15 73.1]
ime mama putrā anena gareṇa vā viṣeṇa vā viparītasaṃjñinaḥ | [SDhPS, 15 73.2]
te khalvidaṃ mahābhaiṣajyaṃ na pibanti māṃ cābhinandanti | [SDhPS, 15 74.1]
yannvahamimān putrānupāyakauśalyena idaṃ bhaiṣajyaṃ pāyayeyamiti | [SDhPS, 15 75.1]
atha khalu sa vaidyastān putrānupāyakauśalyena tadbhaiṣajyaṃ pāyayitukāma evaṃ vadet | [SDhPS, 15 76.1]
jīrṇo 'hamasmi kulaputrā vṛddho mahallakaḥ | [SDhPS, 15 76.2]
kālakriyā ca me pratyupasthitā | [SDhPS, 15 77.1]
mā ca yūyaṃ putrāḥ śociṣṭa mā ca klamam āpadhvam | [SDhPS, 15 78.1]
idaṃ vo mayā mahābhaiṣajyamupanītam | [SDhPS, 15 79.1]
sacedākāṅkṣadhve tadeva bhaiṣajyaṃ pibadhvam | [SDhPS, 15 80.1]
sa evaṃ tān putrānupāyakauśalyena anuśiṣya anyataraṃ janapadapradeśaṃ prakrāntaḥ | [SDhPS, 15 81.1]
tatra gatvā kālagatamātmānaṃ yeṣāṃ glānānāṃ putrāṇāmārocayet te tasmin samaye 'tīva śocayeyur atīva parideveyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 82.1]
yo hyasmākaṃ pitā nātho janako 'nukampakaḥ so 'pi nāmaikaḥ kālagatas te 'dya vayamanāthāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ | [SDhPS, 15 82.2]
te khalvanāthabhūtamātmānaṃ samanupaśyanto 'śaraṇamātmānaṃ samanupaśyanto 'bhīkṣṇaṃ śokārtā bhaveyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 83.1]
teṣāṃ ca tayābhīkṣṇaṃ śokārtatayā sā viparītasaṃjñā aviparītasaṃjñā bhavet | [SDhPS, 15 84.1]
yacca tad bhaiṣajyaṃ varṇagandharasopetaṃ tad varṇagandharasopetam eva saṃjānīyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 85.1]
tatastasmin samaye tadbhaiṣajyamabhyavahareyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 86.1]
te cābhyavaharantastasmādābādhāt parimuktā bhaveyuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 87.1]
atha khalu sa vaidyastān putrānābādhavimuktān viditvā punar evātmānamupadarśayet | [SDhPS, 15 88.1]
tatkiṃ manyadhve kulaputrā mā haiva tasya vaidyasya tad upāyakauśalyaṃ kurvataḥ kaścinmṛṣāvādena saṃcodayet | [SDhPS, 15 89.1]
āhuḥ | [SDhPS, 15 89.2]
no hīdaṃ bhagavan no hīdaṃ sugata | [SDhPS, 15 89.3]
āha | [SDhPS, 15 90.1]
evameva kulaputrāḥ aham apy aprameyāsaṃkhyeyakalpakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrābhisaṃbuddha imāmanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhim api tu khalu punaḥ kulaputrāḥ aham antarāntaramevaṃrūpāṇyupāyakauśalyāni sattvānāmupadarśayāmi vinayārtham | [SDhPS, 15 90.2]
na ca me kaścidatra sthāne mṛṣāvādo bhavati | [SDhPS, 15 91.1]
atha khalu bhagavānimāmeva arthagatiṃ bhūyasyā mātrayā saṃdarśayamānastasyāṃ velāyāmimāṃ gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 15 92.1]
{SDhPS, 16}
asmin khalu punastathāgatāyuṣpramāṇanirdeśe nirdiśyamāne aprameyāṇāmasaṃkhyeyānāṃ sattvānāmarthaḥ kṛto 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 16 1.1]
atha khalu bhagavān maitreyaṃ bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 16 2.1]
asmin khalu punarajita tathāgatāyuṣpramāṇanirdeśadharmaparyāye nirdiśyamāne aṣṭaṣaṣṭigaṅgānadīvālukāsamānāṃ bodhisattvakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇām anutpattikadharmakṣāntirutpannā | [SDhPS, 16 2.2]
ebhyaḥ sahasraguṇena yeṣāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāṃ dhāraṇīpratilambho 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 16 3.1]
anyeṣāṃ ca sāhasrikalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamānāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāmimaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śrutvā asaṅgapratibhānatāpratilambho 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 16 4.1]
anyeṣāṃ ca dvisāhasrikalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamānāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāṃ koṭīnayutaśatasahasraparivartāyā dhāraṇyāḥ pratilambho 'bhūt | [SDhPS, 16 5.1]
anye ca trisāhasrikalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamā bodhisattvā mahāsattvā imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śrutvā avaivartyadharmacakraṃ pravartayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 16 6.1]
anye ca madhyamakalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamā bodhisattvā mahāsattvā imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śrutvā vimalanirbhāsacakraṃ pravartayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 16 7.1]
anye ca kṣudrakalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamā bodhisattvā mahāsattvā imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śrutvā aṣṭajātipratibaddhā abhūvan anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 16 8.1]
anye ca catuścāturdvīpikā lokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamā bodhisattvā mahāsattvā imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śrutvā caturjātipratibaddhā abhūvan anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 16 9.1]
anye ca tricāturdvīpikā lokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamā bodhisattvā mahāsattvā imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śrutvā trijātipratibaddhā abhūvan anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 16 10.1]
anye ca dvicāturdvīpikā lokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamā bodhisattvā mahāsattvā imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śrutvā dvijātipratibaddhā abhūvannanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 16 11.1]
anye caikacāturdvīpikā lokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamā bodhisattvā mahāsattvā imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śrutvā ekajātipratibaddhā abhūvannanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [SDhPS, 16 12.1]
aṣṭatrisāhasramahāsāhasralokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamaiśca bodhisattvair mahāsattvairimaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śrutvā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau cittāny utpāditāni | [SDhPS, 16 13.1]
atha samanantaranirdiṣṭe bhagavataiṣāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāṃ dharmābhisamaye pratiṣṭhāne 'tha tāvad evoparivaihāyasād antarīkṣān māndāravamahāmāndāravāṇāṃ puṣpāṇāṃ puṣpavarṣamabhipravṛṣṭam | [SDhPS, 16 14.1]
teṣu ca lokadhātukoṭīnayutaśatasahasreṣu yāni tāni buddhakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇyāgatya ratnavṛkṣamūleṣu siṃhāsanopaviṣṭāni tāni sarvāṇi cāvakiranti smābhyavakiranti smābhiprakiranti sma | [SDhPS, 16 15.1]
bhagavantaṃ ca śākyamuniṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ taṃ ca bhagavantaṃ prabhūtaratnaṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ parinirvṛtaṃ siṃhāsanopaviṣṭam avakiranti smābhyavakiranti smābhiprakiranti sma | [SDhPS, 16 16.1]
taṃ ca sarvāvantaṃ bodhisattvagaṇaṃ tāścatasraḥ parṣado 'vakiranti smābhyavakiranti smābhiprakiranti sma | [SDhPS, 16 17.1]
divyāni ca candanāgarucūrṇānyantarīkṣāt pravarṣanti sma | [SDhPS, 16 18.1]
upariṣṭāccāntarīkṣe vaihāyasaṃ mahādundubhayo 'ghaṭṭitāḥ praṇedur manojñamadhuragambhīranirghoṣāḥ | [SDhPS, 16 19.1]
divyāni ca dūṣyayugmaśatasahasrāṇy upariṣṭād antarīkṣāt prapatanti sma | [SDhPS, 16 20.1]
hārārdhahāramuktāhāramaṇiratnamahāratnāni copariṣṭād vaihāyasamantarīkṣe samantāt sarvāsu dikṣu pralambanti sma | [SDhPS, 16 21.1]
samantācca anarghaprāptasya dhūpasya ghaṭikāsahasrāṇi ratnamayāni svayameva pravicaranti sma | [SDhPS, 16 22.1]
ekaikasya ca tathāgatasya ratnamayīṃ chatrāvalīṃ yāvad brahmalokādupari vaihāyasam antarīkṣe bodhisattvā mahāsattvā dhārayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 16 23.1]
anena paryāyeṇa sarveṣāṃ teṣām aprameyāṇām asaṃkhyeyānāṃ buddhakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇāṃ te bodhisattvā mahāsattvā ratnamayīṃ chatrāvalīṃ yāvad brahmalokād upari vaihāyasamantarīkṣe dhārayāmāsuḥ | [SDhPS, 16 24.1]
pṛthak pṛthag gāthābhinirhārair bhūtairbuddhastavais tāṃstathāgatān abhiṣṭuvanti sma | [SDhPS, 16 25.1]
atha khalu maitreyo bodhisattvo mahāsattvastasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 16 26.1]
atha khalu bhagavān maitreyaṃ bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvamāmantrayate sma | [SDhPS, 16 43.1]
yair ajita asmiṃstathāgatāyuṣpramāṇanirdeśadharmaparyāye nirdiśyamāne sattvair ekacittotpādikāpyadhimuktir utpāditābhiśraddadhānatā vā kṛtā kiyatte kulaputrā vā kuladuhitaro vā puṇyaṃ prasavantīti tacchṛṇu sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuru | [SDhPS, 16 43.2]
bhāṣiṣye 'haṃ yāvat puṇyaṃ prasavantīti | [SDhPS, 16 44.1]
tadyathāpi nāma ajita kaścideva kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhikāṅkṣamāṇaḥ pañcasu pāramitāsvaṣṭau kalpakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi caret | [SDhPS, 16 45.1]
tadyathā dānapāramitāyāṃ śīlapāramitāyāṃ kṣāntipāramitāyāṃ vīryapāramitāyāṃ dhyānapāramitāyāṃ virahitaḥ prajñāpāramitayā yena ca ajita kulaputreṇa vā kuladuhitrā vā imaṃ tathāgatāyuṣpramāṇanirdeśaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śrutvā ekacittotpādikāpyadhimuktirutpāditā abhiśraddadhānatā vā kṛtāsya puṇyābhisaṃskārasya kuśalābhisaṃskārasya asau paurvakaḥ puṇyābhisaṃskāraḥ kuśalābhisaṃskāraḥ pañcapāramitāpratisaṃyukto 'ṣṭakalpakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrapariniṣpannaḥ śatatamīmapi kalāṃ nopayāti sahasratamīmapi śatasahasratamīmapi koṭīśatasahasratamīmapi koṭīnayutasahasratamīmapi koṭīnayutaśatasahasratamīmapi kalāṃ nopayāti saṃkhyāmapi kalāmapi gaṇanāmapi upamāmapi upanisāmapi na kṣamate | [SDhPS, 16 46.1]
evaṃrūpeṇa ajita puṇyābhisaṃskāreṇa samanvāgataḥ kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā vivartate 'nuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodheriti naitat sthānaṃ vidyate | [SDhPS, 16 47.1]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata | [SDhPS, 16 48.1]
punaraparamajita ya imaṃ tathāgatāyuṣpramāṇanirdeśaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śrutvā avataredadhimucyeta avagāheta avabudhyeta so 'smād aprameyataraṃ puṇyābhisaṃskāraṃ prasaved buddhajñānasaṃvartanīyam | [SDhPS, 16 69.1]
kaḥ punarvādo ya imamevaṃrūpaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śṛṇuyācchrāvayeta vācayed dhārayedvā likhedvā likhāpayedvā pustakagataṃ vā satkuryād gurukuryānmānayet pūjayet satkārayed vā puṣpadhūpagandhamālyavilepanacūrṇacīvaracchatradhvajapatākābhis tailapradīpair vā ghṛtapradīpairvā gandhatailapradīpair vā bahutaraṃ puṇyābhisaṃskāraṃ prasaved buddhajñānasaṃvartanīyam | [SDhPS, 16 70.1]
yadā ca ajita sa kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā imaṃ tathāgatāyuṣpramāṇanirdeśaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śrutvā adhyāśayenādhimucyate tadā tasyedamadhyāśayalakṣaṇaṃ veditavyam | [SDhPS, 16 71.1]
